     INTE    ORGNUM       = 16                         ;; # of ORG
     INTE    MCNUM        = 4                          ;; # of Chips
     INTE    CHIPCNT      = 4                          ;; # of Channels
     INTE    NTESTCH      = 4                          ;; # of Concurrent Test Channels
     INTE    TSTFLG       = 1                          ;; # of Test Routine
     INTE    ORDFLG       = 2                          ;; # of Test Routine                ???
;    INTE    MR7FLG       = 0                          ;; # of AT2 pattern
     INTE    RUPFLG       = 1                          ;; # of CHA. RUP
     INTE    CUMFLG       = 2                          ;; # of CUSTOMER DEFAULT 0
     INTE    MERFLG       = 0                          ;; CS/CKE MERGE FLG , 0:Split 1: 2CS Merge 2: 2CK Merge
     INTE    ODQFLG       = 0                          ;; # of Out DQ 0:16 1:8
     INTE    TMPFLG       = 0                          ;; TDC CONTROL 0: 0'C(HFC),70'C(HFH)  1: 10'C(HFC),70'C(HFH)
     INTE    STEPFLG      = 0                          ;; 0:Normal   1:T090 1step
     INTE    VGAPFLG      = 0                          ;; 0:Normal   1:VDD2=1.26V, VDDQ=1.20
     INTE    LINFLG       = 0                          ;; 0:15LINE   1:13LINE
     INTE    ODTFLG       = 1                          ;; 0:ODT pin x  1: ODT pin using         
     INTE    MSKFLG       = 1                          ;; 1:"A" 2:"B"
     EQUATE  VPARA        ="4"                         ;; # of DUT
     INTE    NTESTDQ      = 64                         ;; # of Test DQ
     STRING  CHSELTYPE(1) ="A"                         ;;
     STRING  CHANNELSEL(1)="0"                         ;; 0:ALL A: A CANNEL B: B C: C D: D
     REAL    FREQMARGIN   = 0.03                       ;; 3% G/B

%ENDC

T7500IOTC:
 ; ARGUMENT(TCKREF,VD2REF,SHM_TYPE,XSTART,XEND,XSTEP,YSTART,YEND,YSTEP,SHMLEVEL,SHMFORMAT,SHMMODE,SHMPATT,SHMIOF,SHMTSAC)
   READ CDUT TO IOTCDUT
   IF IOTCDUT=#0 THEN GOTO CONT

   ALLPIN=OPEN
   RL=0 
   WL=0 
   TSPEED=7500 &  WCKCKRATIO=4 & BA0ADDR="X16" & L_DELAY="N"
   MR11_CAODT=#4 & MR11_DQODT=#4 & MR11_NTODTEN=#0 & MR17_SOCODT=#5 & MR18_WCKODT=#6 & MR41_NTODT=#0
   MR1_WL=#C & MR2_RL=#C & MR2_NWR=#C
   WLSET="A"
   GOSUB WLRLCAL(WCKCKRATIO,MR1_WL,MR2_RL,DVFSC,WLSET,L_DELAY) ;ARGUMENT(I_CKR,I_WL,I_RL,I_DVFSC,I_WLSET,I_DELAY) 

   SROF
   SRON   

   SET WET

   RESET BCLK CCLK STRB DELAYADJUST ; for T5511

   SET ILMODE 16WAY

   LP5TCK=312.5PS*(1-FREQMARGIN)  ;; 6.4Gbps
   TCK=LP5TCK

   WLVLSTART = -0.0000000005       & RDTRSTART = -0.0000000010  & WRTRSTART = -0.0000000010
   WLVLEND   =  0.0000000020       & RDTREND   =  0.0000000020  & WRTREND   =  0.0000000020
   WLVLSHIFT =  0.00000000005      & RDTRSHIFT =  0.00000000001 & WRTRSHIFT =  0.00000000001


   SIWC=300MV &  SIWD=300MV
   TOUTH=0V   & TOUTL=0V
   
GOTO WRIOTC

 ; ARGUMENT(TCKREF,VD2REF,SHM_TYPE,XSTART,XEND,XSTEP,YSTART,YEND,YSTEP,SHMLEVEL,SHMFORMAT,SHMMODE,SHMPATT,SHMIOF,SHMTSAC)

T75M26B:
;  GOSUB FUNA(4905,6,4,4,183,LP5VD2,LP5TCK,"VND01","FMD01","PNNF2","PDCS4FM267N5B",#0000,0.0NS,  1.0S," DCM CHECK                             ")  ;

   GOSUB FUNA(4996,0,5,5,185,LP5VD2,LP5TCK,"VND01","FMD01","PNNF2","PDCS4FM267N5P",#0000,0.0NS,  1.0S," Column Bar test            BL32       ")  ;
   GOSUB DCMA_CHECK
   TSTITEM(1,6)="DCM_F0" & GOSUB CODEREAD(0,151,4905,4.5MA,100MA) ; 7/6 - -6/-7 (F0) 
   TSTITEM(1,6)="DCM_F1" & GOSUB CODEREAD(0,151,4906,4.5MA,100MA) ; 7/6 - -6/-7 (F1) 

   TSTITEM(1,6)="DCM_G0" & GOSUB CODEREAD(0,151,795,1.5MA,100MA)  ; 4 - (-4) (F0/F1 MIN)
   TSTITEM(1,6)="DCM_G1" & GOSUB CODEREAD(0,151,796,0.5MA,100MA) ; 4 - 0    (F0/F1 MIN)
   TSTITEM(1,6)="DCM_G2" & GOSUB CODEREAD(0,151,797,0.5MA,100MA) ; 0 - 4    (F0/F1 MIN)

 IF PRCFLG=1 THEN ENTRY 
   L_DELAY="N"                                                                   
   GOSUB WLRLCAL(WCKCKRATIO,MR1_WL,MR2_RL,DVFSC,WLSET,L_DELAY) ;ARGUMENT(I_CKR,I_WL,I_RL,I_DVFSC,I_WLSET,I_DELAY) 
   TRAININGTEST_VAR 263,Loose Function Test&Training    ,16WAY,PDCS4STRA7O5ANN,#0, ,LP5TCK, ,FMD01 , MR11VAL, CVFCA, CVFDQ
    READ CDUT TO CURDUTQ
    MR30_DCA=#44 & MR_RCAL_BL=#00  ;;     DCA -4step
    IBIS 857,OC_RC4,0,151,#00,PDCS4STQW7N5XNN,TCK,FMD01,10MS,LP5VD2*0.476*0.50,5.98MA,-5.98MA,60MA,#56,#00,#44,#06,#0C,#44
    GOSUB TQWPINSAVE
    MR30_DCA=#00 & MR_RCAL_BL=#00  ;;     DCA  0step
    IBIS 857,OC_RC0,0,151,#00,PDCS4STQW7N5XNN,TCK,FMD01,10MS,LP5VD2*0.476*0.50,5.98MA,-5.98MA,60MA,#56,#00,#44,#06,#0C,#44
    GOSUB TQWPINSAVE
    MR30_DCA=#CC & MR_RCAL_BL=#00  ;;     DCA +4step
    IBIS 857,OC_RCC,0,151,#00,PDCS4STQW7N5XNN,TCK,FMD01,10MS,LP5VD2*0.476*0.50,5.98MA,-5.98MA,60MA,#56,#00,#44,#06,#0C,#44
    GOSUB TQWPINSAVE

     
     DO LTQW75RC I=1,TP
      FDNUM=(MOD((I-1)/TPARA1)/32)*2+(I-1)/TPARA1+1
      RTNUM=I-32*((I-1)/32)-1
      IF SR(CURDUTQ,RTNUM).AND.#01<>#0  THEN ENTRY
      DO TQW75RC J=CHSEL*NTESTCH+1 (CHSEL+1)*NTESTCH 1
         WRITE /,"TQW EACH DUT:",ASCII(I,2,2,0," ")," CH:",ASCII(J,2,1,0," ")," ",ASCII(FIDP2(J,I),0,8,16,"0"),ASCII(FIDP1(J,I),0,8,16,"0")," ",
         WRITE ASCII(DCA_VALUE0(I,J,1)/1UA,2,8,1," "),ASCII(DCA_VALUE0(I,J,2)/1UA,2,8,1," "),ASCII(DCA_VALUE0(I,J,3)/1UA,2,8,1," ")," _ "
         WRITE ASCII(DCA_VALUE0(I,J,4)/1UA,2,8,1," "),ASCII(DCA_VALUE0(I,J,5)/1UA,2,8,1," "),ASCII(DCA_VALUE0(I,J,6)/1UA,2,8,1," ")
TQW75RC:
      EXIT
LTQW75RC:

   TSTITEM(1,6)="DCA_01" & FAPATN="PDCS6STQWDN1X__" & GOSUB CODEREAD(0,157,791,100.0UA,99.0MA)  ; C-0
   TSTITEM(1,6)="DCA_02" & FAPATN="PDCS6STQWDN1X__" & GOSUB CODEREAD(0,157,792,100.0UA,99.0MA)  ; 4-0
       
 EXIT

 WLSET="A"

GOTO CONT

T7500IBIS:
       ; ARGUMENT(TCKREF,VD2REF,SHM_TYPE,XSTART,XEND,XSTEP,YSTART,YEND,YSTEP,SHMLEVEL,SHMFORMAT,SHMMODE,SHMPATT,SHMIOF,SHMTSAC)


RESET WET

   ALLPIN=OPEN
   WLSET="A"
   RL=0
   WL=0
   TSPEED=7500 &  WCKCKRATIO=4 & BA0ADDR="X16" & L_DELAY="N"
   MR11_CAODT=#4 & MR11_DQODT=#4 & MR11_NTODTEN=#0 & MR17_SOCODT=#5 & MR18_WCKODT=#6 & MR41_NTODT=#0
   GOSUB WLRLCAL(WCKCKRATIO,MR1_WL,MR2_RL,DVFSC,WLSET,L_DELAY)
   SROF
   SRON
   SET WET
   RESET BCLK CCLK STRB DELAYADJUST ; for T5511
   SET ILMODE 16WAY
   LP5TCK=2000000PS/(TSPEED*(1+FREQMARGIN)) & TCK=LP5TCK
;  LP5TCK=305PS
   LP5VD2=HVDDCORNER
   LP5VD2=1.05V
   TRAININGTEST_VAR 250,Loose Function Test&Training    ,16WAY,PDCS4STRA7O5ANN,#0, ,LP5TCK, ,FMD01 , MR11VAL, CVFCA, CVFDQ

T7500:   ; 1463 2    1464  4
   ALLPIN=OPEN
   WLSET="A"
   RL=0
   WL=0
   TSPEED=7500 &  WCKCKRATIO=4 & BA0ADDR="X16" & L_DELAY="N"
   MR11_CAODT=#4 & MR11_DQODT=#4 & MR11_NTODTEN=#0 & MR17_SOCODT=#5 & MR18_WCKODT=#6 & MR41_NTODT=#0
   MR1_WL=#C & MR2_RL=#C & MR2_NWR=#C
   GOSUB WLRLCAL(WCKCKRATIO,MR1_WL,MR2_RL,DVFSC,WLSET,L_DELAY)
   SROF
   SRON
   SET WET
   RESET BCLK CCLK STRB DELAYADJUST ; for T5511
   SET ILMODE 16WAY

   LP5VD2=HVDDCORNER

T1600_R41:

   ALLPIN=OPEN
   RL=20  ;28 ; 40 ; 20
   WL=12  ;16 ; 20 ; 12

;--------- WCK:CK RATIO = 2:1 @ 16Bank Mode / DVFSC="ON" / DVFSQ="OFF"  ----------------------------------------------------------------

   TSPEED=1600 & WCKCKRATIO=4 & BA0ADDR="X16" & L_DELAY="Y"   ;; 2:1
   MR1_WL=#2 & MR2_RL=#2 & MR2_NWR=#2
   MR11_CAODT=#4 & MR11_DQODT=#4 & MR11_NTODTEN=#0 & MR17_SOCODT=#5 & MR18_WCKODT=#6 & MR41_NTODT=#0
;  GOSUB WLRLCAL(WCKCKRATIO,MR1_WL,MR2_RL,DVFSC,WLSET,L_DELAY) ;ARGUMENT(I_CKR,I_WL,I_RL,I_DVFSC,I_WLSET,I_DELAY)  
   
  
   SROF
   SRON
SET WET
   SIWC=300MV 
   SIWD=300MV
   PCA=0.20
   PDQ=0.20

   RESET BCLK CCLK STRB DELAYADJUST ; for T5511

   SET ILMODE 16WAY
   LP5VD2=LVDDCORNER
   TSPEED=1600 & WCKCKRATIO=4 & BA0ADDR="X16" & L_DELAY="N"

   LP5TCK=2000000PS/(TSPEED*(1+FREQMARGIN)) & TCK=LP5TCK
   LP5TCK=1250.0PS & TCK=LP5TCK

T3200_R21:

   ALLPIN=OPEN

   TSPEED=3200 & WCKCKRATIO=2 & BA0ADDR="X16" & L_DELAY="N"

   MR1_WL=#5 & MR2_RL=#5 & MR2_NWR=#5
   MR11_CAODT=#0 & MR11_DQODT=#0 & MR11_NTODTEN=#0 & MR17_SOCODT=#5 & MR18_WCKODT=#0 & MR41_NTODT=#0
   IF ORGNUM=8 THEN MR11_CAODT=#3
;  GOSUB WLRLCAL(WCKCKRATIO,MR1_WL,MR2_RL,DVFSC,WLSET,L_DELAY) ;ARGUMENT(I_CKR,I_WL,I_RL,I_DVFSC,I_WLSET,I_DELAY)


   SROF
   SRON
SET WET
   SIWC=300MV
   SIWD=300MV
   PCA=0.20
   PDQ=0.20

   RESET BCLK CCLK STRB DELAYADJUST ; for T5511

   LP5TCK=612.5PS & TCK=LP5TCK

T3200_R41:

   ALLPIN=OPEN
   RL=20  ;28 ; 40 ; 20
   WL=12  ;16 ; 20 ; 12

;--------- WCK:CK RATIO = 2:1 @ 16Bank Mode / DVFSC="ON" / DVFSQ="OFF"  ----------------------------------------------------------------

   TSPEED=3200 & WCKCKRATIO=2 & BA0ADDR="X16" & L_DELAY="Y"   ;; 2:1
   MR1_WL=#5 & MR2_RL=#5 & MR2_NWR=#5
   MR11_CAODT=#4 & MR11_DQODT=#4 & MR11_NTODTEN=#0 & MR17_SOCODT=#5 & MR18_WCKODT=#6 & MR41_NTODT=#0
;  GOSUB WLRLCAL(WCKCKRATIO,MR1_WL,MR2_RL,DVFSC,WLSET,L_DELAY) ;ARGUMENT(I_CKR,I_WL,I_RL,I_DVFSC,I_WLSET,I_DELAY)  
   
  
   SROF
   SRON
SET WET
   SIWC=300MV 
   SIWD=300MV
   PCA=0.20
   PDQ=0.20

   RESET BCLK CCLK STRB DELAYADJUST ; for T5511

   SET ILMODE 16WAY
   LP5VD2=HVDDCORNER
   TSPEED=3200 & WCKCKRATIO=4 & BA0ADDR="X16" & L_DELAY="N"

   LP5TCK=2000000PS/(TSPEED*(1+FREQMARGIN)) & TCK=LP5TCK
   LP5TCK=615.0PS & TCK=LP5TCK

   TRAININGTEST_VAR 231,Loose Function Test&Training    ,16WAY,PDCS6STRA3N2ANN,#0, ,LP5TCK, ,FTD01 , MR11VAL, CVFCA, CVFDQ
   GOSUB FUNA(2250,6,4,4,183,LP5VD2,LP5TCK,"VND01","FSD01","PRNN2","PDCS6FRMW3D2N",#6666,0.0NS,  1.0S," Read Modify Write          BL32            ")  ; 
   GOSUB FUNA(2251,6,4,4,183,LP5VD2,LP5TCK,"VND01","FSD01","PNNN2","PDCS6FPDN3N2A",#6666,0.0NS,  32MS," PDN ALL CASE NEW A                         ")  ;f

   LP5VD2=LVDDCORNER
;  LP5VD2=0.99V
   TSPEED=3200 & WCKCKRATIO=4 & BA0ADDR="X16" & L_DELAY="N"

   LP5TCK=2000000PS/(TSPEED*(1+FREQMARGIN)) & TCK=LP5TCK
   LP5TCK=615.0PS & TCK=LP5TCK

   TRAININGTEST_VAR 231,Loose Function Test&Training    ,16WAY,PDCS6STRA3N2ANN,#0, ,LP5TCK, ,FTD01 , MR11VAL, CVFCA, CVFDQ

T0500VROCHK:

  TEST 4996
     READ CDUT TO CURDUTQ
   DO VROCHK00 I=1,TP
      RTNUM=I-32*((I-1)/32)-1
      IF SR(CURDUTQ,RTNUM).AND.#01<>#0  THEN ENTRY
         NFDQ1(I,1)=#0
         NFDQ1(I,2)=#0
         NFDQ1(I,3)=#0
         NFDQ1(I,4)=#0
         NFDQ2(I,1)=#0
         NFDQ2(I,2)=#0
         NFDQ2(I,3)=#0
         NFDQ2(I,4)=#0
      EXIT
VROCHK00:

   MR11_DQODT=#0
   SEND MPAT PDCS6SWTR0N5BNN
;  GOSUB FUNA(4596,0,4,5,183,LP5VD2,LP5TCK,"VND01","FMD01","PRNNX","PCBH6SWTR0N5B",#0000,0.0NS, 1.00S," WR/RD FIFO CHECK                            ")  ;
   VSWII=60MV
  REG MPAT YT11=#30
  REG MPAT YT3=#56

;DO VVRREF  VSWII= 50MV 150MV 50MV
  REG MPAT YT13=#05
DO VREFCHKX VRQCHK=#0D #7E #4
   REG MPAT YT14=VRQCHK
   REG MPAT YT15=VRQCHK

   I10HF_VRO= (0.1+0.005*VRQCHK)*LP5VDQ+VSWII       
   I10LF_VRO= (0.1+0.005*VRQCHK)*LP5VDQ-VSWII       
;  WRITE /,VRQCHK," : ",(0.1+0.005*VRQCHK)*100,LP5VDQ,(0.1+0.005*VRQCHK)*LP5VDQ," ",I10HF_VRO,I10LF_VRO,VSWII
   IN9  = I10HF_VRO,I10LF_VRO
   IN10 = I10HF_VRO,I10LF_VRO
   MEAS MPAT(3)
;  READ FUNC1(DMIP) TO PFDATA0

   READ FUNC1(DATA0) TO PFDATA0 ;;CS0_0 DO=1
   READ FUNC1(DATA1) TO PFDATA1 ;;CS0_1 DO=2
   READ FUNC1(DATA2) TO PFDATA2 ;;CS1_0 DO=3
   READ FUNC1(DATA3) TO PFDATA3 ;;CS1_1 DO=4


;  WRITE " "," ",PFDATA0(2)," ",PFDATA0(4)

   DO VROCHK0 I=1,TP
      RTNUM=I-32*((I-1)/32)-1
      IF SR(CURDUTQ,RTNUM).AND.#01<>#0  THEN ENTRY
         NFDQ1(I,1)=NFDQ1(I,1).OR.PFDATA0(I)
         NFDQ1(I,2)=NFDQ1(I,2).OR.PFDATA1(I)
         NFDQ1(I,3)=NFDQ1(I,3).OR.PFDATA2(I)
         NFDQ1(I,4)=NFDQ1(I,4).OR.PFDATA3(I)
      EXIT
VROCHK0:
VREFCHKX:
;  REG MPAT CFLG=0
   REG MPAT YT13=#45
   REG MPAT YT14=#0E
   REG MPAT YT15=#0E
   MEAS MPAT(3)
   REG MPAT CFLG=CCFLG
   WAIT TIMES 10MS
;  WRITE /
DO VREFCHKX1 VRQCHK=#0E #7F #4
   REG MPAT YT14=VRQCHK
   REG MPAT YT15=VRQCHK

   I10HF_VRO= (0.1+0.005*VRQCHK)*LP5VDQ+VSWII
   I10LF_VRO= (0.1+0.005*VRQCHK)*LP5VDQ-VSWII
;  WRITE /,VRQCHK," : ",(0.1+0.005*VRQCHK)*100,LP5VDQ,(0.1+0.005*VRQCHK)*LP5VDQ," ",I10HF_VRO,I10LF_VRO,VSWII
   IN9  = I10HF_VRO,I10LF_VRO
   IN10 = I10HF_VRO,I10LF_VRO
   MEAS MPAT(3)
;  READ FUNC1(DMIP) TO PFDATA0
   READ FUNC1(DATA0) TO PFDATA0 ;;CS0_0 DO=1
   READ FUNC1(DATA1) TO PFDATA1 ;;CS0_1 DO=2
   READ FUNC1(DATA2) TO PFDATA2 ;;CS1_0 DO=3
   READ FUNC1(DATA3) TO PFDATA3 ;;CS1_1 DO=4


;  WRITE " "," ",PFDATA0(2)," ",PFDATA0(4)
   DO VROCHK1 I=1,TP
      RTNUM=I-32*((I-1)/32)-1
      IF SR(CURDUTQ,RTNUM).AND.#01<>#0  THEN ENTRY
         NFDQ2(I,1)=NFDQ2(I,1).OR.PFDATA0(I)
         NFDQ2(I,2)=NFDQ2(I,2).OR.PFDATA1(I)
         NFDQ2(I,3)=NFDQ2(I,3).OR.PFDATA2(I)
         NFDQ2(I,4)=NFDQ2(I,4).OR.PFDATA3(I)
;        NFDQ2(I)=NFDQ2(I).OR.PFDATA0(I)
      EXIT
VROCHK1:


VREFCHKX1:


VVRREF:

  ;WRITE /," ",NFDQ1(11)," ",NFDQ1(18)," ",NFDQ1(19)," ",NFDQ1(22)
  ;WRITE /," ",NFDQ2(11)," ",NFDQ2(18)," ",NFDQ2(19)," ",NFDQ2(22)


   REG MPAT YT14=VREFBYTE0
   REG MPAT YT15=VREFBYTE1

   MR11_CAODT=#3 & MR11_DQODT=#3 & MR11_NTODTEN=#0 & MR17_SOCODT=#5 & MR18_WCKODT=#0 & MR41_NTODT=#0;

   IN9  = I3HF,I3LF               ;DM
   IN10 = I3HF,I3LF               ;DM

GOTO CONT

GOTO CONT

;;              GETRDTRB((II-1)*88+(IJ-1)/2*22+17)=0.0 & GETRDTRB((II-1)*88+(IJ-1)/2*22+18)=0.0 
;;              GETRDTRD((II-1)*88+(IJ-1)/2*22+17)=0.0 & GETRDTRD((II-1)*88+(IJ-1)/2*22+18)=0.0
;;           EXIT
;;           EXIT
;; GETRDR2E:

   TRAININGTEST_VAR 240,Loose Function Test&Training    ,16WAY,PDCS4STRA5O5BNN,#0, ,LP5TCK, ,FMD01 , MR11VAL, CVFCA, CVFDQ


    TMRS_1="T0000" & TMRS_2="T0000" & TMRS_3="T0000" & TMRS_4="T0000" & TMRS_5="T0000" & TMRS_6="T0000" & TMRS_7="T0000" & TMRS_8="T0000" & TMRS_9="T0000" &  TMRS_A="T0000" 


   WCKDUTYMRS=1

    TMRS_1="T0000" & TMRS_2="T0000" & TMRS_3="T0000" & TMRS_4="T0000" & TMRS_5="T0000" & TMRS_6="T0000" & TMRS_7="T0000" & TMRS_8="T0000" & TMRS_9="T0000" &  TMRS_A="T0000" 
   GOSUB FUNA(350,0,4,4,183,LP5VD2,LP5TCK,"VND01","FTD01","PNNFX","PDCS4SCOB5N5W",#0000,0.0NS,  1.0S," Column Bar test                       ")  ;
   EXEC CCALL("TrainShowStatus_n_WRC",GETRDTRF)

   GOSUB WCKDUTYRANGE


   WCKDUTYMRS=0
;   TMRS_1="T1414" & TMRS_2="T1413" & TMRS_3="T1412" & TMRS_4="T1411" & TMRS_5="T1410" & TMRS_6="T1407" & TMRS_7="T1406" & TMRS_8="T1405" & TMRS_9="T1404" &  TMRS_A="T0000" 
   VREFBYTE0=#10 & VREFBYTE1=VREFBYTE0
   GOSUB FUNA(350,0,4,4,183,LP5VD2,LP5TCK,"VND01","FTD01","PNNFX","PDCS4SCOB5N5W",#0000,0.0NS,  1.0S," Column Bar test                       ")  ;
   EXEC CCALL("TrainShowStatus_n_WRC",GETRDTRF)

   GOSUB WCKDUTYRANGE


   VREFBYTE0=#70 & VREFBYTE1=VREFBYTE0

   GOSUB FUNA(350,0,4,4,183,LP5VD2,LP5TCK,"VND01","FTD01","PNNFX","PDCS4SCOB5N5W",#0000,0.0NS,  1.0S," Column Bar test                       ")  ;
   EXEC CCALL("TrainShowStatus_n_WRC",GETRDTRF)

;   tWCK2CK_Leveling
;   RDTR
;   WRTR
;   tQW IBIS (RDQS)
;   tQW Duty scr.
;   VRO @ VRCG ON  VREF Output scr. @ VRCG ON
;   VRO @ VRCG OFF VREF Output scr. @ VRCG OFF
;   DQ/DMI PULL_DN @ NOCAL 40    No_ZQCAL IBIS @ 40
;   DQ/DMI PULL_UP 40 
;   DQ/DMI PULL_DN 40
;   IBIS NT ODT        NT ODT scr.
;   ZQ CODE PULL_DN 
;   ZQ CODE PULL_UP
;   WCK2DQI OSC LSB CML Buffer @ 5.5G  
;   WCK2DQI OSC MSB CML Buffer @ 5.5G
;   WCK2DQI OSC LSB CMOS Buffer @ 3.2G
;   WCK2DQI OSC MSB CMOS Buffer @ 3.2G
;   WCK2DQO OSC LSB CML Buffer @ 5.5G
;   WCK2DQO OSC MSB CML Buffer @ 5.5G
;   WCK2DQO OSC LSB CMOS Buffer @ 3.2G
;   WCK2DQO OSC MSB CMOS Buffer @ 3.2G

;  %1  tn
;  %2  item name
;  %3  caregory hbin
;  %4  SORT sbin
;  %5  PC
;  %6  PATN NAME
;  %7  tck
;  %8  FORMAT
;  %9  wait time
;  %10 force
;  %11 high limit
;  %12 low limit
;  %13 Meas range
;  %14 mr3  pdds
;  %15 mr41 nt dq odt 
;  %16 mr11 ca/dq odt
;  %17 mr17 socodt
;  %18 mr18 wckterm 
;  %7  tck
;  %7  tck
;          REG MPAT YT3  = #06                ; (MR3)  RZQ/6, 4Bank/4BG, SET_A, DBI_OFF 
;          REG MPAT YT5  = #00                ; (MR41) NT DQ ODT RZQ/4, PRR Disable,                                                 
;          REG MPAT YT7  = #05                ; (MR17) SOCODT, RZQ/5, CLK_EN. CA_EN                                                  
;          REG MPAT YT8  = #06                ; (MR18) WCK Term RZQ/4, Half-rate sync, CKR 4:1                                       
;          REG MPAT YT11 = #44                ; (MR11) DQ_ODT RZQ/4, CAODT RZQ/4                                                    


GOTO CONT


WCKDUTYRANGE:

DO GETRDR1Q II=1 TP 1
    RTNUM=II-32*((II-1)/32)-1
    IF SR(CURDUT,RTNUM).AND.#01<>#0 THEN ENTRY
      DO GETRDR2Q IJ=1 NTESTCH 1
        IF ORGNUM=16 THEN ENTRY
           IF FK=#10 THEN WRITE /,"WCK",ASCII(WCKDUTYMRS,2,1,0," ")," DUT:",ASCII(II,2,1,0," ")," CH:",ASCII(IJ+NTESTCH*CHSEL,2,1,0," ")," ",ASCII(FIDP2(IJ+NTESTCH*CHSEL,II),0,8,16,"0"),ASCII(FIDP1(IJ+NTESTCH*CHSEL,II),0,8,16,"0")," DQ:"
           GETWRMIN(WCKDUTYMRS*32+(II-1)*8+CHSEL*NTESTCH+IJ)=500
           DO GETRDR3Q IK=1 16 1
              IF GETWRMIN(WCKDUTYMRS*32+(II-1)*8+CHSEL*NTESTCH+IJ)>GETRDTRF((II-1)*88+(IJ-1)*22+IK) THEN GETWRMIN(WCKDUTYMRS*32+(II-1)*8+CHSEL*NTESTCH+IJ)=GETRDTRF((II-1)*88+(IJ-1)*22+IK)
              IF FK=#10 THEN WRITE ,ASCII(GETRDTRF((II-1)*88+(IJ-1)*22+IK),2,7,2," ")
         GETRDR3Q:
              IF FK=#10 THEN WRITE " (",ASCII(GETWRMIN(WCKDUTYMRS*32+(II-1)*8+CHSEL*NTESTCH+IJ),2,7,2," ")," )"
        EXIT
        IF ORGNUM=8  THEN ENTRY
           IF FK=#10 THEN WRITE /,"WCK",ASCII(WCKDUTYMRS,2,1,0," ")," DUT:",ASCII(II,2,1,0," ")," CH:",ASCII(IJ+NTESTCH*CHSEL,2,1,0," ")," ",ASCII(FIDP2(IJ+NTESTCH*CHSEL,II),0,8,16,"0"),ASCII(FIDP1(IJ+NTESTCH*CHSEL,II),0,8,16,"0")," DQ:"
           GETWRMIN(WCKDUTYMRS*32+(II-1)*8+CHSEL*NTESTCH+IJ)=500
           DO GETRDR3QX8 IK=1 8 1
              IF IJ=1 OR IJ=3 OR IJ=5 OR IJ=7 THEN ENTRY
                 IF GETWRMIN(WCKDUTYMRS*32+(II-1)*8+IJ)>GETRDTRF((II-1)*88+(IJ-1)/2*22+IK) THEN GETWRMIN(WCKDUTYMRS*32+(II-1)*8+IJ)=GETRDTRF((II-1)*88+(IJ-1)/2*22+IK)
                 IF FK=#10 THEN WRITE ,ASCII(GETRDTRF((II-1)*88+(IJ-1)/2*22+IK),2,7,2," ")
              EXIT
              IF IJ=2 OR IJ=4 OR IJ=6 OR IJ=8 THEN ENTRY
                 IF GETWRMIN(WCKDUTYMRS*32+(II-1)*8+IJ)>GETRDTRF((II-1)*88+(IJ-2)/2*22+8+IK) THEN GETWRMIN(WCKDUTYMRS*32+(II-1)*8+IJ)=GETRDTRF((II-1)*88+(IJ-2)/2*22+8+IK)
                 IF FK=#10 THEN WRITE ,ASCII(GETRDTRF((II-1)*88+(IJ-2)/2*22+8+IK),2,7,2," ")
              EXIT
         GETRDR3QX8:
              IF FK=#10 THEN WRITE " (",ASCII(GETWRMIN(WCKDUTYMRS*32+(II-1)*8+CH_CODE*NTESTCH+IJ),2,7,2," ")," )"
        EXIT
    GETRDR2Q:
    EXIT
    IF SR(CURDUT,RTNUM).AND.#01=#0 THEN ENTRY
       DO GETRDR2T IJ=1 NTESTCH 1
       DO GETRDR3T IK=1 16 1 
          IF ORGNUM=16 THEN GETRDTRF((II-1)*88+(IJ-1)*22+IK)=0.0
          IF ORGNUM=8  THEN GETRDTRF((II-1)*88+(IJ-1)/2*22+IK)=0.0
GETRDR3T:          
GETRDR2T:
    EXIT
GETRDR1Q:

;  IF WCKDUTYMRS=0 THEN  GOSUB CODEREAD(0,151,931,30PS,1000PS)  ; SCREEN Cond. tDIN < 30ps  vrefdq #10             
;  IF WCKDUTYMRS=1 THEN  GOSUB CODEREAD(6,151,932,75PS,1000PS)  ; SCREEN Cond. tDIN < 85ps 0%
;  IF WCKDUTYMRS=2 THEN  GOSUB CODEREAD(0,151,933,30PS,1000PS)  ; SCREEN Cond. tDIN < 30ps  vrefdq #70             

   IF WCKDUTYMRS=0 THEN  GOSUB CODEREAD(0,151,931,30PS,1000PS)  ; SCREEN Cond. tDIN < 85ps -5%  r to f   cob 4266
   IF WCKDUTYMRS=1 THEN  GOSUB CODEREAD(0,151,932,75PS,1000PS)  ; SCREEN Cond. tDIN < 85ps 0%
   IF WCKDUTYMRS=2 THEN  GOSUB CODEREAD(0,151,933,70PS,1000PS)  ; SCREEN Cond. tDIN < 85ps 5% 


GOTO CONT

     READ CDUT TO CURDUT

           READ DCT   PDATA(DQ11C) TO TMP00 & GOSUB TQWSAVE16(NTESTCH*CHSEL+3,12)
           READ DCT   PDATA(DQ12C) TO TMP00 & GOSUB TQWSAVE16(NTESTCH*CHSEL+3,13)
           READ DCT   PDATA(DQ13C) TO TMP00 & GOSUB TQWSAVE16(NTESTCH*CHSEL+3,14)
           READ DCT   PDATA(DQ14C) TO TMP00 & GOSUB TQWSAVE16(NTESTCH*CHSEL+3,15)

           READ DCT   PDATA(DQ11D) TO TMP00 & GOSUB TQWSAVE16(NTESTCH*CHSEL+4,12)
           READ DCT   PDATA(DQ12D) TO TMP00 & GOSUB TQWSAVE16(NTESTCH*CHSEL+4,13)
           READ DCT   PDATA(DQ13D) TO TMP00 & GOSUB TQWSAVE16(NTESTCH*CHSEL+4,14)
           READ DCT   PDATA(DQ14D) TO TMP00 & GOSUB TQWSAVE16(NTESTCH*CHSEL+4,15)
           READ DCT   PDATA(DQ15D) TO TMP00 & GOSUB TQWSAVE16(NTESTCH*CHSEL+4,16)
           READ DCT   PDATA(DMI0D) TO TMP00 & GOSUB TQWSAVE16(NTESTCH*CHSEL+4,17)
           READ DCT   PDATA(DMI1D) TO TMP00 & GOSUB TQWSAVE16(NTESTCH*CHSEL+4,18)

        IF TSTITEM(1,5)="OC_RC"  THEN ENTRY
           IF TSTITEM(1,6)="OC_RC4"  THEN ENTRY
              READ DCT PDATA(RDQS0CA) TO TMP00 & GOSUB TQWSAVE15(NTESTCH*CHSEL+1,1)
              READ DCT PDATA(RDQS1CA) TO TMP00 & GOSUB TQWSAVE15(NTESTCH*CHSEL+1,4)
              READ DCT PDATA(RDQS0CB) TO TMP00 & GOSUB TQWSAVE15(NTESTCH*CHSEL+2,1)
              READ DCT PDATA(RDQS1CB) TO TMP00 & GOSUB TQWSAVE15(NTESTCH*CHSEL+2,4)
              READ DCT PDATA(RDQS0CC) TO TMP00 & GOSUB TQWSAVE15(NTESTCH*CHSEL+3,1)
              READ DCT PDATA(RDQS1CC) TO TMP00 & GOSUB TQWSAVE15(NTESTCH*CHSEL+3,4)
              READ DCT PDATA(RDQS0CD) TO TMP00 & GOSUB TQWSAVE15(NTESTCH*CHSEL+4,1)
              READ DCT PDATA(RDQS1CD) TO TMP00 & GOSUB TQWSAVE15(NTESTCH*CHSEL+4,4)
           EXIT
           IF TSTITEM(1,6)="OC_RC0"  THEN ENTRY

              READ DCT PDATA(RDQS1CB) TO TMP00 & GOSUB TQWSAVE15(NTESTCH*CHSEL+2,5)
              READ DCT PDATA(RDQS0CC) TO TMP00 & GOSUB TQWSAVE15(NTESTCH*CHSEL+3,2)
              READ DCT PDATA(RDQS1CC) TO TMP00 & GOSUB TQWSAVE15(NTESTCH*CHSEL+3,5)
              READ DCT PDATA(RDQS0CD) TO TMP00 & GOSUB TQWSAVE15(NTESTCH*CHSEL+4,2)
              READ DCT PDATA(RDQS1CD) TO TMP00 & GOSUB TQWSAVE15(NTESTCH*CHSEL+4,5)
           EXIT
           IF TSTITEM(1,6)="OC_RCC"  THEN ENTRY
              READ DCT PDATA(RDQS0CA) TO TMP00 & GOSUB TQWSAVE15(NTESTCH*CHSEL+1,3)
              READ DCT PDATA(RDQS1CA) TO TMP00 & GOSUB TQWSAVE15(NTESTCH*CHSEL+1,6)
              READ DCT PDATA(RDQS0CB) TO TMP00 & GOSUB TQWSAVE15(NTESTCH*CHSEL+2,3)

              READ DCT PDATA(RDQS1CC) TO TMP00 & GOSUB TQWSAVE15(NTESTCH*CHSEL+3,6)
              READ DCT PDATA(RDQS0CD) TO TMP00 & GOSUB TQWSAVE15(NTESTCH*CHSEL+4,3)
              READ DCT PDATA(RDQS1CD) TO TMP00 & GOSUB TQWSAVE15(NTESTCH*CHSEL+4,6)
           EXIT
        EXIT

     EXIT

;    IF ORGNUM=8  THEN ENTRY
;    EXIT


GOTO CONT

TQWSAVE15:
ARGUMENT(TSTORDTQW,SIDX0)

TTQW=TSTORDTQW
SIDX=SIDX0
;      WRITE /,"aaa ",TTQW,SIDX
       DO TQWDOE15A I=1,TP
         RTNUM=I-32*((I-1)/32)-1
         FDNUM=1   
         IF SR(CURDUT,RTNUM).AND.#01 <> #0 THEN ENTRY
            IF TSTITEM(1,3)="TQW" THEN TQW_VALUE0(I,TTQW,SIDX)=TMP00(I)    
            IF TSTITEM(1,3)="TQ1" THEN TQW_VALUE1(I,TTQW,SIDX)=TMP00(I)    
            IF TSTITEM(1,3)="OC_" THEN DCA_VALUE0(I,TTQW,SIDX)=TMP00(I)    
         EXIT
         ELSE ENTRY
            IF TSTITEM(1,3)="TQW" THEN TQW_VALUE0(I,TTQW,SIDX)=0MA
            IF TSTITEM(1,3)="TQ1" THEN TQW_VALUE1(I,TTQW,SIDX)=0MA
            IF TSTITEM(1,3)="OC_" THEN DCA_VALUE0(I,TTQW,SIDX)=0MA    
         EXIT

TQWDOE15A:

GOTO CONT



TQWSAVE16:
ARGUMENT(TSTORDODT,OIDX0)

TTQW=TSTORDODT
OIDX=OIDX0
;      WRITE /,"aaa ",TTQW,OIDX0
       DO TQWDOE16A I=1,TP
         RTNUM=I-32*((I-1)/32)-1
         FDNUM=1   
;        IF SR(CURDUTQ,RTNUM).AND.#01 <> #0 THEN ENTRY
         IF SR(CURDUT,RTNUM).AND.#01 <> #0 THEN ENTRY
            IF TSTITEM(1,3)="NT_"      THEN ODT_VALUE0(I,TTQW,OIDX0)=TMP00(I)    
            IF TSTITEM(1,7)="OCD_4P1"  THEN TQW_PHASE1(I,TTQW,OIDX0)=TMP00(I)    
            IF TSTITEM(1,7)="OCD_4P2"  THEN TQW_PHASE2(I,TTQW,OIDX0)=TMP00(I)    
            IF TSTITEM(1,7)="OCD_4P4"  THEN TQW_PHASE4(I,TTQW,OIDX0)=TMP00(I)    
            IF TSTITEM(1,7)="OCD_4P8"  THEN TQW_PHASE8(I,TTQW,OIDX0)=TMP00(I)    
            IF TSTITEM(1,7)="TQW_BL1"  THEN TQW_PHASE1(I,TTQW,OIDX0)=TMP00(I)    
            IF TSTITEM(1,7)="TQW_BL2"  THEN TQW_PHASE2(I,TTQW,OIDX0)=TMP00(I)    
            IF FAPATN(7,7)="TQW0N10"   THEN TQW_VALUE5(I,TTQW,OIDX0)=TMP00(I)  
            IF FAPATN(7,7)="TQW0N1A"   THEN TQW_VALUEA(I,TTQW,OIDX0)=TMP00(I)  
            IF FAPATN(7,7)="TQW0D10"   THEN TQW_VALUE5(I,TTQW,OIDX0)=TMP00(I)  
            IF FAPATN(7,7)="TQW0D1A"   THEN TQW_VALUEA(I,TTQW,OIDX0)=TMP00(I)  
            IF FAPATN(7,7)="TQW0T10"   THEN TQW_VALUT5(I,TTQW,OIDX0)=TMP00(I)  
            IF FAPATN(7,7)="TQW0T1A"   THEN TQW_VALUTA(I,TTQW,OIDX0)=TMP00(I)  
            IF TSTITEM(1,8)="OCD_TQW5" THEN TQW_VALUE5(I,TTQW,OIDX0)=TMP00(I)    
            IF TSTITEM(1,8)="OCD_TQWA" THEN TQW_VALUEA(I,TTQW,OIDX0)=TMP00(I)    
         EXIT
;        EXIT
         ELSE ENTRY
            IF TSTITEM(1,3)="NT_"      THEN ODT_VALUE0(I,TTQW,OIDX0)=0MA
            IF TSTITEM(1,7)="OCD_4P1"  THEN TQW_PHASE1(I,TTQW,OIDX0)=0MA    
            IF TSTITEM(1,7)="OCD_4P2"  THEN TQW_PHASE2(I,TTQW,OIDX0)=0MA    
            IF TSTITEM(1,7)="OCD_4P4"  THEN TQW_PHASE4(I,TTQW,OIDX0)=0MA    
            IF TSTITEM(1,7)="OCD_4P8"  THEN TQW_PHASE8(I,TTQW,OIDX0)=0MA    
            IF TSTITEM(1,7)="TQW_BL1"  THEN TQW_PHASE1(I,TTQW,OIDX0)=0MA    
            IF TSTITEM(1,7)="TQW_BL2"  THEN TQW_PHASE2(I,TTQW,OIDX0)=0MA    
            IF FAPATN(7,7)="TQW0N10"   THEN TQW_VALUE5(I,TTQW,OIDX0)=0MA  
            IF FAPATN(7,7)="TQW0N1A"   THEN TQW_VALUEA(I,TTQW,OIDX0)=0MA  
            IF FAPATN(7,7)="TQW0D10"   THEN TQW_VALUE5(I,TTQW,OIDX0)=0MA  
            IF FAPATN(7,7)="TQW0D1A"   THEN TQW_VALUEA(I,TTQW,OIDX0)=0MA  
            IF FAPATN(7,7)="TQW0T10"   THEN TQW_VALUE5(I,TTQW,OIDX0)=0MA 
            IF FAPATN(7,7)="TQW0T1A"   THEN TQW_VALUEA(I,TTQW,OIDX0)=0MA 
            IF TSTITEM(1,8)="OCD_TQW5" THEN TQW_VALUE5(I,TTQW,OIDX0)=TMP00(I)    
            IF TSTITEM(1,8)="OCD_TQWA" THEN TQW_VALUEA(I,TTQW,OIDX0)=TMP00(I)    
         EXIT

TQWDOE16A:

GOTO CONT


 
T0100CODE:
   ALLPIN=OPEN
   DVFSC="D"
   NRTFLG=0

TOSCRT:

  STRING WCK2DQ_TYPE(1)="-"
  
  ARGUMENT(TOSCTN1,TOSCFBIN,TOSCCOLDREV,TOSCHOTREV,TOSCSBIN,TOSC_TYPE,WCK_OSC_CODE,MR1WL,MR2RL,MR2NWR,LLM,HLM)
  WCK2DQ_TYPE=TOSC_TYPE
  
  IF PRCFLG=0 AND TOSCCOLDREV<REVFLG THEN GOTO TOSCEND
  IF PRCFLG=1 AND TOSCHOTREV<REVFLG  THEN GOTO TOSCEND

     WCK_OSC=WCK_OSC_CODE
     MR1_WL=MR1WL & MR2_RL=MR2RL & MR2_NWR=MR2NWR
     
     IF T_IVCOFF=0 THEN ENTRY
     
     IF WCK2DQ_TYPE(1)="A" THEN GOSUB FUNA(4996,0,5,5,179,LP5VD2,LP5TCK,"VND01","FMD01","PNNNX","PDCS6SOSC0N1A",#0000,0.0NS, 1.00S," WCKDQI OSC CML  INT.                  ") 
     IF WCK2DQ_TYPE(1)="B" THEN GOSUB FUNA(4996,0,5,5,179,LP5VD2,LP5TCK,"VND01","FMD01","PNNNX","PDCS6SOSC0N1B",#0000,0.0NS, 1.00S," WCKDQI OSC CML  STOP                  ") 
     IF WCK2DQ_TYPE(1)="C" THEN GOSUB FUNA(4996,0,5,5,179,LP5VD2,LP5TCK,"VND01","FMD01","PNNNX","PDCS6SOSC0N1C",#0000,0.0NS, 1.00S," WCKDQO OSC CML  INT.                  ")
     IF WCK2DQ_TYPE(1)="D" THEN GOSUB FUNA(4996,0,5,5,179,LP5VD2,LP5TCK,"VND01","FMD01","PNNNX","PDCS6SOSC0N1D",#0000,0.0NS, 1.00S," WCKDQO OSC CML  STOP                  ")
     
     EXIT
     IF T_IVCOFF=1 THEN ENTRY
     
     IF WCK2DQ_TYPE(1)="A" THEN GOSUB FUNA(4996,0,5,5,179,LP5VD2,LP5TCK,"VND01","FMD01","PNNNX","PDCS6SOSC0N3A",#0000,0.0NS, 1.00S," WCKDQI OSC CML  INT.                  ") 
     IF WCK2DQ_TYPE(1)="B" THEN GOSUB FUNA(4996,0,5,5,179,LP5VD2,LP5TCK,"VND01","FMD01","PNNNX","PDCS6SOSC0N3B",#0000,0.0NS, 1.00S," WCKDQI OSC CML  STOP                  ") 
     IF WCK2DQ_TYPE(1)="C" THEN GOSUB FUNA(4996,0,5,5,179,LP5VD2,LP5TCK,"VND01","FMD01","PNNNX","PDCS6SOSC0N3C",#0000,0.0NS, 1.00S," WCKDQO OSC CML  INT.                  ")
     IF WCK2DQ_TYPE(1)="D" THEN GOSUB FUNA(4996,0,5,5,179,LP5VD2,LP5TCK,"VND01","FMD01","PNNNX","PDCS6SOSC0N3D",#0000,0.0NS, 1.00S," WCKDQO OSC CML  STOP                  ")
     
     EXIT
     
     
     GOSUB CODEREAD(TOSCFBIN,TOSCSBIN,TOSCTN1,LLM,HLM)

TOSCEND:  
   WCK_OSC=#0  
GOTO CONT

             SET EXCLUSION :TEXT

                CALL LIB FORK("./t5511gammacombine_256.o","WAIT")
        EXIT
        IF VPARA=16 THEN ENTRY
                CALL LIB FORK("./t5511pkgcombine_128.o","WAIT")
                CALL LIB FORK("./t5511gammacombine_128.o","WAIT")
        EXIT
        IF VPARA=8  THEN ENTRY
                CALL LIB FORK("./t5511pkgcombine_64.o","WAIT")
                CALL LIB FORK("./t5511gammacombine_64.o","WAIT")
        EXIT
        IF VPARA=4  THEN ENTRY
                CALL LIB FORK("./t5511pkgcombine_32.o","WAIT")
                CALL LIB FORK("./t5511gammacombine_32.o","WAIT")
        EXIT

        IF VPGM="SUB" THEN RETURN
        CALL CUNLD("t5511_wh_train.so")
 ;      CALL LIB FORK("fssplogend","WAIT")

        STOP


;;==========================================================================================================================================================
;;        CELL&CORE, FUNCTION ITEM TEST ROUTINE
;;==========================================================================================================================================================
FUNA:
        STRING FACAL2(7)=""  & STRING FAPAT2(13)="" & STRING FASCR(8)=""   &                      & STRING FAIDX1(5)=""
        STRING FALEV2(10)="" & STRING FAFMT2(10)="" & STRING FATLE2(25)="" & STRING FATLE1(25)="" & STRING FAPAT3(9)=""
        STRING FASCM1(8)=""  & STRING FBFMT2(10)="" & STRING FBFMT5(10)="" & STRING CALN(7)=""

        ARGUMENT(FATN1,FAFBIN,COLDREVIDX,HOTREVIDX,FASBIN,FAVDD2,FRATE,FALEV1,FAFMT1,FAMOD1,FAPAT1,FATPH1,FTSAC,FAREF1,FATLE)
XXT=1
        IF DROOP_VD2_MEAS<>"Y" THEN XXT1=2
        IF DROOP_VD2_MEAS<>"Y" THEN XXT2=10

        IF DROOP_VD2_MEAS<>"Y" THEN XXT1=1000
        IF DROOP_VD2_MEAS<>"Y" THEN XXT2=1

        IF DROOP_VD2_MEAS="Y" THEN ENTRY
         XXT1=1000
        WRITE /,FAPAT1," : "
;  DO AAY6 XXT=1 1200 1
EXIT
FUNA_T:
        TN=FATN1 & FALEV2=FALEV1 & FBFMT2=FAFMT1 & FAPAT2(1,13)=FAPAT1 & FAPAT3(1,9)=FAPAT2(5,9)
                                                 ;PU414NADC5K4ANN 
        TEST TN

        FAMOD2=FAMOD1 & FATLE1=FATLE & FALEV3=NUMERIC(FALEV2(4,2)) & FBFMT4=FBFMT2 & FATLE1=FATLE
        FBFMT3=NUMERIC(FBFMT2(4,2)) & FACFMT=FBFMT2 & FAFMT2(1,1)=FACFMT(6,1) & FBFMT5(1,5)=FBFMT2(1,5) & FBFMT5(6,1)=" "

        TSTORD=1
        TSTCNT=TSTFLG
        INXCHK=0
        DINV=0
        TSAC=FTSAC

        IF PRCFLG=0 AND COLDREVIDX<REVFLG             THEN GOTO FSKP          ; COLD OLD REVISION ITEM SKIP
        IF PRCFLG=1 AND  HOTREVIDX<REVFLG             THEN GOTO FSKP          ; HOT  OLD REVISION ITEM SKIP
    
;;--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
;       PATTERN SETTING
;;--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
        RESET MPAT
        FAPATN(1,13)=FAPAT1
        IF ORGNUM=8 THEN FAPATN(3,1)="3"
;       FAPATN(14,1)=FAMOD2(2,1)                             ; NOR(NN),HSDO(DO),XOR_FIXH(XH),XOR_FIXL(XL),XOR_RDBI_HL(XT),XOR_RDBI_LH(XC)
;       IF FAMOD2(3,2)="XO" THEN FAPATN(13,1)="O"           ; XOR_OTF(XO)
;       IF FAMOD2(3,2)="XD" THEN FAPATN(13,1)="O"           ; XOR_OTF_RDBI(XD)
;       IF FAMOD2(3,2)="XT" THEN FAPATN(13,1)="O"           ; XOR_OTF(XT)
        IF FAMOD2(1,1)="D"  THEN DINV=1
        FAPATN(14,1)="N"
        FAPATN(15,1)="N"     
        IF FAMOD2(4,1)="F"  THEN FAPATN(15,1)="F"

        HSDOCNT=1
        IF SHMTESTING=1 OR DOUMI_SHM="Y" THEN ENTRY      ;ONLY SHM
           IF FAMOD2(4,1)="E" OR FAMOD2(4,1)="O" THEN ENTRY
              IF FAMOD2(4,1)="E" THEN HSDOCNT=1   ; HSDO EVEN
              IF FAMOD2(4,1)="O" THEN HSDOCNT=2   ; HSDO ODD
              FAMOD2(4,1)="D"
           EXIT
        EXIT
        IF HSDOSEL="E" THEN HSDOCNT=1
        IF HSDOSEL="O" THEN HSDOCNT=2
;;--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
;       VCC Setting
;;--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
        FAVCC2=FAVDD2

;;--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
;       PATTERN INDEX REGISETER SETTING
;;--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
       GOSUB WHINDX

;      IF FBFMT2(3,1)="D" THEN ENTRY
             IF FAMOD2(5,1)="X" THEN XSP      = XSP/#100    ; FXCELL / 256   ;        
             IF FAMOD2(5,1)="2" THEN XSP      = XSP/#200    ; FXCELL / 512   ;        
             IF FAMOD2(5,1)="N" THEN XSP      = XSP/#100    ; PARTAIL NOSCR FXCELL / 256   ;        
             IF FAMOD2(5,1)="B" THEN XSP      = XSP/#200    ; PARTAIL NOSCR FXCELL / 512   ;        
             IF FAMOD2(5,1)="Y" THEN Y16MAX   = #4 
             IF FAMOD2(5,1)="Y" THEN YSP      = #3F
;      EXIT
       
;;--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
;       SCRAMBLE ENABLE                                
;;--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
       IF ORGNUM=16 THEN ENTRY
          FASCR="CDCS8FUL"
          IF FAMOD2(5,1)="X" THEN FASCR = "CDCS8PA1"     ; FXCELL / 128
;         IF FAMOD2(5,1)="X" THEN FASCR = "CDCS8PA2"     ; FXCELL / 128
          IF FAMOD2(5,1)="2" THEN FASCR = "CDCS8PA2"     ; FXCELL / 512
          IF FAMOD2(5,1)="N" THEN FASCR = "CDCS8FUL"     ; FXCELL / 128
          IF FAMOD2(5,1)="Y" THEN FASCR = "CDCS8FUL" 
          IF FAMOD2(5,1)="B" THEN FASCR = "CDCS8PB3"     ; 2/BLOCK
       EXIT
       
       IF ORGNUM=8 THEN ENTRY
          FASCR="CC3S8FUL"
          IF FAMOD2(5,1)="X" THEN FASCR = "CD3S8PA1"     ; FXCELL / 128
          IF FAMOD2(5,1)="2" THEN FASCR = "CD3S8PA2"     ; FXCELL / 256
          IF FAMOD2(5,1)="N" THEN FASCR = "CD3S8FUL"     ; FXCELL / 128
          IF FAMOD2(5,1)="Y" THEN FASCR = "CD3S8FUL" 
       EXIT
       
;      IF CURSCR<>FASCR THEN ENTRY       
           SELECT SCRDATA ENABLE
           SEND SCRDATA <FASCR>    
           EXEC CCALL("SetScramblebit",FASCR) 
           CURSCR=FASCR
;      EXIT

;;--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
;       DBI SETTING                                    
;;--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
        MR3_WDBI=0   &  MR3_RDBI=0
        IF FAMOD2(2,1)="W" THEN MR3_WDBI=#1
        IF FAMOD2(2,1)="R" THEN MR3_RDBI=#1
        IF FAMOD2(2,1)="D" THEN ENTRY & MR3_WDBI=#1 & MR3_RDBI=#1 & EXIT
       
;       WCK FREERUN       
        MR18_WCKALWAYSON=#0
        IF FAPAT3(2,1)="F" OR FAPAT3(2,1)="R" THEN MR18_WCKALWAYSON=#1
        IF FAPAT3(2,1)="F" OR FAPAT3(2,1)="R" THEN L_DELAY="Y"   
        IF FAPAT3(2,1)="F" AND TSPEED>7499 THEN L_DELAY="N"   
        MR22_RECC=#0 & MR22_WECC=#0 
        IF FAMOD2(1,1)="L" THEN ENTRY & MR22_RECC=#1 & MR22_WECC=#1 & EXIT

;       IF TSPEED=7500 THEN ENTRY
;          IF MR3_RDBI=#1 THEN ENTRY & MR1_WL=#7 & MR2_RL=#B & MR2_NWR=#B & EXIT
;          IF MR3_RDBI=#0 THEN ENTRY & MR1_WL=#7 & MR2_RL=#A & MR2_NWR=#B & EXIT     
;          IF FAMOD2(1,1)="L" THEN ENTRY & MR1_WL=#7 & MR2_RL=#B & MR2_NWR=#B & EXIT
;       EXIT

        GOSUB WLRLCAL(WCKCKRATIO,MR1_WL,MR2_RL,DVFSC,WLSET,L_DELAY)

       IF TMRS_GRP_NAME(1,6)="RLCHG4" THEN ENTRY
          CWL=0 & CRL=16
       EXIT  

        WL=CWL & RL=CRL

;      IF FAPATN(11,1)="D" OR FAPATN(11,1)="L"  THEN RL=CRL+RDBI_DIFF     ; RDBI ON OR LINK_ECC ON
;      ALLIO=OPEN

       GOSUB (FBFMT3) FMD01CA,FMD02CA,FMD03CA,FMD04CA
     
 C2TSTF:    

;;--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
;       Speed Item STRB OFFSET Setting
;;--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
       IF FBFMT2(3,1)<>"R" THEN ENTRY
          TCK=FRATE
;         GOSUB DDRTIM
          IF SHMTESTING=1 OR DOUMI_SHM="Y" THEN ENTRY ; setting in training 
             IF WCKCKRATIO=4 THEN GOSUB TFCHG1(TCK,4.5NS)
             IF WCKCKRATIO=2 THEN GOSUB TFCHG2(TCK,  9NS)
          EXIT
          STRB1   =<1>TSACE+TSAC
          STRB3   =<1>TSACE+TSAC 
          STRB129 =<1>TSACO+TSAC
          STRB131 =<1>TSACO+TSAC         
          
          IF FAMOD2(4,1)="D" OR FAMOD2(4,1)="X" OR FAMOD2(4,1)="F" THEN ENTRY
;            STRB129 =<1>TSACE+TSAC
;            STRB131 =<1>TSACE+TSAC      

             IF HSDOCNT=1  THEN ENTRY & STRB1   =<1>TSACE+TSAC  & STRB3   =<1>TSACE+TSAC  & STRB129 =<1>TSACO+TSAC  & STRB131 =<1>TSACO+TSAC & EXIT
             IF HSDOCNT=2  THEN ENTRY & STRB129 =<1>TSACE+TSAC  & STRB131 =<1>TSACE+TSAC  & STRB1   =<1>TSACO+TSAC  & STRB3   =<1>TSACO+TSAC & EXIT
            IF CRL=79 THEN ENTRY
             IF HSDOCNT=1  THEN ENTRY & STRB1   =<1>TSACE+TSAC+TRATE  & STRB3   =<1>TSACE+TSAC+TRATE  & STRB129 =<1>TSACO+TSAC+TRATE  & STRB131 =<1>TSACO+TSAC+TRATE & EXIT
             IF HSDOCNT=2  THEN ENTRY & STRB129 =<1>TSACE+TSAC+TRATE  & STRB131 =<1>TSACE+TSAC+TRATE  & STRB1   =<1>TSACO+TSAC+TRATE  & STRB3   =<1>TSACO+TSAC+TRATE & EXIT
            EXIT
 
          EXIT   
       ;  IF FAMOD2(4,1)="N" AND TSPEED>3500 THEN ENTRY 
       ;  
       ;     STRB1   =<1>TSACE+TSAC-TRATE/4
       ;     STRB3   =<1>TSACE+TSAC-TRATE/4 
       ;     STRB129 =<1>TSACO+TSAC-TRATE/4
       ;     STRB131 =<1>TSACO+TSAC-TRATE/4         
       ;  
       ;  
       ;  EXIT
       EXIT
             
;;--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
;       PIN FORMAT                      
;;--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
;      SRON

           IF ORGNUM<>8 THEN GOSUB IOFX16
           IF ORGNUM=8  THEN GOSUB IOFX8

;      NORMAL/FUNCTION ITEM CS/CKE Control
;---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
;       CFLG SETTING BY TEST MRS 
;;--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
        CCFLG=#01
        IF FBFMT2(2,1)="S" OR FBFMT2(2,1)="P"  THEN CCFLG=#00
        IF                    FBFMT2(2,1)="P"  THEN CCFLG=#00
        IF DOUMITEST<>0    OR DOUMI_SHM="Y"    THEN CCFLG=#00
        IF FBFMT2(3,1)="D" THEN ENTRY                                          ; DVFSC  DVFSQ   HSDI  HSDI  HSDO  HSDO  HSDO
                                                  HSDOFLG = #00                ;   8      7      6     5     4     3     2 
           IF FAMOD2(3,1)="N"               THEN    CCFLG = CCFLG.OR.#00       ;                                              ;NOR  
           IF FAMOD2(4,1)="D" AND HSDOCNT=1 THEN  HSDOFLG = HSDOFLG.OR.#04     ;                                  EVEN        ;HSDO_EVEN
           IF FAMOD2(4,1)="D" AND HSDOCNT=2 THEN  HSDOFLG = HSDOFLG.OR.#08     ;                            ODD               ;HSDO_ODD
           IF FAMOD2(4,1)="X"               THEN  HSDOFLG = HSDOFLG.OR.#0C     ;                            XOR   XOR         ;XOR_FIXH/FIXL/OTF/RDBI
           IF FAMOD2(4,1)="F"               THEN  HSDOFLG = HSDOFLG.OR.#02     ;                                        OTF   ;HSDO_OTF 

           IF FAMOD2(3,1)="O"               THEN    CCFLG = CCFLG.OR.#20       ;               DIOTF                          ;HSDI
           IF FAMOD2(3,1)="T"               THEN    CCFLG = CCFLG.OR.#10       ;                     DMIOTF                   ;HSDI

;          IF DVFSC="E" AND TSPEED <=1600   THEN    CCFLG = CCFLG.OR.#80       ;  EN                    
;          IF DVFSQ="E" AND TSPEED <=3200   THEN    CCFLG = CCFLG.OR.#40       ;         EN             
                                                                              
           IF FBFMT2(2,1)="M"               THEN    CCFLG = CCFLG.OR.#000      ;   9 EXTRA TMRS OFF
           IF FBFMT2(2,1)="S"               THEN    CCFLG = CCFLG.OR.#100      ;   9 EXTRA TMRS ON
           IF FBFMT2(2,1)="T"               THEN    CCFLG = CCFLG.OR.#100      ;   9 EXTRA TMRS ON

        EXIT

 ;---------- wck free enter ----------;
           IF L_DELAY="Y" THEN ENTRY                     ;MR2 7  6  5  4  DBI
                                                         ;    16 15 14 13 12
              IF MR1_WL=#0   THEN CCFLG = CCFLG.OR.#0000 ;               
              IF MR1_WL=#1   THEN CCFLG = CCFLG.OR.#1000 ;             Y 
              IF MR1_WL=#2   THEN CCFLG = CCFLG.OR.#2000 ;          Y    
              IF MR1_WL=#3   THEN CCFLG = CCFLG.OR.#3000 ;          Y  Y 
              IF MR1_WL=#4   THEN CCFLG = CCFLG.OR.#4000 ;       Y       
              IF MR1_WL=#5   THEN CCFLG = CCFLG.OR.#5000 ;       Y     Y 
              IF MR1_WL=#6   THEN CCFLG = CCFLG.OR.#6000 ;       Y  Y    
              IF MR1_WL=#7   THEN CCFLG = CCFLG.OR.#7000 ;       Y  Y  Y 
              IF MR1_WL=#8   THEN CCFLG = CCFLG.OR.#8000 ;    Y          
              IF MR1_WL=#9   THEN CCFLG = CCFLG.OR.#9000 ;    Y        Y 
              IF MR1_WL=#A   THEN CCFLG = CCFLG.OR.#A000 ;    Y     Y    
              IF MR1_WL=#B   THEN CCFLG = CCFLG.OR.#B000 ;    Y     Y  Y 
              IF MR1_WL=#C   THEN CCFLG = CCFLG.OR.#C000 ;    Y     Y    
              IF MR1_WL=#D   THEN CCFLG = CCFLG.OR.#D000 ;    Y     Y  Y 
           EXIT
           
;          IF FAPAT3(2,1)="F" AND TSPEED=7500 THEN ENTRY
;             IF MR1_WL=#7 THEN CCFLG = CCFLG.OR.#C000 ;    Y     Y    
;          EXIT

           IF FAPATN(7,3)="OSC" THEN ENTRY               ;MR2 7  6  5  4  DBI
                                                         ;    16 15 14 13 12
              IF MR1_WL=#0   THEN CCFLG = CCFLG.OR.#0000 ;               
              IF MR1_WL=#1   THEN CCFLG = CCFLG.OR.#1000 ;             Y 
              IF MR1_WL=#2   THEN CCFLG = CCFLG.OR.#2000 ;          Y    
              IF MR1_WL=#3   THEN CCFLG = CCFLG.OR.#3000 ;          Y  Y 
              IF MR1_WL=#4   THEN CCFLG = CCFLG.OR.#4000 ;       Y       
              IF MR1_WL=#5   THEN CCFLG = CCFLG.OR.#5000 ;       Y     Y 
              IF MR1_WL=#6   THEN CCFLG = CCFLG.OR.#6000 ;       Y  Y    
              IF MR1_WL=#7   THEN CCFLG = CCFLG.OR.#7000 ;       Y  Y  Y 
              IF MR1_WL=#8   THEN CCFLG = CCFLG.OR.#8000 ;    Y          
              IF MR1_WL=#9   THEN CCFLG = CCFLG.OR.#9000 ;    Y        Y 
              IF MR1_WL=#A   THEN CCFLG = CCFLG.OR.#A000 ;    Y     Y    
              IF MR1_WL=#B   THEN CCFLG = CCFLG.OR.#B000 ;    Y     Y  Y 
              IF MR1_WL=#C   THEN CCFLG = CCFLG.OR.#C000 ;    Y     Y    
              IF MR1_WL=#D   THEN CCFLG = CCFLG.OR.#D000 ;    Y     Y  Y 
              IF MR3_RDBI=#1 THEN CCFLG = CCFLG.OR.#0800 ;                 Y


           EXIT
         CCFLG = CCFLG.OR.HSDOFLG
               
;;--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
;       PATTERN SENDING START    
;---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
        
        SEND MPAT <FAPATN>
        GOSUB PIDXST(FAPAT3)
        IF INXCHK=0 THEN ENTRY & WRITE/"CHECK INDEX SUB (PATN=",FAPAT3,",INXCHK=",INXCHK,")" & GOTO ERRMSG & EXIT

        IF FAMOD2(4,1)="N"                 THEN ENTRY & REG MPAT CPE1=RD  & REG MPAT CPE2=RD  & REG MPAT CPE3=C12 & REG MPAT CPE4=C12 & EXIT
;       IF FAMOD2(4,1)="N"                 THEN ENTRY & REG MPAT CPE1=RD  & REG MPAT CPE2=RD  & REG MPAT CPE3=C30 & REG MPAT CPE4=C30 & EXIT

        IF FAMOD2(4,1)="N" AND FAPATN(7,3)="RDC" THEN ENTRY & REG MPAT CPE1=RD  & REG MPAT CPE2=RD  & REG MPAT CPE3=C12 & REG MPAT CPE4=C12 & EXIT
        IF FAMOD2(4,1)="N" AND FAPATN(7,3)="WTR" THEN ENTRY & REG MPAT CPE1=RD  & REG MPAT CPE2=RD  & REG MPAT CPE3=C12 & REG MPAT CPE4=C12 & EXIT

;       IF FAMOD2(4,1)="N" AND TSPEED>3500 THEN ENTRY & REG MPAT CPE1=RD  & REG MPAT CPE2=RD  & REG MPAT CPE3=C30 & REG MPAT CPE4=C30 & EXIT
        IF FAMOD2(4,1)="N" AND FAPATN(7,3)="OSC" THEN ENTRY & REG MPAT CPE1=RD  & REG MPAT CPE2=C30 & REG MPAT CPE3=C12 & REG MPAT CPE4=C12 & EXIT

        IF FAMOD2(4,1)="D" AND HSDOCNT=1   THEN ENTRY & REG MPAT CPE1=RD  & REG MPAT CPE2=C30 & REG MPAT CPE3=C30 & REG MPAT CPE4=C30 & EXIT
        IF FAMOD2(4,1)="D" AND HSDOCNT=2   THEN ENTRY & REG MPAT CPE1=C30 & REG MPAT CPE2=RD  & REG MPAT CPE3=C30 & REG MPAT CPE4=C30 & EXIT

        IF FAMOD2(4,1)="X"                 THEN ENTRY & REG MPAT CPE1=RD  & REG MPAT CPE2=C30 & REG MPAT CPE3=C30 & REG MPAT CPE4=C30 & EXIT
        IF FAMOD2(4,1)="F"                 THEN ENTRY & REG MPAT CPE1=RD  & REG MPAT CPE2=C30 & REG MPAT CPE3=C30 & REG MPAT CPE4=C30 & EXIT
        IF TN=369                          THEN ENTRY & REG MPAT CPE1=RD  & REG MPAT CPE2=RD  & REG MPAT CPE3=C30 & REG MPAT CPE4=C30 & EXIT


        IF FAPATN(7,7)="LEC5N5C" OR FAPATN(7,7)="LEC5N5D" OR FAPATN(7,7)="LEC4N2C" OR FAPATN(7,7)="LEC4N2D"  THEN ENTRY     
           IF FAMOD2(4,1)="D" AND HSDOCNT=1   THEN ENTRY & REG MPAT CPE1=RD  & REG MPAT CPE2=C30 & REG MPAT CPE3=C13 & REG MPAT CPE4=C30 & EXIT
           IF FAMOD2(4,1)="D" AND HSDOCNT=2   THEN ENTRY & REG MPAT CPE1=C30 & REG MPAT CPE2=RD  & REG MPAT CPE3=C30 & REG MPAT CPE4=C13 & EXIT
        EXIT
        
        REG MPAT PC=#00
        REG MPAT CFLG = CCFLG

        REG MPAT TIMER=FAREF1

        IF FATPH1<>#0000 THEN ENTRY
           REG MPAT TPH1_1=FATPH1
           REG MPAT TPH2_1=FATPH1
        EXIT  
        
        GOSUB MR_SETTING ;  MR_VALUE TO YTx
        IF SHMTESTING=1     THEN GOSUB SHMCONDTION
        IF DOUMI_SHM="Y"    THEN GOSUB DSHM_CONDTION
        IF FBFMT2(2,1)="S"  THEN GOSUB TEST_TMRS_SETTING
        IF FBFMT2(2,1)="T"  THEN GOSUB TEST_TMRS_SETTING
        IF TN=369 THEN REG MPAT YT8=#08
   
   
        IF C8OFFSET<>0PS THEN ENTRY
        TIMING SET = 1
        
        BCLK8  =  WCKR           WCKR2   WCKR   WCKR   WCKR   WCKR   WCKR   WCKR2        ;WCK
        CCLK8  =  WCKF+C8OFFSET  WCKF2   WCKF   WCKF   WCKF   WCKF   WCKF   WCKF2        ;WCK
        
        
        EXIT

        IF FAPATN(7,4)="SEC1"  THEN ENTRY
              TIMING SET=1
           ;            1      2      3
           BCLK9  =  TDSVA  TDSVA2  TDSVA+TRATE/4
           CCLK9  =  TDHVA  TDHVA2  TDHVA+TRATE/4

           BCLK10 =  TDSVA  TDSVA2  TDSVA+TRATE/4
           CCLK10 =  TDHVA  TDHVA2  TDHVA+TRATE/4

        EXIT
        IF FAPATN(7,7)="M265N5A" OR FAPATN(7,7)="M265N5B"  THEN ENTRY
              TIMING SET=1
           ;            1      2      3     4                  5                6             7
;          BCLK8  =  WCKR   WCKR2   WCKR   WCKR+TRATE*0.1    WCKR-TRATE*0.1    WCKR   WCKR   WCKR2        ;WCK
           CCLK8  =  WCKF   WCKF2   WCKF   WCKF+TRATE*0.1    WCKF-TRATE*0.1    WCKF   WCKF   WCKF2        ;WCK

        EXIT
       IF FAPATN(7,7)="COB7N5W" OR FAPATN(7,7)="COB6N4W" THEN ENTRY 
          REG MPAT D1B_1=MR30_DCA
          REG MPAT D1E_1=MR24_DFE
       EXIT


;--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
;------NRT NG_BIN For PKGMAP-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
;--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
        IF NRTFLG=1 THEN ENTRY  ;;NRT
           FATT=TN+5000          ;;NRT
           TEST FATT
        EXIT

        SSBIN=FASBIN
;--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
;       TEST
;--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
       ;INSERT MAIN_SDEFINE           ; for manual shmoo

        IF FK=#4000 AND SHMFLG=1 THEN GOTO CONT     ; HSUSHM


        IF DROOP_VD2_MEAS="Y" THEN ENTRY
 ; DO AAY6 XXT=1 50 1
        
           START MPAT *
 ; XXT=1
 ;         WAIT TIME 1MS
           WAIT TIME XXT*10US   
           MEAS VS2!1:IMDAT
           WAIT TIME 20MS
 
           WAIT TIME 200MS
           STOP MPAT
       ;   WRITE /,XXT*10," : ",IMDAT(2),ASCII(IMDAT(2)/1MA,2,8,1," ")
           WRITE ASCII(IMDAT(2)/1MA,2,8,1," ")
 ;         GOTO CONT
                

        EXIT


        IF DROOP_VD2_MEAS<>"Y" THEN ENTRY
        MEAS MPAT(3) & XXX: 
        EXIT




        READ CDUT TO CURDUT
        READ FDUT TO CFDUT

;       IF FBFMT2(3,1)<>"R" AND FK=#4000 THEN  GOTO HSHMS    ;HSUSHM

;-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    IF ORGNUM=16 THEN ENTRY
       READ FUNC1(DATA0) TO PFDATA0 ;;CS0_0 DO=1
       READ FUNC1(DATA1) TO PFDATA1 ;;CS0_1 DO=2
       READ FUNC1(DATA2) TO PFDATA2 ;;CS1_0 DO=3
       READ FUNC1(DATA3) TO PFDATA3 ;;CS1_1 DO=4
    EXIT
    IF ORGNUM=8 THEN ENTRY
       READ FUNC1(DATAX80) TO PFDATA0 ;;CS_A0 DO=1
       READ FUNC1(DATAX81) TO PFDATA1 ;;CS_A1 DO=2
       READ FUNC1(DATAX82) TO PFDATA2 ;;CS_B0 DO=3
       READ FUNC1(DATAX83) TO PFDATA3 ;;CS_B1 DO=4
       READ FUNC1(DATAX84) TO PFDATA4 ;;CS_C0 DO=5
       READ FUNC1(DATAX85) TO PFDATA5 ;;CS_C1 DO=6
       READ FUNC1(DATAX86) TO PFDATA6 ;;CS_D0 DO=7
       READ FUNC1(DATAX87) TO PFDATA7 ;;CS_D1 DO=8
    EXIT
   
       GOSUB DUTRESLT
       IF DOUMI_SHM="Y" THEN GOTO LOOPCTRL

  IF FK=#10 AND SHMTESTING=0 AND FAPATN(7,3)<>"OSC" AND FAPATN(7,3)<>"ZQC"THEN ENTRY
       WRITE /,STEP," ",CSN," ","TN=",ASCII(TN,2,5,0," "),ASCII(LP5VD2/1V,2,6,3," "),"V",ASCII(LP5VD2L/1V,2,6,3," "),"V",ASCII(LP5VDQ/1V,2,6,3," "),"V",ASCII(LP5TCK/1PS,2,7,1," "),"PS" 
       WRITE  ," ",FREQ," ",FAFMT1," ",FAMOD2," ",ASCII(HSDOCNT,2,1,0," ")," ",FAPATN," ",ASCII(AA/1S,1,6,1," "),ASCII(CC/1S,1,6,2," "),"   "
       WRITE ,DSPREPA(1,TP),"_(",DSPREPA(1*TP+1,TP),")(",DSPREPA(2*TP+1,TP),")(",DSPREPA(3*TP+1,TP),")(",DSPREPA(4*TP+1,TP),")"
       IF EXT_IOF="Y"  OR  FATPH1<>#0000 THEN WRITE " #",ASCII(FATPH1,5,4)
       IF EXT_IOF<>"Y" AND FATPH1=#0000  THEN WRITE " -----"
       IF FBFMT2(2,1)="S" OR FBFMT2(2,1)="T" THEN ENTRY
          IF TMRS_GRP_NAME="" THEN WRITE " ",TMRS_1
          IF TMRS_GRP_NAME<>"" THEN WRITE " ",TMRS_GRP_NAME
       EXIT
  EXIT

;    IF FK=#10 AND SHMTESTING=0 AND FAPATN(7,3)<>"OSC" AND ORGNUM=8  THEN ENTRY 
;      WRITE /,STEP," ",CSN," ","TN=",ASCII(TN,2,5,0," "),ASCII(LP5VD2/1V,2,6,3," "),"V",ASCII(LP5VD2L/1V,2,6,3," "),"V",ASCII(LP5VDQ/1V,2,6,3," "),"V",ASCII(LP5TCK/1PS,2,7,1," "),"PS"
;      WRITE  ," ",FREQ," ",FAFMT1," ",FAMOD2," ",ASCII(HSDOCNT,2,1,0," ")," ",FAPATN," ",ASCII(AA/1S,1,6,1," "),ASCII(CC/1S,1,6,2," "),"   ", DSPREPA(1,TP)
;      WRITE  ,"_(",DSPREPA(1*TP+1,TP),")(",DSPREPA(2*TP+1,TP),")(",DSPREPA(3*TP+1,TP),")(",DSPREPA(4*TP+1,TP),")",DSPREPA(5*TP+1,TP),")(",DSPREPA(6*TP+1,TP),")(",DSPREPA(7*TP+1,TP),")(",DSPREPA(8*TP+1,TP),")"
;    EXIT


;------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
;;--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
; NG CHECK LOGIC
;;--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   IF NRTFLG=2 AND FAPAT2(5,3)="NGC" THEN ENTRY
     GOSUB NGCHK1
     GOTO LOOPCTRL
   EXIT

;--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
; NRT LOGIC
;--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   IF NRTFLG=0 THEN ENTRY          ;;NRT
      IF FAFBIN<>0 THEN GOSUB FCHK
      GOSUB FBIN(FAFBIN,FASBIN)    ;;NORMAL REJECTION
   EXIT
   ELSE ENTRY
;;==================  NO REJECTION TEST LOGIC =====================
 
     NFDUT=CFDUT.AND.(.NOT.TFDUT).AND.CURDUT
    ;NFDUT(1)=CFDUT(1).AND.(.NOT.TFDUT(1)).AND.CURDUT(1)
    ;NFDUT(3)=CFDUT(3).AND.(.NOT.TFDUT(3)).AND.CURDUT(3)
     GOSUB NRNCHK(TN,FATT)
     IF FAFBIN<0 OR FAFBIN>8 THEN ENTRY
        GOSUB FBIN(8,008)
        GOTO TEXT
     EXIT
 
     IF FAFBIN=0 THEN ENTRY
        IF MAX(NFDUT)>#0 THEN ENTRY
           SET JDUT NFDUT
           SET FAIL TN
           RESET JDUT
        EXIT
     EXIT
 
     IF FAFBIN>0 AND FAFBIN<=8 THEN ENTRY
        IF MAX(NFDUT)>#0 THEN ENTRY
           SET JDUT NFDUT
           TEST TN
           SET FAIL TN
           GOSUB FCHK
           SET CATEGORY FASBIN
           SET SORT FAFBIN
           RESET JDUT
        EXIT
       ;TFDUT(1)=TFDUT(1).OR.CFDUT(1)
       ;TFDUT(3)=TFDUT(3).OR.CFDUT(3)
        TFDUT=TFDUT.OR.CFDUT
        TFDUT=TFDUT.OR.CFDUT
     EXIT
    ;WRITE /,"NFDUT = ",NFDUT
    ;WRITE /,"CFDUT = ",CFDUT
    ;WRITE /,"TFDUT = ",TFDUT
    ;WRITE /,"CRDUT = ",CURDUT
;;==================  NO REJECTION TEST LOGIC =====================
   EXIT


LOOPCTRL:
;;--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
;  ******  TEST LOOPING CONTORL LOGIC START  ******
;;--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------


    INXCHK=0
     IF SHMTESTING=1 OR DOUMI_SHM="Y" OR HSDOSEL="E" OR HSDOSEL="O" THEN GOTO FSKP   ; ONLY SHMTEST
     IF FAMOD2(4,1)="D" AND HSDOCNT=1 THEN ENTRY & HSDOCNT=2 & GOTO C2TSTF & EXIT

;;--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
;  ******  TEST LOOPING CONTORL LOGIC END    ******
;;--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 HSHME:                          ;HSUSHM
 FSKP:
     GOSUB WHINDX     ;; Return Real IOFLG VALUE @ DDPFLG=7 Case & INDEX REFRESH EVERY CYCLE
     TEST TN       ;; TEST NO. INITIALIZE
     TSAC=0NS
     
       AAY6:

     
GOTO CONT

WHINDX:
         XYMAX=#100000 & NBANK = #10 & XLOOPMAX=#10000 & Y16MAX=#40 & Y32MAX=#20   ;; 16Gb XH/WH-ver
                                       XSP     =#FFFF  & YSP   =#3FF              
;        XYMAX=#C0000  & NBANK = #10 & XLOOPMAX=#C000  & Y16MAX=#40 & Y32MAX=#20   ;; 12Gb KL-ver
;                                      XSP     =#BFFF  & YSP   =#3FF              
;        XYMAX=#80000  & NBANK = #10 & XLOOPMAX=#8000  & Y16MAX=#40 & Y32MAX=#20   ;; 8Gb KU-ver 
;                                      XSP     =#7FFF  & YSP   =#3FF

GOTO CONT

DUTRESLT:

    IF ORGNUM=16 THEN ENTRY
       READ FUNC1(DATA0) TO PFDATA0 ;;CS0_0 DO=1
       READ FUNC1(DATA1) TO PFDATA1 ;;CS0_1 DO=2
       READ FUNC1(DATA2) TO PFDATA2 ;;CS1_0 DO=3
       READ FUNC1(DATA3) TO PFDATA3 ;;CS1_1 DO=4
    EXIT
    IF ORGNUM=8 THEN ENTRY
       READ FUNC1(DATAX80) TO PFDATA0 ;;CS_A0 DO=1
       READ FUNC1(DATAX81) TO PFDATA1 ;;CS_A1 DO=2
       READ FUNC1(DATAX82) TO PFDATA2 ;;CS_B0 DO=3
       READ FUNC1(DATAX83) TO PFDATA3 ;;CS_B1 DO=4
       READ FUNC1(DATAX84) TO PFDATA4 ;;CS_C0 DO=5
       READ FUNC1(DATAX85) TO PFDATA5 ;;CS_C1 DO=6
       READ FUNC1(DATAX86) TO PFDATA6 ;;CS_D0 DO=7
       READ FUNC1(DATAX87) TO PFDATA7 ;;CS_D1 DO=8
    EXIT

          CSN="CS0"
          IF CHSEL=0 THEN CSN="R0"
          IF CHSEL=1 THEN CSN="R1"

          READ TIMER TO AA
          CC=AA-BB
          BB=AA
;         WRITE [1,1(7,2)]AA/1S "s ",[1,1(7,2)]CC/1S "s ","   "

           READ CDUT TO CURDUT
           READ FDUT TO CFDUT

           FREQ=(((1/LP5TCK)*2)/(1GHZ))*1000
           FREQ=TRUNK(FREQ)
           FREQ=ASCII(FREQ,1,4,10,"0")

   IF ORGNUM=16 THEN ENTRY

;;;;;;     READ FUNC1(DATA0) TO PFDATA0
;;;;;;     READ FUNC1(DATA1) TO PFDATA1
;;;;;;     READ FUNC1(DATA2) TO PFDATA2
;;;;;;     READ FUNC1(DATA3) TO PFDATA3

        DO N01 DN=1,TP
           DSPREPA(DN,1)="-"
           DSPREPA(TP*1+DN,1)="-"
           DSPREPA(TP*2+DN,1)="-"
           DSPREPA(TP*3+DN,1)="-"
           DSPREPA(TP*4+DN,1)="-"
           FDNUM=(MOD((DN-1)/TPARA1)/32)*2+(DN-1)/TPARA1+1
           RTNUM=DN-32*((DN-1)/32)-1

          ;IF SR(CURDUT(FDNUM),RTNUM).AND.#01 <> #0 THEN ENTRY
           IF SR(CURDUT,RTNUM).AND.#01 <> #0 THEN ENTRY
              DSPREPA(DN,1)="P"
              DSPREPA(TP*1+DN,1)="P"
              DSPREPA(TP*2+DN,1)="P"
              DSPREPA(TP*3+DN,1)="P"
              DSPREPA(TP*4+DN,1)="P"
             ;IF SR(CFDUT(FDNUM),RTNUM).AND.#01 <> #0 THEN DSPREPA(DN,1)="*"
              IF SR(CFDUT,RTNUM).AND.#01 <> #0 THEN DSPREPA(DN,1)="*"
              IF PFDATA0(DN) <> #0 THEN DSPREPA(TP*1+DN,1)="*"
              IF PFDATA1(DN) <> #0 THEN DSPREPA(TP*2+DN,1)="*"
              IF PFDATA2(DN) <> #0 THEN DSPREPA(TP*3+DN,1)="*"
              IF PFDATA3(DN) <> #0 THEN DSPREPA(TP*4+DN,1)="*"
           EXIT
        N01:
        IF TP=16 THEN ENTRY
           IF FK=#2000 AND FK<>#20 THEN ENTRY
              WRITE "   ", DSPREPA(1,TP)," "
           EXIT
           IF FK=#20 THEN ENTRY
              WRITE /," ",FAPAT1,"  :      8|     16|"
              WRITE /,"   ",ASCII(TN,2,5,1," "),"(B):",DSPREPA(1,TP)," "
              WRITE /,"   ",ASCII(TN,2,5,1," "),"(",ASCII(0,2,1,1," "),"):",DSPREPA(TP*1+1,TP)," "
              WRITE /,"   ",ASCII(TN,2,5,1," "),"(",ASCII(1,2,1,1," "),"):",DSPREPA(TP*2+1,TP)," "
              WRITE /,"   ",ASCII(TN,2,5,1," "),"(",ASCII(2,2,1,1," "),"):",DSPREPA(TP*3+1,TP)," "
              WRITE /,"   ",ASCII(TN,2,5,1," "),"(",ASCII(3,2,1,1," "),"):",DSPREPA(TP*4+1,TP)," "
           EXIT
        EXIT
   EXIT

   IF ORGNUM=8 THEN ENTRY

;;;;    READ FUNC1(DATAX80) TO PFDATA0 ;;CS_A0 DO=1
;;;;    READ FUNC1(DATAX81) TO PFDATA1 ;;CS_A1 DO=2
;;;;    READ FUNC1(DATAX82) TO PFDATA2 ;;CS_B0 DO=3
;;;;    READ FUNC1(DATAX83) TO PFDATA3 ;;CS_B1 DO=4
;;;;    READ FUNC1(DATAX84) TO PFDATA4 ;;CS_C0 DO=5
;;;;    READ FUNC1(DATAX85) TO PFDATA5 ;;CS_C1 DO=6
;;;;    READ FUNC1(DATAX86) TO PFDATA6 ;;CS_D0 DO=7
;;;;    READ FUNC1(DATAX87) TO PFDATA7 ;;CS_D1 DO=8

        DO N02 DN=1,TP
           DSPREPA(DN,1)="-"
           DSPREPA(TP*1+DN,1)="-"
           DSPREPA(TP*2+DN,1)="-"
           DSPREPA(TP*3+DN,1)="-"
           DSPREPA(TP*4+DN,1)="-"
           DSPREPA(TP*5+DN,1)="-"
           DSPREPA(TP*6+DN,1)="-"
           DSPREPA(TP*7+DN,1)="-"
           DSPREPA(TP*8+DN,1)="-"
           FDNUM=(MOD((DN-1)/TPARA1)/32)*2+(DN-1)/TPARA1+1
           RTNUM=DN-32*((DN-1)/32)-1

          ;IF SR(CURDUT(FDNUM),RTNUM).AND.#01 <> #0 THEN ENTRY
           IF SR(CURDUT,RTNUM).AND.#01 <> #0 THEN ENTRY
              DSPREPA(DN,1)="P"
              DSPREPA(TP*1+DN,1)="P"
              DSPREPA(TP*2+DN,1)="P"
              DSPREPA(TP*3+DN,1)="P"
              DSPREPA(TP*4+DN,1)="P"
              DSPREPA(TP*5+DN,1)="P"
              DSPREPA(TP*6+DN,1)="P"
              DSPREPA(TP*7+DN,1)="P"
              DSPREPA(TP*8+DN,1)="P"
             ;IF SR(CFDUT(FDNUM),RTNUM).AND.#01 <> #0 THEN DSPREPA(DN,1)="*"
              IF SR(CFDUT,RTNUM).AND.#01 <> #0 THEN DSPREPA(DN,1)="*"
              IF PFDATA0(DN) <> #0 THEN DSPREPA(TP*1+DN,1)="*"
              IF PFDATA1(DN) <> #0 THEN DSPREPA(TP*2+DN,1)="*"
              IF PFDATA2(DN) <> #0 THEN DSPREPA(TP*3+DN,1)="*"
              IF PFDATA3(DN) <> #0 THEN DSPREPA(TP*4+DN,1)="*"
              IF PFDATA4(DN) <> #0 THEN DSPREPA(TP*5+DN,1)="*"
              IF PFDATA5(DN) <> #0 THEN DSPREPA(TP*6+DN,1)="*"
              IF PFDATA6(DN) <> #0 THEN DSPREPA(TP*7+DN,1)="*"
              IF PFDATA7(DN) <> #0 THEN DSPREPA(TP*8+DN,1)="*"
           EXIT
        N02:
        IF TP=16 THEN ENTRY
           IF FK=#2000 AND FK<>#20 THEN ENTRY
              WRITE "   ", DSPREPA(1,TP)," "
           EXIT
           IF FK=#20 THEN ENTRY
              WRITE /," ",FAPAT1,"  :      8|     16|"
              WRITE /,"   ",ASCII(TN,2,5,1," "),"(B):",DSPREPA(1,TP)," "
              WRITE /,"   ",ASCII(TN,2,5,1," "),"(",ASCII(0,2,1,1," "),"):",DSPREPA(TP*1+1,TP)," "
              WRITE /,"   ",ASCII(TN,2,5,1," "),"(",ASCII(1,2,1,1," "),"):",DSPREPA(TP*2+1,TP)," "
              WRITE /,"   ",ASCII(TN,2,5,1," "),"(",ASCII(2,2,1,1," "),"):",DSPREPA(TP*3+1,TP)," "
              WRITE /,"   ",ASCII(TN,2,5,1," "),"(",ASCII(3,2,1,1," "),"):",DSPREPA(TP*4+1,TP)," "
           EXIT
        EXIT
   EXIT

GOTO CONT
;=========================================================================================================================================================
;; NG CHECK
;=========================================================================================================================================================
NGCHK1:

        LOGICAL[2] FDQCNT(VPARA)=#0 ;;
        INTE CNTDQ(VPARA)=#0
        DIM  EDQTST(VPARA)=0MA!VPARA

        TSTDQ=16

        READ FUNC1(DQALL) TO FDQCNT
          DO JJ1 JI=1,TP,1
                 CNTDQ(JI)=0
                 DO WW2 I=0,63,1
                       IF (SL(FDQCNT(JI),I).AND.#80000000)=#80000000 THEN CNTDQ(JI)=CNTDQ(JI)+1
                 WW2:
           JJ1:

DQTST:
        READ CDUT TO CURDUT
        DO EDQCHK DN=1,TP
            EDQTST(DN)=0MA

            FDNUM=(MOD((DN-1)/(TP))/32)*2+(DN-1)/(TP)+1
            RTNUM=DN-32*((DN-1)/32)-1
            IF TP=32 THEN FDNUM=1
           ;IF SR(CURDUT(FDNUM),RTNUM).AND.#01 = #1 THEN ENTRY
            IF SR(CURDUT,RTNUM).AND.#01 = #1 THEN ENTRY
               IF CNTDQ(DN)=TSTDQ  THEN EDQTST(DN)=1MA
            EXIT
        EDQCHK:

        TEST TN
        LIMIT JUDGE = NEGLECT, 0.5MA
        JUDGE EDQTST

        GOSUB FCHK
        GOSUB FBIN(FAFBIN,FASBIN)

GOTO CONT
;=========================================================================================================================================================
;;        OPEN/SHORT TEST ROUTINE
;=========================================================================================================================================================
SHORT1:
    TEST TN
        VDD1=1.8V &  VDD2H=1.05V & VDD2L=1.05V & VDDQ=1.05V & FAVCC2=1.05V
        GOSUB VDOWN
        PINALL = IN1,FIXL

        VSIM=1.10V,R8V,M800UA
        LIMIT=100UA,-25UA

        IF MCNUM=8 THEN MEAS DC(PINALL)
        IF MCNUM=4 THEN MEAS DC(QDPALL)

        IF FK=#10 THEN GOSUB DUTRESLT
        IF FK=#10 THEN ENTRY
           WRITE /,STEP," ",CSN," ","TN=",ASCII(TN,2,5,0," ")," ","                                         ",ASCII(MCNUM,2,1,0," "),"CHIP","   SHORT VSIM     "
           WRITE  ," ",ASCII(AA/1S,1,6,1," "),ASCII(CC/1S,1,6,2," "),"   ",DSPREPA(1,TP)
        EXIT
        SSBIN=114 & GOSUB FCHK & GOSUB FBIN(8,SSBIN)

GOTO CONT
;;--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
SHORT2:
    TEST TN
        VDD1=1.8V &  VDD2H=1.05V & VDD2L=1.05V & VDDQ=1.05V & FAVCC2=1.05V
        GOSUB VDOWN
        PINALL = IN1,FIXL
        
        ISVM=-100UA,R800UA,M(20V),0.60V,-1.4V      ; When local DC unit enable(0.60V) for T5511
        LIMIT=-0.1V,NEGLECT
        IF MCNUM=8 THEN MEAS DC(PINALL)
        IF MCNUM=4 THEN MEAS DC(QDPALL)

        IF FK=#10 THEN GOSUB DUTRESLT
        IF FK=#10 THEN ENTRY
           WRITE /,STEP," ",CSN," ","TN=",ASCII(TN,2,5,0," ")," ","                                         ",ASCII(MCNUM,2,1,0," "),"CHIP","   SHORT ISVM     "
           WRITE  ," ",ASCII(AA/1S,1,6,1," "),ASCII(CC/1S,1,6,2," "),"   ",DSPREPA(1,TP)
        EXIT
        SSBIN=114 & GOSUB FCHK & GOSUB FBIN(8,SSBIN)

GOTO CONT
;;--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
OPENCHK:
    TEST TN
        VDD1=1.8V &  VDD2H=1.05V & VDD2L=1.05V & VDDQ=1.05V & FAVCC2=1.05V
        GOSUB VDOWN
        PINALL=OPEN 

        ISVM=-2MA,R8MA,M(20V),0.60V,-1.4V       ; When local DC unit enable(0.60V) for T5511
        LIMIT=NEGLECT,-1.2V
        IF MCNUM=8 THEN MEAS DC(PINALL)
        IF MCNUM=4 THEN MEAS DC(QDPALL)

        IF FK=#10 THEN GOSUB DUTRESLT
        IF FK=#10 THEN ENTRY
           WRITE /,STEP," ",CSN," ","TN=",ASCII(TN,2,5,0," ")," ","                                         ",ASCII(MCNUM,2,1,0," "),"CHIP","   OPEN CHECK     "
           WRITE  ," ",ASCII(AA/1S,1,6,1," "),ASCII(CC/1S,1,6,2," "),"   ",DSPREPA(1,TP)
        EXIT
        SSBIN=114 & GOSUB FCHK & GOSUB FBIN(8,SSBIN)

GOTO CONT
;;--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
DCHK:
        ARGUMENT(DCSRT,DSBIN,DCVCC,DCFOR,DCIN1,DCINN,DCFMT,DCFMTN,DCRNG,DCHLM,DCLLM,DCWAT,DCTLE)
        FBFMT4(3,1)="S"

        DRG(1)=DCRNG
        DRG(2)=DCHLM*TSTFLG
        DRG(3)=DCLLM*TSTFLG
        DRG(4)=DCVCC

;;--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
        VDD1=1.95V & VDD2=1.12V & VDDQ=0.57V & FAVCC2=1.12V
        FAVCC2=VDD2
        IN1 = FAVCC2 0V
        PINALL = IN1 FIXL
        ;GOSUB (DCIN1) VDOWN,VVOH                     ; INPUT LEVEL
        ;GOSUB  PNLKG                                ; PIN FORMAT

        IF DCFOR = 1  THEN VSIM = DRG(4) R8V  M(DRG(1))
        IF DCFOR = 2  THEN VSIM = 0.00V  R8V  M(DRG(1))
        LIMIT = DRG(2),DRG(3)

        IF DCFOR = 1  THEN  ENTRY & PININ =IN1,FIXL & PINIO  = IN1,FIXL & EXIT  ;CAP,CLKP,CLKBP,DQMP,ODTP,CSP,CKEP,DQSA
        IF DCFOR = 2  THEN  ENTRY & PININ =IN1,FIXH & PINIO  = IN1,FIXH & EXIT

        IF DCWAT = 1MS  THEN ENTRY                 ;IIH/IIL
           PINIO  = IN1,FIXL
           TEST TN
           SRON
             MEAS DC(PININ)
           SROF
        EXIT

        IF DCWAT = 2MS  THEN ENTRY                 ;IOH/IOL
           TEST TN
           SRON
             MEAS DC(PINIO)
           SROF
        EXIT

        IF FK=#10 THEN GOSUB DUTRESLT
        IF FK=#10 THEN ENTRY
           WRITE /,STEP," ",CSN," ","TN=",ASCII(TN,2,5,0," ")," ","                                         ",ASCII(MCNUM,2,1,0," "),"CHIP","   PIN LKG        "
           WRITE  ," ",ASCII(AA/1S,1,6,1," "),ASCII(CC/1S,1,6,2," "),"   ",DSPREPA(1,TP)
        EXIT

        SSBIN = DSBIN
        IF DCSRT<>0 THEN GOSUB FCHK

        GOSUB FBIN(DCSRT,DSBIN)
GOTO CONT


;;--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

NOP:    GOTO CONTINUE

POPEN:  PINALL  = OPEN 
        GOTO CONTINUE
    
VCONTL:
       VDD1    = OPEN
       VDD2H   = OPEN
       VDD2L   = OPEN
       VDDQ    = OPEN
       ISVM    = -100.0UA R(800.0UA) M(-1.500V) 600.0MV -1.500V 
       GOTO CONTINUE

;========================================================================================================================================================================
;        PIN LEVEL START
;========================================================================================================================================================================
VND01:
        ARGUMENT(VND2,VND3)
        FAVCC2  = VND2   ;;by kkk
        VDDS2   = VND2
        VDDS    = VDDS2*1.714
        VDDQS   = VND3

        ODT_A   = 1.2V
        ODT_B   = 1.2V
        VDD1    = VDDS
        VDD2    = VDDS2
        VDDQ    = VDDQS

        ;120Ohm
        VREFCA  = VND2*0.240*8/3
        VREFCMD = VND2*0.240*11/6
        VREFCK  = VND2*0.240*11/6
        VREFDQ  = VND2*0.240*11/6
        VREFDQS = VND2*0.240*17/12

        VSWING_DQ=350MV
        VSWING_CK=350MV
        VSWING_CMD=300MV
        VSWING_CA=300MV

        ;;120Ohm
        VIHCA   = VREFCA+(VSWING_CA*8/3)   ;120ohm 50+(120/4)/30ohm
        VILCA   = VREFCA-(VSWING_CA*8/3)   ;120ohm
        VIHCK   = VREFCK+(VSWING_CK*11/6)
        VILCK   = VREFCK-(VSWING_CK*11/6)
        VIHCMD  = VREFCMD+(VSWING_CMD*11/6)
        VILCMD  = VREFCMD-(VSWING_CMD*11/6)
        VIHDQ   = VREFDQ+(VSWING_DQ*8/3)
        VILDQ   = VREFDQ-(VSWING_DQ*8/3)
        VIHDQS  = VREFDQS+(VSWING_DQ*11/6)
        VILDQS  = VREFDQS-(VSWING_DQ*11/6)
        VIHDMI  = VREFDQS+(VSWING_DQ*11/6)  ;120ohm (50+120)/120ohm
        VILDMI  = VREFDQS-(VSWING_DQ*11/6)  ;120ohm

        VILCK   = 0V ;
        VILCA   = 0V ;
        VILCMD  = 0V
        VILDQS  = 0V
        VILDMI  = 0V
        VILDQ   = 0V ;

        VOUTH   = (VND3*0.16)+0.055V ; shared DQ VOH+60mV
        VOUTL   = (VND3*0.16)-0.01V ; shared DQ VOL-10mV
       IF TN=1234 OR TN=6234 THEN ENTRY
        VOUTH   = (VND3*0.16)+0.200V ; shared DQ VOH+60mV
        VOUTL   = (VND3*0.16)+0.135V ; shared DQ VOL-10mV
       EXIT
       IF FATLE1(1,3)="ATM" OR FATLE1(1,3)="MRR" THEN ENTRY
        VOUTH   = (VND3*0.14);+0.055V ; shared DQ VOH+60mV
        VOUTL   = (VND3*0.14);-0.01V ; shared DQ VOL-10mV
       EXIT
        
        VOUTH2  = (VND3*0.14)        ; no-shared DMI
        VOUTL2  = (VND3*0.14)        ; no-shared DMI
        VDT1    = 0V

        IF VIHCA>1.6V THEN VIHCA = 1.6V
        IF VIHDQ>1.6V THEN VIHDQ = 1.6V

        IN1     = 1.1V            -100MV         ; DQS
        IN2     = VND2+200MV      -100MV         ; CKE
        IN3     = 1.3V            -200MV         ; DQ
       IF FATLE1(1,3)="PCP" THEN ENTRY
        IN3     = 1.0V            200MV          ; DQ
       EXIT
        IN4     = 1.1V            -200MV         ; CS, RST
        IN5     = 1.3V            -250MV         ; CA
        IN6     = 1.0V            0V             ; DMI
        IN15    = VIHCK            VILCK         ; CK

        OUT1    = VOUTH           VOUTL
        OUT2    = VOUTH2          VOUTL2
        VT1     = VDT1

GOTO CONT

VND02:
        VDD1=FAVCC2*1.714
        VDD2=FAVCC2
        VDDQ=FAVCC2*0.47*0.47
        ODT_A=1.2V    ; for T5511
        ODT_B=1.2V    ; for T5511

      IF ODQFLG=0 THEN ENTRY
         VREFCA=FAVCC2*0.200*11/6
         VREFDQ=FAVCC2*0.200*11/6

         VSWING_DQ=300MV
         VSWING_CA=300MV
         VSWING_CK=300MV
         VSWING_CMD=300MV

         VIHCA   = VREFCA+(VSWING_CA*11/6)
         VILCA   = VREFCA-(VSWING_CA*11/6)
         VIHDQ   = VREFDQ+(VSWING_DQ*11/6)
         VILDQ   = VREFDQ-(VSWING_DQ*11/6)
         VIHCK   = VREFCA+(VSWING_CK*11/6)
         VILCK   = VREFCA-(VSWING_CK*11/6)
         VIHCMD  = VREFCA+(VSWING_CMD*11/6)
         VILCMD  = VREFCA-(VSWING_CMD*11/6)


         VILCK   = 0V ;VREFCA-(VSWING_CK*11/6)
         VILCMD  = 0V
         VILDQ   = 0V ;VREFDQ-(VSWING_DQ*11/6)

         VOUTH   = FAVCC2*0.14
         VOUTL   = FAVCC2*0.14
         VDT1    = 0V

         IN1     = VIHCK           VILCK          ; CK ,DQS
         ;IN2     = VIHCMD          VILCMD        ;
         IN2     = FAVCC2*0.75     -100MV         ; CKE
         IN3     = VIHDQ           VILDQ          ; DQ
         IN4     = VIHCMD          VILCMD         ; CA, CS, RST, DMI
         IN5     = VIHCMD          VILCMD         ; CA, CS, RST, DMI
         IN6     = VIHCMD          VILCMD         ; CAODT

         IN15    = VIHCK           VILCK          ; CK ,DQS

         OUT1    = VOUTH           VOUTL
         OUT2    = VOUTH           VOUTL
         VT1     = VDT1

         ;PCON = VS1, VS2, VS3
      EXIT

      IF ODQFLG=1 THEN ENTRY
        VREFCA  = FAVCC2*0.200*8/3  
        VREFCMD = FAVCC2*0.200*11/6 
        VREFCK  = FAVCC2*0.200*11/6 
        VREFDQ  = FAVCC2*0.200*11/6 
        VREFDQS = FAVCC2*0.200*11/6  

        VSWING_DQ=300MV
        VSWING_CK=350MV
        VSWING_CMD=300MV

        IF FAVCC2>=1.1V  THEN VSWING_CA=300MV
        IF FAVCC2<1.1V THEN VSWING_CA=200MV

        VIHCA   = VREFCA+(VSWING_CA*8/3)   ;120ohm 50+(120/4)/30ohm
        VILCA   = VREFCA-(VSWING_CA*8/3)   ;120ohm     VIHCK    = VREFCK+(VSWING_CK*11/6)
        VILCK    = VREFCK-(VSWING_CK*11/6)  
        VIHCMD    = VREFCMD+(VSWING_CMD*11/6)
        VILCMD    = VREFCMD-(VSWING_CMD*11/6)    
        VIHDQ    = VREFDQ+(VSWING_DQ*11/6)   
        VILDQ    = VREFDQ-(VSWING_DQ*11/6)
        VIHDQS  = VREFDQS+(VSWING_DQ*11/6) 
        VILDQS  = VREFDQS-(VSWING_DQ*11/6) 
        VIHDMI  = VREFDQS+(VSWING_DQ*11/6)   ;120ohm (50+120)/120ohm
        VILDMI  = VREFDQS-(VSWING_DQ*11/6)   ;120ohm
        VILCK    = 0V ;    
        VILCA    = 0V ;    
        VILCMD    = 0V         
        VILDQS    = 0V         
        VILDMI    = 0V        
        VILDQ    = 0V ;

        VOUTH   = (FAVCC2*0.14)+60MV   ; shared DQ VOH+60mV
        VOUTL   = (FAVCC2*0.14)-10MV   ; shared DQ VOL-10mV
        VOUTH2  = (FAVCC2*0.14)        ; no-shared DMI 
        VOUTL2  = (FAVCC2*0.14)        ; no-shared DMI 
        VDT1    = 0V

        IF FAVCC2>=1.17V                 THEN VIHCA=1.6V
        IF FAVCC2<1.17V AND FAVCC2>=1.1V THEN VIHCA=1.35V

        IF VIHCA>1.6V THEN VIHCA = 1.6V

        IN1     = VIHDQS          VILDQS         ; DQS
        IN2     = FAVCC2+200MV    -100MV         ; CKE
        IN3     = VIHDQ           VILDQ          ; DQ, DMI
        IN4     = VIHCMD          VILCMD         ; CS, RST
        IN5     = VIHCA           VILCA          ; CA  ;CA4daisy  
        IN6     = VIHCMD          VILCMD         ; CAODT
        IN7     = VIHDQS          VILDQS         ; DQS

        IN15    = VIHCK            VILCK         ; FOB CKP level   

        OUT1    = VOUTH           VOUTL
        OUT2    = VOUTH2          VOUTL2
        VT1     = VDT1

        ;PCON = VS1, VS2, VS3             ; PPS cap connect
EXIT

        GOTO CONTINUE

         VOUTL   = FAVCC2*0.14
         VDT1    = 0V

         IN1     = VIHCK           VILCK          ; CK ,DQS
         ;IN2     = VIHCMD          VILCMD        ;

         IN4     = VIHCMD          VILCMD         ; CA, CS, RST, DMI
         IN5     = VIHCMD          VILCMD         ; CA, CS, RST, DMI
         IN6     = VIHCMD          VILCMD         ; CAODT

        VREFCA  = FAVCC2*0.240*8/3
        VREFCMD = FAVCC2*0.240*11/6
        VREFCK  = FAVCC2*0.240*11/6
        VREFDQ  = FAVCC2*0.240*11/6
        VREFDQS = FAVCC2*0.240*17/12

  IF ODTFLG=0 THEN ENTRY
        VSWING_DQ=350MV
  EXIT
  ELSE ENTRY
        IF FAVCC2>1.20V THEN ENTRY
        VSWING_DQ=350MV
        EXIT
        ELSE ENTRY
        VSWING_DQ=300MV
        EXIT
  EXIT

        VSWING_CK=350MV
        VSWING_CMD=300MV
        VSWING_CA=300MV

        VIHCA   = VREFCA+(VSWING_CA*8/3)   ;120ohm 50+(120/4)/30ohm
        VILCA   = VREFCA-(VSWING_CA*8/3)   ;120ohm
        VIHCK   = VREFCK+(VSWING_CK*11/6)
        VILCK   = VREFCK-(VSWING_CK*11/6)
        VIHCMD  = VREFCMD+(VSWING_CMD*11/6)
        VILCMD  = VREFCMD-(VSWING_CMD*11/6)
        VIHDQ   = VREFDQ+(VSWING_DQ*11/6)
        VILDQ   = VREFDQ-(VSWING_DQ*11/6)
        VIHDQS  = VREFDQS+(VSWING_DQ*17/12)
        VILDQS  = VREFDQS-(VSWING_DQ*17/12)
        VIHDMI  = VREFDQS+(VSWING_DQ*17/12)  ;120ohm (50+120)/120ohm
        VILDMI  = VREFDQS-(VSWING_DQ*17/12)  ;120ohm

        VILCK   = 0V ;
        VILCA   = 0V ;
        VILCMD  = 0V
        VILDQS  = 0V
        VILDMI  = 0V
        VILDQ   = 0V ;

        VOUTH   = (FAVCC2*0.19)+60MV   ; shared DQ VOH+60mV
        VOUTL   = (FAVCC2*0.19)-10MV   ; shared DQ VOL-10mV
        VOUTH2  = (FAVCC2*0.14)        ; no-shared DMI 
        VOUTL2  = (FAVCC2*0.14)        ; no-shared DMI 
        VDT1    = 0V

        IF VIHCA>1.6V THEN VIHCA = 1.6V


        IN1     = VIHDQS          VILDQS         ; DQS
       ;IN2     = VIHCMD          VILCMD        ;
        IN2     = FAVCC2+200MV    -100MV         ; CKE
        IN3     = VIHDQ           VILDQ          ; DQ, DMI
        IN4     = VIHCMD          VILCMD         ; CS, RST
        IN5     = VIHCA           VILCA          ; CA  ;CA4daisy
        IN6     = VIHCMD          VILCMD         ; CAODT

        IN15    = VIHCK            VILCK         ; FOB CKP level

        OUT1    = VOUTH           VOUTL
        OUT2    = VOUTH2          VOUTL2
        VT1     = VDT1

        ;PCON = VS1, VS2, VS3             ; PPS cap connect
EXIT

        GOTO CONTINUE

        VSWING_CA=300MV
        IF FAVCC2>1.1V  THEN VSWING_CA=300MV
        IF FAVCC2<=1.1V THEN VSWING_CA=200MV

        VIHCA   = VREFCA+(VSWING_CA*8/3)   ;120ohm 50+(120/4)/30ohm
        VILCA   = VREFCA-(VSWING_CA*8/3)   ;120ohm     
        VIHCK    = VREFCK+(VSWING_CK*11/6)
        VILCK    = VREFCK-(VSWING_CK*11/6)    
        VIHCMD    = VREFCMD+(VSWING_CMD*11/6)
        VILCMD    = VREFCMD-(VSWING_CMD*11/6)    
        VIHDQ    = VREFDQ+(VSWING_DQ*11/6)    
        VILDQ    = VREFDQ-(VSWING_DQ*11/6)
        VIHDQS  = VREFDQS+(VSWING_DQ*17/12)
        VILDQS  = VREFDQS-(VSWING_DQ*17/12)
        VIHDMI  = VREFDQS+(VSWING_DQ*17/12)  ;120ohm (50+120)/120ohm
        VILDMI  = VREFDQS-(VSWING_DQ*17/12)  ;120ohm
        VILCK    = 0V ;    
        VILCA    = 0V ;    
        VILCMD    = 0V         
        VILDQS    = 0V         
        VILDMI    = 0V         
        VILDQ    = 0V ;

        VOUTH   = (FAVCC2*0.11)        ; shared DQ VOH+60mV
        VOUTL   = (FAVCC2*0.11)        ; shared DQ VOL-10mV
        VOUTH2  = (FAVCC2*0.11)        ; no-shared DMI 
        VOUTL2  = (FAVCC2*0.11)        ; no-shared DMI 
        VDT1    = 0V

        IF FAVCC2>=1.20V                 THEN VIHCA=1.6V
        IF FAVCC2<1.20V AND FAVCC2>=1.1V THEN VIHCA=1.35V
        IF VIHCA>1.6V THEN VIHCA = 1.6V

        IN1     = VIHDQS          VILDQS         ; DQS
       ;IN2     = VIHCMD          VILCMD        ;
        IN2     = FAVCC2+200MV    -100MV         ; CKE
        IN3     = VIHDQ           VILDQ          ; DQ, DMI
        IN4     = VIHCMD          VILCMD         ; CS, RST
        IN5     = VIHCA           VILCA          ; CA  ;CA4daisy  
        IN6     = VIHCMD          VILCMD         ; CAODT

        IN15    = VIHCK            VILCK         ; FOB CKP level   

        OUT1    = VOUTH           VOUTL
        OUT2    = VOUTH2          VOUTL2
        VT1     = VDT1

        ;PCON = VS1, VS2, VS3             ; PPS cap connect
     EXIT

        GOTO CONTINUE

VND07:
        GOTO CONTINUE
VND08:
        GOTO CONTINUE
VND09:
        GOTO CONTINUE

        VREFCK  = ICVCC2*0.240*11/6

        VSWING_CK=350MV

        VIHCK    = VREFCK+(VSWING_CK*11/6)
        VILCK    = VREFCK-(VSWING_CK*11/6)   
        VIHCMD    = VREFCMD+(VSWING_CMD*11/6)
        VILCMD    = VREFCMD-(VSWING_CMD*11/6)    
        VIHDQ    = VREFDQ+(VSWING_DQ*11/6)    
        VILDQ    = VREFDQ-(VSWING_DQ*11/6)
        VIHDQS  = VREFDQS+(VSWING_DQ*17/12)
        VILDQS  = VREFDQS-(VSWING_DQ*17/12)
        VIHDMI  = VREFDQS+(VSWING_DQ*17/12)  ;120ohm (50+120)/120ohm
        VILDMI  = VREFDQS-(VSWING_DQ*17/12)  ;120ohm
        VILCK    = 0V ;    
        VILCA    = 0V ;    
        VILCMD    = 0V         
        VILDQS    = 0V         
        VILDMI    = 0V         
        VILDQ    = 0V ;

        VOUTH   = (ICVCC2*0.19)+60MV   ; shared DQ VOH+60mV
        VOUTL   = (ICVCC2*0.19)-10MV   ; shared DQ VOL-10mV
        VOUTH2  = (ICVCC2*0.14)        ; no-shared DMI 
        VOUTL2  = (ICVCC2*0.14)        ; no-shared DMI

       ;IN2     = VIHCMD          VILCMD        ;
