        IN4     = VIHCMD          VILCMD         ; CS, RST
        IN5     = VIHCA           VILCA          ; CA  ;CA4daisy  
        IN6     = VIHCMD          VILCMD         ; CAODT

        IN15    = VIHCK            VILCK         ; FOB CKP level   

        OUT1    = VOUTH           VOUTL
        OUT2    = VOUTH2          VOUTL2

        ;PCON = VS1, VS2, VS3             ; PPS cap connect
GOTO CONT

VNS01:                                ;G.FUN /CELL & CORE

        VDD1   = FAVCC1     ;VDD1
        VDD2H  = FAVCC2     ;VDD2
        VDD2L  = FAVCC2     ;VDD2L
        VDDQ   = FAVCCQ     ;VDDQ


        VREFF  = FAVCCQ*0.5           ;??
        IN1    = FAVCC2*1.0, 0V    ;CK     
        IN2    = FAVCC2*1.0, 0V    ;CS 
        IN3    = FAVCC2*1.0, 0V    ;DQ
        IN4    = FAVCC2*1.0, 0V    ;CA
        IN5    = FAVCC2*1.0, 0V    ;DM
        IN6    = FAVCC2*1.0, 0V    ;   
        IN7    = FAVCC2*1.0, 0V    ;RDQS
        IN8    = FAVCC2*1.0, 0V    ;WCK 
        IN9    = FAVCC2*1.0, 0V    ;RESET

        OUT1  = VREFF+0.025V, VREFF-0.025V
        OUT2  = VREFF+0.025V, VREFF-0.025V
        OUT3  = VREFF+0.025V, VREFF-0.025V

        VT1   = VREFF
        VT2   = VREFF
        VT3   = VREFF

;       PCON  = 0 ;VD1 VD2
;       VCON  = 0

        GOTO CONT

        VILDQS  = VREFDQS-(VSWING_DQ*11/6);17/12)
        VIHDMI  = VREFDQS+(VSWING_DQ*11/6);17/12)  ;120ohm (50+120)/120ohm

        VOUTL   = (ICVCC3*0.14)-10MV   ; shared DQ VOL-10mV

        IN1     = 1.4V -0.0V ;VIHDQS          VILDQS         ; DQS
       ;IN2     = VIHCMD          VILCMD        ;
        IN2     = 1.4V -0.1V ;ICVCC3+200MV    -100MV         ; CKE
        IN3     = 1.4V -0.0V ; VIHDQ           VILDQ          ; DQ, DMI
        IN4     = VIHCMD          VILCMD         ; CS, RST
        IN5     = 1.4V -0.0V ;VIHCA           VILCA          ; CA  ;CA4daisy
        IN6     = 1.4V 0.0V ;VIHCMD          VILCMD         ; CAODT

        IN15    = 1.4V 0.0V ;VIHCK            VILCK         ; FOB CKP level

        OUT1    = VOUTH           VOUTL
        OUT2    = VOUTH2          VOUTL2
        VT1     = VDT1

        ;PCON = VS1, VS2, VS3             ; PPS cap connect
GOTO CONT


VTRAIN:
        ARGUMENT(VTR2,VTR3)
        FAVCC2  = VTR2   ;;by kkk
        VDDS2   = VTR2
        VDDS    = VDDS2*1.714
        VDDQS   = VTR3

        ODT_A   = 1.2V
        ODT_B   = 1.2V
        VDD1    = VDDS
        VDD2    = VDDS2
        VDDQ    = VDDQS
    IF VGAPFLG=1 THEN ENTRY
        IF FAVCC2>1.20V THEN VDDQ=1.20V
    EXIT

IF ODQFLG=0 THEN ENTRY
        VREFCA=VDDS2*0.28*11/6
        VREFDQ=VDDQS*0.28*11/6

        VSWING_DQ=300MV
        VSWING_CA=300MV
        VSWING_CK=300MV
        VSWING_CMD=300MV
 
        VIHCA   = VREFCA+(VSWING_CA*11/6)
        VILCA   = VREFCA-(VSWING_CA*11/6)
        VIHDQ   = VREFDQ+(VSWING_DQ*11/6)
        VILDQ   = VREFDQ-(VSWING_DQ*11/6)
        VIHCK   = VREFCA+(VSWING_CK*7/6)
        VILCK   = 0V ;VREFCA-(VSWING_CK*11/6)

        VIHCMD  = VREFCA+(VSWING_CMD*11/6)
        VILCMD  = VREFCA-(VSWING_CMD*11/6)

        VILCK   = 0V ;VREFCA-(VSWING_CK*11/6)
        VILCMD  = -50MV
        VILDQ   = 0V ;VREFDQ-(VSWING_DQ*11/6)

        VOUTH   = VDDQS*0.14
        VOUTL   = VDDQS*0.14
        VDT1    = 0V

        IN1     = VIHDQ           VILDQ          ; DQ
        IN2     = FAVCC2*0.85     -100MV         ; CKE
        IN3     = VIHDQ           VILDQ          ; DQ
        IN4     = VIHCMD          VILCMD         ; CA, CS, RST, DMI
        IN5     = VIHCMD          VILCMD         ; CA, CS, RST, DMI
        IN6     = VIHCMD          VILCMD         ; CAODT

        IN15    = VIHCK           VILCK          ; CK ,DQS

        OUT1    = VOUTH           VOUTL
        OUT2    = VOUTH           VOUTL
        VT1     = VDT1
EXIT

IF ODQFLG=1 THEN ENTRY
        ;120Ohm
        VREFCA  = VTR2*0.240*8/3
        VREFCMD = VTR2*0.240*11/6
        VREFCK  = VTR2*0.240*11/6
        VREFDQ  = VTR2*0.240*11/6
        VREFDQS = VTR2*0.240*17/12

        VSWING_DQ=350MV
        VSWING_CK=350MV
        VSWING_CMD=300MV
        VSWING_CA=300MV

        ;;120Ohm
        VIHCA   = VREFCA+(VSWING_CA*8/3)   ;120ohm 50+(120/4)/30ohm
        VILCA   = VREFCA-(VSWING_CA*8/3)   ;120ohm
        VIHCK   = VREFCK+(VSWING_CK*11/6)
        VILCK   = VREFCK-(VSWING_CK*11/6)
        VIHCMD  = VREFCMD+(VSWING_CMD*11/6)
        VILCMD  = VREFCMD-(VSWING_CMD*11/6)
        VIHDQ   = VREFDQ+(VSWING_DQ*8/3)
        VILDQ   = VREFDQ-(VSWING_DQ*8/3)
        VIHDQS  = VREFDQS+(VSWING_DQ*11/6)
        VILDQS  = VREFDQS-(VSWING_DQ*11/6)
        VIHDMI  = VREFDQS+(VSWING_DQ*11/6)  ;120ohm (50+120)/120ohm
        VILDMI  = VREFDQS-(VSWING_DQ*11/6)  ;120ohm

        VILCK   = 0V ;
        VILCA   = 0V ;
        VILCMD  = 0V
        VILDQS  = 0V
        VILDMI  = 0V
        VILDQ   = 0V ;

        VOUTH   = (VTR3*0.16) ;+0.055V ; shared DQ VOH+60mV
        VOUTL   = (VTR3*0.16) ;-0.01V ; shared DQ VOL-10mV
        VOUTH2  = (VTR3*0.14)        ; no-shared DMI
        VOUTL2  = (VTR3*0.14)        ; no-shared DMI
        VDT1    = 0V

        IF VIHCA>1.6V THEN VIHCA = 1.6V
        IF VIHDQ>1.6V THEN VIHDQ = 1.6V

        IN1     = 1.0V            0V             ; DQS
        IN2     = FAVCC2+200MV    -100MV         ; CKE
        IN3     = 1.3V            VILDQ          ; DQ
        IN4     = 1.2V            0V             ; CS, RST
        IN5     = 1.0V            -300MV         ; CA
        IN15    = VIHCK            VILCK         ; FOB CKP level

        OUT1    = VOUTH           VOUTL
        OUT2    = VOUTH2          VOUTL2
        VT1     = VDT1
EXIT
        GOTO CONT

VTRAINL:
        FAVCC2  = LP5VD2   ;;by kkk    
        VDDS2   = LP5VD2    
        VDDS    = VDDS2*1.714    
        VDDQS   = VDDS2  
        VDD1    = VDDS    
        VDD2    = VDDS2    
        VDDQ    = VDDQS
        ODT_A=1.2V    ; for T5511
        ODT_B=1.2V    ; for T5511

     IF ODQFLG=0 THEN ENTRY
        VREFCA=VDDS2*0.20*11/6
        VREFDQ=VDDQS*0.20*11/6

        VSWING_DQ=300MV
        VSWING_CA=300MV
        VSWING_CK=300MV
        VSWING_CMD=300MV

        VIHCA   = VREFCA+(VSWING_CA*11/6)
        VILCA   = VREFCA-(VSWING_CA*11/6)
        VIHDQ   = VREFDQ+(VSWING_DQ*11/6)
        VILDQ   = VREFDQ-(VSWING_DQ*11/6)
        VIHCK   = VREFCA+(VSWING_CK*11/6)
        VILCK   = VREFCA-(VSWING_CK*11/6)
        VIHCMD  = VREFCA+(VSWING_CMD*11/6)
        VILCMD  = VREFCA-(VSWING_CMD*11/6)

        VILCK   = 0V ;VREFCA-(VSWING_CK*11/6)
        VILCMD  = 0V
        VILDQ   = 0V ;VREFDQ-(VSWING_DQ*11/6)

        VOUTH   = VDDS2*0.14
        VOUTL   = VDDS2*0.14
        VDT1    = 0V

        IN1     = VIHCK           VILCK          ; CK ,DQS
       ;IN2     = VIHCMD          VILCMD         ; CA, CS, RST, DMI
        IN2     = FAVCC2*0.75     -100MV         ; CKE
        IN3     = VIHDQ           VILDQ          ; DQ
        IN4     = VIHCMD          VILCMD         ; CA, CS, RST, DMI
        IN5     = VIHCMD          VILCMD         ; CA, CS, RST, DMI
        IN6     = VIHCMD          VILCMD         ; CAODT

        IN15    = VIHCK           VILCK          ; CK ,DQS

        OUT1    = VOUTH           VOUTL
        OUT2    = VOUTH           VOUTL
        VT1     = VDT1

        ;PCON = VS1, VS2, VS3
     EXIT

     IF ODQFLG=1 THEN ENTRY
        ;120Ohm
        VREFCA  = LP5VD2*0.200*8/3  
        VREFCMD = LP5VD2*0.200*11/6 
        VREFCK  = LP5VD2*0.200*11/6 
        VREFDQ  = LP5VD2*0.240*11/6 
        VREFDQS = LP5VD2*0.240*11/6 

        VSWING_DQ=300MV
       ;VSWING_DQ=300MV
        VSWING_CK=350MV
        VSWING_CMD=300MV
        VSWING_CA=300MV

        ;;120Ohm
        VIHCA   = VREFCA+(VSWING_CA*8/3)   ;120ohm 50+(120/4)/30ohm
        VILCA   = VREFCA-(VSWING_CA*8/3)   ;120ohm     
        VIHCK    = VREFCK+(VSWING_CK*11/6)
        VILCK    = VREFCK-(VSWING_CK*11/6)    
        VIHCMD    = VREFCMD+(VSWING_CMD*11/6)
        VILCMD    = VREFCMD-(VSWING_CMD*11/6)    
        VIHDQ    = VREFDQ+(VSWING_DQ*11/6)    
        VILDQ    = VREFDQ-(VSWING_DQ*11/6)
        VIHDQS  = VREFDQS+(VSWING_DQ*11/6)
        VILDQS  = VREFDQS-(VSWING_DQ*11/6)
        VIHDMI  = VREFDQS+(VSWING_DQ*11/6)  ;120ohm (50+120)/120ohm
        VILDMI  = VREFDQS-(VSWING_DQ*11/6)  ;120ohm
        VILCK    = 0V ;    
        VILCA    = 0V ;    
        VILCMD    = 0V         
        VILDQS    = 0V         
        VILDMI    = 0V         
        VILDQ    = 0V ;

        IF FAVCC2>=1.17V THEN ENTRY
           VIHCA  = 1.6V       
           VIHDQ  = 1.6V            
           VIHDQS = 1.6V     
        EXIT
        IF FAVCC2>1.20V THEN ENTRY
           VOUTH   = (LP5VD2*0.18)+0.035V ; shared DQ VOH+60mV
           VOUTL   = (LP5VD2*0.18)-0.01V  ; shared DQ VOL-10mV
           VOUTH2  = (LP5VD2*0.18)        ; no-shared DMI 
           VOUTL2  = (LP5VD2*0.18)        ; no-shared DMI 
        VDT1    = 0V
        EXIT
        IF FAVCC2<=1.20V THEN ENTRY
           VOUTH   = (LP5VD2*0.18)+0.035V ; shared DQ VOH+60mV
           VOUTL   = (LP5VD2*0.18)-0.01V  ; shared DQ VOL-10mV
           VOUTH2  = (LP5VD2*0.18)        ; no-shared DMI 
           VOUTL2  = (LP5VD2*0.18)        ; no-shared DMI 
        VDT1    = 0V
        EXIT
        IF VIHCA>1.6V THEN VIHCA = 1.6V
 
        IN1     = VIHDQS          VILDQS         ; DQS,DMI
        IN2     = FAVCC2+200MV    -100MV         ; CKE      
        IN3     = VIHDQ           VILDQ          ; DQ    
        IN4     = VIHCMD          VILCMD         ; CS, RST      

    IF VGAPFLG<>1 THEN ENTRY
        IN5     = VIHCA           VILCA          ; CA  ;CA4daisy  
    EXIT
    ELSE ENTRY
        IF FAVCC2>1.20V THEN ENTRY
        IN5     = 1.6V            0MV         ; CA  ;CA4daisy
        EXIT
        ELSE ENTRY
        IN5     = 1.5V            -100MV         ; CA  ;CA4daisy
        EXIT
    EXIT
        IN6     = VIHCMD          VILCMD         ; CAODT
        IN15    = VIHCK            VILCK         ; FOB CKP level   
        OUT1    = VOUTH           VOUTL           
        OUT2    = VOUTH2          VOUTL2    
        VT1     = VDT1                                
        ;PCON = VS1, VS2, VS3             ; PPS cap connect
EXIT    
GOTO CONT

        IN5     = VIHCMD          VILCMD         ; CA, CS, RST, DMI
        IN6     = VIHCMD          VILCMD         ; CAODT

        IN15    = VIHCK           VILCK          ; CK ,DQS

        OUT1    = VOUTH           VOUTL
        OUT2    = VOUTH           VOUTL
        VT1     = VDT1

        ;PCON = VS1, VS2, VS3
     EXIT

     IF ODQFLG=1 THEN ENTRY
        ;120Ohm
        VREFCA  = LP5VD2*0.200*8/3  
        VREFCMD = LP5VD2*0.200*11/6 
        VREFCK  = LP5VD2*0.200*11/6 
        VREFDQ  = LP5VD2*0.240*11/6 
        VREFDQS = LP5VD2*0.240*11/6 

        VSWING_DQ=300MV
       ;VSWING_DQ=300MV
        VSWING_CK=350MV
        VSWING_CMD=300MV
        VSWING_CA=300MV

        ;;120Ohm
        VIHCA   = VREFCA+(VSWING_CA*8/3)   ;120ohm 50+(120/4)/30ohm
        VILCA   = VREFCA-(VSWING_CA*8/3)   ;120ohm     
        VIHCK    = VREFCK+(VSWING_CK*11/6)
        VILCK    = VREFCK-(VSWING_CK*11/6)    
        VIHCMD    = VREFCMD+(VSWING_CMD*11/6)
        VILCMD    = VREFCMD-(VSWING_CMD*11/6)    
        VIHDQ    = VREFDQ+(VSWING_DQ*11/6)    
        VILDQ    = VREFDQ-(VSWING_DQ*11/6)
        VIHDQS  = VREFDQS+(VSWING_DQ*11/6)
        VILDQS  = VREFDQS-(VSWING_DQ*11/6)
        VIHDMI  = VREFDQS+(VSWING_DQ*11/6)  ;120ohm (50+120)/120ohm
        VILDMI  = VREFDQS-(VSWING_DQ*11/6)  ;120ohm
        VILCK    = 0V ;    
        VILCA    = 0V ;            
        VILCMD    = 0V         
        VILDQS    = 0V         
        VILDMI    = 0V         
        VILDQ    = 0V ;

        IF FAVCC2>1.20V THEN ENTRY
           VIHCA  = 1.6V       
           VIHDQ  = 1.6V            
           VIHDQS = 1.6V     
        EXIT
        IF FAVCC2>1.20V THEN ENTRY
           VOUTH   = (LP5VD2*0.18)+0.035V ; shared DQ VOH+60mV
           VOUTL   = (LP5VD2*0.18)-0.01V  ; shared DQ VOL-10mV
           VOUTH2  = (LP5VD2*0.18)        ; no-shared DMI 
           VOUTL2  = (LP5VD2*0.18)        ; no-shared DMI 
        VDT1    = 0V
        EXIT
        IF FAVCC2<=1.20V THEN ENTRY
           VOUTH   = (LP5VD2*0.18)+0.035V ; shared DQ VOH+60mV
           VOUTL   = (LP5VD2*0.18)-0.01V  ; shared DQ VOL-10mV
           VOUTH2  = (LP5VD2*0.18)        ; no-shared DMI 
           VOUTL2  = (LP5VD2*0.18)        ; no-shared DMI 
        VDT1    = 0V
        EXIT
        IF VIHCA>1.6V THEN VIHCA = 1.6V

        IN1     = VIHDQS          VILDQS         ; DQS,DMI
        IN2     = FAVCC2+200MV    -100MV         ; CKE      
        IN3     = VIHDQ           VILDQ          ; DQ    
        IN4     = VIHCMD          VILCMD         ; CS, RST      

    IF VGAPFLG<>1 THEN ENTRY
        IN5     = VIHCA           VILCA          ; CA  ;CA4daisy  
    EXIT
    ELSE ENTRY
        IF FAVCC2>1.20V THEN ENTRY
        IN5     = 1.6V            0MV         ; CA  ;CA4daisy
        EXIT
        ELSE ENTRY
        IN5     = 1.5V            -100MV         ; CA  ;CA4daisy
        EXIT
    EXIT
        IN6     = VIHCMD          VILCMD         ; CAODT
        IN15    = VIHCK            VILCK         ; FOB CKP level   
        OUT1    = VOUTH           VOUTL           
        OUT2    = VOUTH2          VOUTL2    
        VT1     = VDT1                                
        ;PCON = VS1, VS2, VS3             ; PPS cap connect
EXIT    
GOTO CONT

;========================================================================================================================================================================
;        PIN LEVEL END  
;========================================================================================================================================================================


    

;========================================================================================================================================================================
;        PIN FORMAT START
;========================================================================================================================================================================

       CURIOFMT="IOFTRA"
       CURDMFMT="DMITRA"
       CURRL=RL

        RDQSBP= IN11,  DNRZ,  BCLK11, CCLK11,IOC, OUTL3, VT1, DRE2, DRENRZ, DRCYCDLY(WL),EXPCYCDLY(RL),CPECYCDLY(RL),[STRB3,CPE3], EXPA1, [STRB131,CPE4], EXPB129, EINV1, EINV129 ,CYP1, C17C18DATA ; <C17,C18>x16

    EXIT
   EXIT

        RDQSBP= IN11,  DNRZ,  BCLK11, CCLK11,IOC, OUTL3, VT1, DRE2, DRENRZ, DRCYCDLY(WL),EXPCYCDLY(RL),CPECYCDLY(RL),[STRB3,CPE3], EXPA1, [STRB131,CPE4], EXPB129, EINV1, EINV129 ,CYP1, C17C18DATA ; <C17,C18>x16      
        CURDSFMT="RQSNOR"
    EXIT
   EXIT

    RDQS0CD= IN11,  DNRZ,  BCLK11, CCLK11,IOC, OUTL3, VT1, DRE2, DRENRZ, DRCYCDLY(WL),EXPCYCDLY(RL),CPECYCDLY(RL),                                                             ,CYP1, C17C18DATA ; <C17,C18>x16      
    RDQS1CD= IN11,  DNRZ,  BCLK11, CCLK11,IOC, OUTL3, VT1, DRE2, DRENRZ, DRCYCDLY(WL),EXPCYCDLY(RL),CPECYCDLY(RL),                                                             ,CYP1, C17C18DATA ; <C17,C18>x16

   IF FAPATN(7,7)="LEC5N5C" OR FAPATN(7,7)="LEC5N5D" OR FAPATN(7,7)="LEC4N2C" OR FAPATN(7,7)="LEC4N2D" THEN ENTRY

         UDMIP = IN10,  DNRZ,  BCLK10, CCLK10,IOC, OUTL1, VT1, DRE2, DRENRZ, DRCYCDLY(WL),EXPCYCDLY(RL),CPECYCDLY(RL),[STRB1,CPE3], EXPA1, [STRB129,CPE4], EXPB129, CYP1, C19C20DATA ; <C21,C22>x16
       CURIOFMT="DMILE2"
       CURRL=RL
    EXIT



GOTO CONT
    
FMD00:  
FH00DS:                 ; 4Bank/4Bank Group, 16Bank BA Address                                            
;       ALLPIN=OPEN
 ;      WL=0 & RL=0

        CLKP  = IN1    NRZB   BCLK1   CCLK1  CYP1   <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14>
        CLKBP = IN1   /NRZB   BCLK1   CCLK1  CYP1   <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14>

        WCKP  = IN8    DNRZ   BCLK8   CCLK8  CYP1   <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28>
        WCKBP = IN8   /DNRZ   BCLK8   CCLK8  CYP1   <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28>
;       IF TSPEED=500 THEN ENTRY   ; FOR SINGLE ENDED
;           WCKBP = IN8   /DNRZ   BCLK8   CCLK8  CYP1   <C24,C25> <C24,C25> <C24,C25> <C24,C25> <C24,C25> <C24,C25> <C24,C25> <C24,C25> <C24,C25> <C24,C25> <C24,C25> <C24,C25> <C24,C25> <C24,C25> <C24,C25> <C24,C25>
;       EXIT

        RST   = IN4   /NRZB   BCLK4   CCLK4  CYP1   <C10> <C10> <C10> <C10> <C10> <C10> <C10> <C10> <C10> <C10> <C10> <C10> <C10> <C10> <C10> <C10>

;       CSP   = IN3    NRZB   BCLK3   CCLK3  CYP1   <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>
;       CS1P  = IN3    NRZB   BCLK3   CCLK3  CYP1   <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29>

      IF ORGNUM=16 THEN ENTRY
       IF CHSEL=0 THEN ENTRY
        CS0P  = IN3    NRZB   BCLK3   CCLK3  CYP1   <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>
        CS1P  = IN3    NRZB   BCLK3   CCLK3  CYP1   <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29>
       EXIT

       IF CHSEL=1 THEN ENTRY
        CS1P  = IN3    NRZB   BCLK3   CCLK3  CYP1   <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>
        CS0P  = IN3    NRZB   BCLK3   CCLK3  CYP1   <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29>
       EXIT
      EXIT

      IF ORGNUM=8 AND MIXEDCHIP(1)="N" THEN ENTRY
        CS0P  = IN3    NRZB   BCLK3   CCLK3  CYP1   <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>
        CS1P  = IN3    NRZB   BCLK3   CCLK3  CYP1   <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29>
      EXIT

      IF ORGNUM=8 AND MIXEDCHIP(1)="1" THEN ENTRY
        CS1P  = IN3    NRZB   BCLK3   CCLK3  CYP1   <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>
        CS0P  = IN3    NRZB   BCLK3   CCLK3  CYP1   <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29>
      EXIT
     
            
FMD00CA:   
;12G
       ;---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
       ;                                          | CYP1      CYP2   CYP3    CYP4       CYP5      CYP6      CYP7   CYP8   CYP9   CYP10     CYP11     CYP12  CYP13  CYP14      CYP15     CYP16    
       ;---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
       ;                                          | MPC2      ACT12  ACT21   MRW11      PRE2      ACT22     WR1    WR2    WRL1   MPC1      ACT11     ACT12  PRE2   WR2        TMRS12    CAS2

       ;                                          | TMRS22           PDE11   DSM2       MRR2      RD1                            TMRS20

       ;                                          |                  TMRS10  TMRS23C    TMRS23S   TMRS23G

       ;------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
IF ORGNUM=16 THEN ENTRY
        CA0   = IN2   NRZB  BCLK2  CCLK2 PSM CYP1   <Y0 ,Y8 > <X16>  <C0>    <C0,Y8 >   <X16,Y4>  <X0,Y0>   <C0>   <Y16>  <C0>   <C0 ,C0 > <C0 ,Y12> </X16> </X16> </Y16,Y12> <C0 ,Y14> <C0,FL >

        CA3   = IN2   NRZB  BCLK2  CCLK2 PSM CYP1   <Y3 ,Y11> <X19>  <X7>    <C3,Y11>   <X19,Y7>  <X3,Y3>   <Y4>   <Y19>  <C3>   <C3 ,C3 > <X14,Y15> </X19> </X19> </Y19,FL > <C3 ,FL > <C3,FL >
        CA4   = IN2   NRZB  BCLK2  CCLK2 PSM CYP1   <Y4 ,Y12> <X11>  <X8>    <C4,FL >   <FL ,FL>  <X4,FL>   <Y7>   <Y5>   <Y7>   <C4 ,C4 > <X15,FL > <X11>  <FL>   <Y5  ,FL > <Y9 ,FL > <C4,FL >
        CA5   = IN2   NRZB  BCLK2  CCLK2 PSM CYP1   <Y5 ,Y13> <X12>  <X9>    <C5,FL >   <C5 ,FL>  <X5,FL>   <Y8>   <Y6>   <Y8>   <C5 ,C5 > <FL ,FL > <X12>  <C5>   <Y6  ,FL > <Y9 ,FL > <C5,FL >
        CA6   = IN2   NRZB  BCLK2  CCLK2 PSM CYP1   <Y6 ,Y14> <X13>  <X10>   <C6,FL >   <C6 ,FL>  <X6,FL>   <Y9>   <C6>   <Y9>   <Y7 ,Y15> <FL ,FL > <X13>  <C6>   <C6  ,FL > <Y8 ,FL > <Y3,FL >
EXIT
IF ORGNUM=8  THEN ENTRY
        CA0   = IN2   NRZB  BCLK2  CCLK2 PSM CYP1   <Y0 ,Y8 > <X17>  <C0>    <C0,Y8 >   <X17,Y4>  <X0,Y0>   <C0>   <Y17>  <C0>   <C0 ,C0 > <C0 ,Y12> </X17> </X17> </Y17,Y12> <C0 ,Y14> <C0,FL >

        CA4   = IN2   NRZB  BCLK2  CCLK2 PSM CYP1   <Y4 ,Y12> <X11>  <X8>    <C4,FL >   <FL ,FL>  <X4,FL>   <Y7>   <Y5>   <Y7>   <C4 ,C4 > <X15,FL > <X11>  <FL>   <Y5  ,FL > <Y9 ,FL > <C4,FL >
        CA5   = IN2   NRZB  BCLK2  CCLK2 PSM CYP1   <Y5 ,Y13> <X12>  <X9>    <C5,FL >   <C5 ,FL>  <X5,FL>   <Y8>   <Y6>   <Y8>   <C5 ,C5 > <X16,FL > <X12>  <C5>   <Y6  ,FL > <Y9 ,FL > <C5,FL >
        CA6   = IN2   NRZB  BCLK2  CCLK2 PSM CYP1   <Y6 ,Y14> <X13>  <X10>   <C6,FL >   <C6 ,FL>  <X6,FL>   <Y9>   <C6>   <Y9>   <Y7 ,Y15> <FL ,FL > <X13>  <C6>   <C6  ,FL > <Y8 ,FL > <Y3,FL >
EXIT
       ;------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
      CURFMT="FMD00"

GOTO CONT

FMD01:  
FH001S:                 ; 4Bank/4Bank Group, 16Bank BA Address                                            
;       ALLPIN=OPEN
 ;      WL=0 & RL=0

        CLKP  = IN1    NRZB   BCLK1   CCLK1  CYP1   <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14>

        WCKP  = IN8    DNRZ   BCLK8   CCLK8  CYP1   <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28>

;       CSP   = IN3    NRZB   BCLK3   CCLK3  CYP1   <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>
;       CS1P  = IN3    NRZB   BCLK3   CCLK3  CYP1   <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29>

      IF CHSEL=0 THEN ENTRY
        CS0P  = IN3    NRZB   BCLK3   CCLK3  CYP1   <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>

      EXIT

      EXIT

        CS1P  = IN3    NRZB   BCLK3   CCLK3  CYP1   <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29> <C29>
      EXIT

      CURFMT="FMD01"

FMD02: 
FH02DS:                 ; 4Bank/4Bank Group, 16Bank  BA Ctrl
;       ALLPIN=OPEN
;       WL=0 & RL=0

        CLKP  = IN1    NRZB   BCLK1   CCLK1  CYP1   <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14> <C14>

        RST   = IN4   /NRZB   BCLK4   CCLK4  CYP1   <C10> <C10> <C10> <C10> <C10> <C10> <C10> <C10> <C10> <C10> <C10> <C10> <C10> <C10> <C10> <C10>
      
      IF CHSEL=0 THEN ENTRY
        CS0P  = IN3    NRZB   BCLK3   CCLK3  CYP1   <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>

      EXIT

      EXIT

      EXIT

        CS1P  = IN3    NRZB   BCLK3   CCLK3  CYP1   <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>  <C9>

      EXIT

SDR_CKCARSTFMT:

   CKT   = IN1  RZX  BCLK1  CCLK1
   CKC   = IN1 /RZX  BCLK1  CCLK1
                            
   RST   = IN9 /NRZB BCLK9  CCLK9  CYP1   <C23>,<C23>,<C23>,<C23>,<C23>,<C23>,<C23>,<C23>,<C23>,<C23>,<C23>,<C23>,<C23>,<C23>,<C23>,<C23>

FMP01:
   ALLPIN=OPEN
   
   GOSUB SDR_CKCARSTFMT
   GOSUB TARGET_CS_SDR(TSTORD,DSPSLT)

;  DMPSEC= IN5  RZO  BCLK7  CCLK7  CYP1   <C0 >,<C0 >,<C0 >,<C0 >,<C0 >,<C0 >,<C0 >,<C0 >,<C0 >,<C0 >,<C0 >,<C0 >,<C0 >,<C0 >,<C0 >,<C0 >

   IF DSPSLT=0  THEN ENTRY  ;NON DPPBT
      IF TSTFLG=1 THEN DQP40A  = IN3,NRZB,BCLK3,CCLK3,IOC,DRENRZ,OUTL1,STRB1,VT1,CPEDLY0,EXPDLY0 CYP1 PBTX4FMT ; PBTX4FMT = "<DATAD4,-,-,FH> x16" defined pinlist file
      IF TSTFLG=2 THEN DQP40B  = IN3,NRZB,BCLK3,CCLK3,IOC,DRENRZ,OUTL1,STRB1,VT1,CPEDLY0,EXPDLY0 CYP1 PBTX4FMT
      IF TSTFLG=3 THEN DQP40C  = IN3,NRZB,BCLK3,CCLK3,IOC,DRENRZ,OUTL1,STRB1,VT1,CPEDLY0,EXPDLY0 CYP1 PBTX4FMT
      IF TSTFLG=4 THEN DQP40D  = IN3,NRZB,BCLK3,CCLK3,IOC,DRENRZ,OUTL1,STRB1,VT1,CPEDLY0,EXPDLY0 CYP1 PBTX4FMT
      IF TSTFLG=5 THEN DQP41A  = IN3,NRZB,BCLK3,CCLK3,IOC,DRENRZ,OUTL1,STRB1,VT1,CPEDLY0,EXPDLY0 CYP1 PBTX4FMT
      IF TSTFLG=6 THEN DQP41B  = IN3,NRZB,BCLK3,CCLK3,IOC,DRENRZ,OUTL1,STRB1,VT1,CPEDLY0,EXPDLY0 CYP1 PBTX4FMT
      IF TSTFLG=7 THEN DQP41C  = IN3,NRZB,BCLK3,CCLK3,IOC,DRENRZ,OUTL1,STRB1,VT1,CPEDLY0,EXPDLY0 CYP1 PBTX4FMT
      IF TSTFLG=8 THEN DQP41D  = IN3,NRZB,BCLK3,CCLK3,IOC,DRENRZ,OUTL1,STRB1,VT1,CPEDLY0,EXPDLY0 CYP1 PBTX4FMT
   EXIT    ;;IF DSPSLT=0
   IF DSPSLT<>0  THEN ENTRY
                       DQP4    = IN3,NRZB,BCLK3,CCLK3,IOC,DRENRZ,OUTL1,      VT1,CPEDLY0,EXPDLY0 CYP1 PBTX4FMT  
      IF TSTFLG>0 THEN DQ0     = IN3,NRZB,BCLK3,CCLK3,IOC,DRENRZ,OUTL1,STRB1,VT1,CPEDLY0,EXPDLY0 CYP1 DSDQ0FMT ; DSDQ0FMT = "<D0,-,-,FH> x16" defined pinlist file  
      IF TSTFLG>1 THEN DQ1     = IN3,NRZB,BCLK3,CCLK3,IOC,DRENRZ,OUTL1,STRB1,VT1,CPEDLY0,EXPDLY0 CYP1 DSDQ1FMT ; DSDQ1FMT = "<D1,-,-,FH> x16" defined pinlist file  
      IF TSTFLG>2 THEN DQ2     = IN3,NRZB,BCLK3,CCLK3,IOC,DRENRZ,OUTL1,STRB1,VT1,CPEDLY0,EXPDLY0 CYP1 DSDQ2FMT ; DSDQ2FMT = "<D2,-,-,FH> x16" defined pinlist file  
      IF TSTFLG>3 THEN DQ3     = IN3,NRZB,BCLK3,CCLK3,IOC,DRENRZ,OUTL1,STRB1,VT1,CPEDLY0,EXPDLY0 CYP1 DSDQ3FMT ; DSDQ3FMT = "<D3,-,-,FH> x16" defined pinlist file  
      IF TSTFLG>4 THEN DQ4     = IN3,NRZB,BCLK3,CCLK3,IOC,DRENRZ,OUTL1,STRB1,VT1,CPEDLY0,EXPDLY0 CYP1 DSDQ4FMT ; DSDQ4FMT = "<D0,-,-,FH> x16" defined pinlist file  
      IF TSTFLG>5 THEN DQ5     = IN3,NRZB,BCLK3,CCLK3,IOC,DRENRZ,OUTL1,STRB1,VT1,CPEDLY0,EXPDLY0 CYP1 DSDQ5FMT ; DSDQ5FMT = "<D1,-,-,FH> x16" defined pinlist file  
      IF TSTFLG>6 THEN DQ6     = IN3,NRZB,BCLK3,CCLK3,IOC,DRENRZ,OUTL1,STRB1,VT1,CPEDLY0,EXPDLY0 CYP1 DSDQ6FMT ; DSDQ6FMT = "<D2,-,-,FH> x16" defined pinlist file  
      IF TSTFLG>7 THEN DQ7     = IN3,NRZB,BCLK3,CCLK3,IOC,DRENRZ,OUTL1,STRB1,VT1,CPEDLY0,EXPDLY0 CYP1 DSDQ7FMT ; DSDQ7FMT = "<D3,-,-,FH> x16" defined pinlist file 
   EXIT    ;;IF DSPSLT<>0
  
      CURFMT="FMP01"


GOTO CONT

FMS07:  ;FOR CHIPPING

   ALLPIN=OPEN

   GOSUB SDR_CKCARSTFMT
;  GOSUB TARGET_CS_SDR(TSTORD,DSPSLT)

   IF CHSEL=0 THEN ENTRY
   CS0P  = IN2  DNRZ BCLK2  CCLK2  CYP1 <C11,Y12> <C11,C19> <C11,Y12> <C11,C19> <C11,Y12> <C11,C19> <C11,C11> <C11,FL > <C11,C11> <C11,C11> <C11,C11> <C11,C11> <C11,C11> <C11,C11> <C11,C11> <C11,C11> 
   CS1P  = IN2  DNRZ BCLK2  CCLK2  CYP1 < M1,Y12> < M1,C19> < M1,Y12> < M1,C19> < M1,Y12> < M1,C19> < M1, M1> < M1,FL > < M1, M1> < M1, M1> < M1, M1> < M1, M1> < M1, M1> < M1, M1> < M1, M1> < M1, M1> 
   EXIT
   IF CHSEL=1 THEN ENTRY
   CS0P  = IN2  DNRZ BCLK2  CCLK2  CYP1 < M1,Y12> < M1,C19> < M1,Y12> < M1,C19> < M1,Y12> < M1,C19> < M1, M1> < M1,FL > < M1, M1> < M1, M1> < M1, M1> < M1, M1> < M1, M1> < M1, M1> < M1, M1> < M1, M1> 
   CS1P  = IN2  DNRZ BCLK2  CCLK2  CYP1 <C11,Y12> <C11,C19> <C11,Y12> <C11,C19> <C11,Y12> <C11,C19> <C11,C11> <C11,FL > <C11,C11> <C11,C11> <C11,C11> <C11,C11> <C11,C11> <C11,C11> <C11,C11> <C11,C11> 
   EXIT


;  WCK1C  = IN5,DNRZ,BCLK5,CCLK5 CYP1 <C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>
;  RDQS0C = IN5,DNRZ,BCLK5,CCLK5 CYP1 <C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>

;  CKE    = IN5,NRZB,BCLK5,CCLK5 CYP1 <C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>
;  RDQS0C = IN5,DNRZ,BCLK5,CCLK5 CYP1 <C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>


   WCK1T  = IN5,NRZB,BCLK5,CCLK5 CYP1 <C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>
   WCK1C  = IN5,NRZB,BCLK5,CCLK5 CYP1 <C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>
   RDQS1T = IN5,NRZB,BCLK5,CCLK5 CYP1 <C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>
   RDQS1C = IN5,NRZB,BCLK5,CCLK5 CYP1 <C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>,<C2,C3>


   DQ1   = IN3 NRZB BCLK3 CCLK3 IOC DRENRZ OUTL1 STRB1 EXPA1 EXPDLY0 CPEDLY0 VT1 CYP1 <D0>,<D0>,<D0>,<D0>,<D0>,<D0>,<D0>,<D0>,<D0>,<D0>,<D0>,<D0>,<D0>

      CURFMT="FMS07"


GOTO CONT

    
FTPD1: ;for rccm x1 test
   ALLPIN=OPEN


   CKT   = IN1  RZX  BCLK1  CCLK1
   CKC   = IN1 /RZX  BCLK1  CCLK1
                            
   RST   = IN7 /NRZB BCLK9  CCLK9  CYP1   <C23>,<C23>,<C23>,<C23>,<C23>,<C23>,<C23>,<C23>,<C23>,<C23>,<C23>,<C23>,<C23>,<C23>,<C23>,<C23>
                            
;-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
;                                        CYP1      CYP2      CYP3      CYP4      CYP5      CYP6      CYP7      CYP8      CYP9      CYP10     CYP11     CYP12     CYP13     CYP14     CYP15     CYP16     
;-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------   
;                                        SDR       SDR       SDR       SDR       SDR       SDR       SDR       SDR       DDR       DDR       DDR       DDR       DDR       DDR       DDR       DDR       
;                                        ACT1      ACT2      WR/RD     WR/RD2    PRE1      PRE/REF   MRW       NOP       MRW1      MRW2      ACT1      ACT2      RD        CAS       PRE/REF   SRE       
;                                                                                                    TMRS      SRE/PD    NOP/                                    WR/MWR                                   
;-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------   
   CA0   = IN4  DNRZ BCLK4  CCLK4  CYP1 <C4 ,Y13> <C4 ,C20> <C4 ,Y13> <C4 ,C20> <C4 ,Y13> <C4 ,C20> <C4 ,C6 > <C4 ,FL > <C4 ,Y0 > <C4 ,X0 > <C4 ,C19> <C4 ,X0 > <C4 ,C19> <C4 ,X0 > <C4 ,Y12> <C4 ,Y0 >  
   CA1   = IN4  DNRZ BCLK4  CCLK4  CYP1 <X0 ,X9 > <X0 ,X9 > <C5 ,C7 > <C5 ,C7 > <C5 ,C7 > <C5 ,C7 > <C5 ,C7 > <C5 ,FL > <C5 ,Y1 > <C5 ,X1 > <C5 ,C20> <C5 ,X1 > <C5 ,C20> <C5 ,X1 > <C5 ,Y13> <C5 ,Y1 >  
   CA2   = IN4  DNRZ BCLK4  CCLK4  CYP1 <X1 ,X10> <X1 ,X10> <Y0 ,D0 > <Y0 ,D0 > <FL ,C8 > <FL ,C8 > <Y0 ,X0 > <C6 ,FL > <C6 ,Y2 > <C6 ,X2 > <C6 ,C21> <C6 ,X2 > <C6 ,C21> <C6 ,X2 > <C6 ,Y14> <C6 ,Y2 >  
   CA3   = IN4  DNRZ BCLK4  CCLK4  CYP1 <X2 ,X11> <X2 ,X11> <Y1 ,D1 > <Y1 ,D1 > <FL ,C9 > <FL ,C9 > <Y1 ,X1 > <C7 ,FL > <C7 ,Y3 > <C7 ,X3 > <X14,C22> <X7 ,X3 > <Y4 ,C22> <C7 ,X3 > <C7 ,Y15> <C7 ,Y3 >  
   CA4   = IN4  DNRZ BCLK4  CCLK4  CYP1 <X3 ,X12> <X3 ,X12> <Y2 ,D2 > <Y2 ,D2 > <FL ,FL > <FL ,FL > <Y2 ,X2 > <C8 ,FL > <C8 ,Y4 > <C8 ,X4 > <X15,X11> <X8 ,X4 > <Y7 ,Y5 > <C8 ,C20> <C8 ,FL > <C8 ,Y4 >  
   CA5   = IN4  DNRZ BCLK4  CCLK4  CYP1 <X4 ,X13> <X4 ,X13> <Y3 ,Y10> <Y3 ,Y10> <FL ,FL > <FL ,FL > <Y3 ,X3 > <C9 ,FL > <C9 ,Y5 > <C9 ,X5 > <X16,X12> <X9 ,X5 > <Y8 ,Y6 > <C9 ,FL > <C9 ,FL > <C9 ,C20>  
   CA6   = IN4  DNRZ BCLK4  CCLK4  CYP1 <X5 ,X14> <X5 ,X14> <Y4 ,FL > <Y4 ,FL > <FL ,FL > <FL ,FL > <Y4 ,X4 > <C10,FL > <C10,Y6 > <X7 ,X6 > <X17,X13> <X10,X6 > <Y9 ,M2 > <C10,Y3 > <C10,M2 > <C10,M2 >  
IF ORGNUM=16 THEN ENTRY
   CA7   = IN4  DNRZ BCLK4  CCLK4  CYP1 <X6 ,X15> <X6 ,X15> <Y5 ,FL > <Y5 ,FL > <FL ,FL > <FL ,FL > <Y5 ,X5 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 >  
   CA8   = IN4  DNRZ BCLK4  CCLK4  CYP1 <X7 ,Y14> <X7 ,C21> <Y6 ,Y14> <Y6 ,C21> <FL ,Y14> <FL ,C21> <Y6 ,X6 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 >  
   CA9W  = IN4  DNRZ BCLK4  CCLK4  CYP1 <X8 ,Y15> <X8 ,C22> <Y7 ,Y15> <Y7 ,C22> <FL ,Y15> <FL ,C22> <FL ,X7 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 >  

   IF CHSEL=0 THEN ENTRY
   CS0P  = IN2  DNRZ BCLK2  CCLK2  CYP1 <C11,Y12> <C11,C19> <C11,Y12> <C11,C19> <C11,Y12> <C11,C19> <C11,C11> <C11,FL > <C11,C11> <C11,C11> <C11,C11> <C11,C11> <C11,C11> <C11,C11> <C11,C11> <C11,C11> 
   CS1P  = IN2  DNRZ BCLK2  CCLK2  CYP1 < M1,Y12> < M1,C19> < M1,Y12> < M1,C19> < M1,Y12> < M1,C19> < M1, M1> < M1,FL > < M1, M1> < M1, M1> < M1, M1> < M1, M1> < M1, M1> < M1, M1> < M1, M1> < M1, M1> 
   EXIT
   IF CHSEL=1 THEN ENTRY
   CS0P  = IN2  DNRZ BCLK2  CCLK2  CYP1 < M1,Y12> < M1,C19> < M1,Y12> < M1,C19> < M1,Y12> < M1,C19> < M1, M1> < M1,FL > < M1, M1> < M1, M1> < M1, M1> < M1, M1> < M1, M1> < M1, M1> < M1, M1> < M1, M1> 
   CS1P  = IN2  DNRZ BCLK2  CCLK2  CYP1 <C11,Y12> <C11,C19> <C11,Y12> <C11,C19> <C11,Y12> <C11,C19> <C11,C11> <C11,FL > <C11,C11> <C11,C11> <C11,C11> <C11,C11> <C11,C11> <C11,C11> <C11,C11> <C11,C11> 
   EXIT

EXIT
IF ORGNUM=8 THEN ENTRY
   CA7X8 = IN4  DNRZ BCLK4  CCLK4  CYP1 <X6 ,X15> <X6 ,X15> <Y5 ,FL > <Y5 ,FL > <FL ,FL > <FL ,FL > <Y5 ,X5 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 >  
   CA8X8 = IN4  DNRZ BCLK4  CCLK4  CYP1 <X7 ,Y14> <X7 ,C21> <Y6 ,Y14> <Y6 ,C21> <FL ,Y14> <FL ,C21> <Y6 ,X6 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 >  
   CA9X8 = IN4  DNRZ BCLK4  CCLK4  CYP1 <X8 ,Y15> <X8 ,C22> <Y7 ,Y15> <Y7 ,C22> <FL ,Y15> <FL ,C22> <FL ,X7 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 > <C2 ,C3 >  
   IF MIXEDCHIP="1" THEN ENTRY
   CS0P  = IN2  DNRZ BCLK2  CCLK2  CYP1 < M1,Y12> < M1,C19> < M1,Y12> < M1,C19> < M1,Y12> < M1,C19> < M1, M1> < M1,FL > < M1, M1> < M1, M1> < M1, M1> < M1, M1> < M1, M1> < M1, M1> < M1, M1> < M1, M1> 
   CS1P  = IN2  DNRZ BCLK2  CCLK2  CYP1 <C11,Y12> <C11,C19> <C11,Y12> <C11,C19> <C11,Y12> <C11,C19> <C11,C11> <C11,FL > <C11,C11> <C11,C11> <C11,C11> <C11,C11> <C11,C11> <C11,C11> <C11,C11> <C11,C11> 
   EXIT      
   IF MIXEDCHIP="0" THEN ENTRY
   CS0P  = IN2  DNRZ BCLK2  CCLK2  CYP1 <C11,Y12> <C11,C19> <C11,Y12> <C11,C19> <C11,Y12> <C11,C19> <C11,C11> <C11,FL > <C11,C11> <C11,C11> <C11,C11> <C11,C11> <C11,C11> <C11,C11> <C11,C11> <C11,C11> 
   CS1P  = IN2  DNRZ BCLK2  CCLK2  CYP1 < M1,Y12> < M1,C19> < M1,Y12> < M1,C19> < M1,Y12> < M1,C19> < M1, M1> < M1,FL > < M1, M1> < M1, M1> < M1, M1> < M1, M1> < M1, M1> < M1, M1> < M1, M1> < M1, M1> 
   EXIT      
   
EXIT

   LDMIP  = IN4  NRZB BCLK7  CCLK7  CYP1   <C0>,<C0>,<C0>,<C0>,<C0>,<C0>,<C0>,<C0>,<C0>,<C0>,<C0>,<C0>,<C0>,<C0>,<C0>
   UDMIP  = IN4  NRZB BCLK7  CCLK7  CYP1   <C1>,<C1>,<C1>,<C1>,<C1>,<C1>,<C1>,<C1>,<C1>,<C1>,<C1>,<C1>,<C1>,<C1>,<C1>
                         
   DQ0   = IN3  NRZB   BCLK11 CCLK11 CYP1 <M2 >,<M2 >,<M2 >,<M2 >,<M2 >,<M2 >,<M2 >,<M2 >,<M2 >,<M2 >,<M2 >,<M2 >,<M2 >  ;input
   DQ1   = IN3  NRZB   BCLK3  CCLK3  IOC DRENRZ OUTL1 STRB1 EXPA1 EXPDLY0 CPEDLY0 VT1 CYP1 <D0>,<D0>,<D0>,<D0>,<D0>,<D0>,<D0>,<D0>,<D0>,<D0>,<D0>,<D0>,<D0>
   
  IF ORGNUM=8 THEN ENTRY
   DQ8   = IN3  NRZB   BCLK11 CCLK11 CYP1 <M2 >,<M2 >,<M2 >,<M2 >,<M2 >,<M2 >,<M2 >,<M2 >,<M2 >,<M2 >,<M2 >,<M2 >,<M2 >  ;input
   DQ9   = IN3  NRZB   BCLK3  CCLK3  IOC DRENRZ OUTL1 STRB1 EXPA1 EXPDLY0 CPEDLY0 VT1 CYP1 <D0>,<D0>,<D0>,<D0>,<D0>,<D0>,<D0>,<D0>,<D0>,<D0>,<D0>,<D0>,<D0>
  EXIT

      CURFMT="FTPD1"


GOTO CONT


;========================================================================================================================================================================
;        PIN FORMAT END
;========================================================================================================================================================================

;========================================================================================================================================================================
;        PIN TIMMING START
;========================================================================================================================================================================
DDRTIM:                            TIMING SET = 1
    FTRATE = TCK                                                      
        FTCKR  = FTRATE*0.8      
        FTCKF  = FTRATE*1.3      
 
        FTCS   = FTRATE*0.0                                                     
        FTDQSR = FTRATE*0.8                                                     
        FTDQSF = FTRATE*1.3                                                     
        FTDQ1  = FTRATE*0.25                                                           
        FTDQ2  = FTRATE*0.75                                                           
        FTCA   = FTRATE*0.0                                                     
        FTDM1  = FTRATE*0.25                                                           
        FTDM2  = FTRATE*0.75                                                           
        FTCKE  = FTRATE*0.0                                                     
        FTRESET= FTRATE*0.0                                                     
        
        FTSTRB1  = FTRATE*1.000+FTRATE*0.35     ;Shift tck/4 to adjust strb point for Test mode "SDR"-tdv
        FTSTRB3  = FTSTRB1
        FTSTRB1TR= FTRATE*1.000
        FTSTRB129= FTRATE*1.500+FTRATE*0.35
        FTSTRB131= FTSTRB129 

     IF FAMOD2(3,2)="NN" THEN ENTRY  ;;Normal
        FTSTRB1  = FTRATE*1.000
        FTSTRB129= FTRATE*1.500
        FTSTRB3  = FTSTRB1
        FTSTRB131= FTSTRB129 
     EXIT

      IF TCK>=5NS THEN ENTRY
          FTDQ1  = FTRATE*0.50
          FTDQ2  = FTDQ1+(FTRATE*0.5)
          FTDM1  = FTRATE*0.50
          FTDM2  = FTDM1+(FTRATE*0.5)
          FTSTRB1  = FTRATE*0.50
          FTSTRB129= FTSTRB1+(FTRATE*0.5)
          FTSTRB3  = FTSTRB1
          FTSTRB131= FTSTRB129 
     EXIT

     IF FAPAT2(5,3)= "AT2" OR FAPAT2(5,3)= "ATM" THEN ENTRY  ;;MR Read
        FTSTRB1  = FTRATE*1.000+FTRATE*0.35-150PS
     EXIT

     IF TCK<2NS THEN ENTRY    
     RATE    =  FTRATE     <2>FTRATE*5    <12>FTRATE      <13>FTRATE        <15>FTRATE    <16>FTRATE        
     BCLK1   =  FTCKR      <2>FTCKR*5     <12>OPEN        <13>FTCKR         <15>FTCKR     <16>FTCKR     ; CK RISING    
     CCLK1   =  FTCKF      <2>FTCKF*5     <12>FTCKF       <13>OPEN          <15>FTCKF     <16>FTCKF     ; CK FALLING
     EXIT
     IF TCK=>2NS THEN ENTRY    
     RATE    =  FTRATE     <2>FTRATE      <12>FTRATE      <13>FTRATE        <15>FTRATE    <16>FTRATE        
     BCLK1   =  FTCKR      <2>FTCKR       <12>OPEN        <13>FTCKR         <15>FTCKR     <16>FTCKR     ; CK RISING    
     CCLK1   =  FTCKF      <2>FTCKF       <12>FTCKF       <13>OPEN          <15>FTCKF     <16>FTCKF     ; CK FALLING
     EXIT
    BCLK2   =  FTCS       <2>FTCS*5      <12>FTCS        <13>FTCS          <15>FTCS      <16>FTCS      ; CS    
    CCLK2   =  FTCS       <2>FTCS*5      <12>FTCS        <13>FTCS          <15>FTCS      <16>FTCS      
       ;DREL1   =  FTDQ1      <2>FTDQ1*5     <12>FTDQ1       <13>FTDQ1         <15>FTDQ1     <16>FTDQ1     ; DQ 1ST
       ;DRET1   =  FTDQ1      <2>FTDQ1*5     <12>FTDQ1       <13>FTDQ1         <15>FTDQ1     <16>FTDQ1     ; DQ 1ST    
       BCLK3   =  FTDQ1      <2>FTDQ1*5     <12>FTDQ1       <13>FTDQ1         <15>FTDQ1     <16>FTDQ1     ; DQ 1ST    
       CCLK3   =  FTDQ2      <2>FTDQ2*5     <12>FTDQ2       <13>FTDQ2         <15>FTDQ2     <16>FTDQ2     ; DQ 2ND    
       BCLK4   =  FTCA       <2>FTCA*5      <12>FTCA        <13>FTCA          <15>FTCA      <16>FTCA      ; CA    
       CCLK4   =  FTCA       <2>FTCA*5      <12>FTCA        <13>FTCA          <15>FTCA      <16>FTCA      
       ;DREL2   =  FTDQSR     <2>FTDQSR*5    <12>FTDQSR      <13>FTDQSR        <15>FTDQSR    <16>FTDQSR    ; DQS RISING
       ;DRET2   =  FTDQSR     <2>FTDQSR*5    <12>FTDQSR      <13>FTDQSR        <15>FTDQSR    <16>FTDQSR    ; DQS RISING    
       BCLK5   =  FTDQSR     <2>FTDQSR*5    <12>FTDQSR      <13>FTDQSR        <15>FTDQSR    <16>FTDQSR    ; DQS RISING    
       CCLK5   =  FTDQSF     <2>FTDQSF*5    <12>FTDQSF      <13>FTDQSF        <15>FTDQSF    <16>FTDQSF    ; DQS FALLING    
       BCLK7   =  FTDM1      <2>FTDM1*5     <12>FTDM1       <13>FTDM1         <15>FTDM1     <16>FTDM1     ; DM    
       CCLK7   =  FTDM2      <2>FTDM2*5     <12>FTDM2       <13>FTDM2         <15>FTDM2     <16>FTDM2         
       BCLK8   =  FTCKE      <2>FTCKE*5     <12>FTCKE       <13>FTCKE         <15>FTCKE     <16>FTCKE     ; CKE    
       CCLK8   =  FTCKE      <2>FTCKE*5     <12>FTCKE       <13>FTCKE         <15>FTCKE     <16>FTCKE         
       BCLK9   =  FTRESET    <2>FTRESET*5   <12>FTRESET     <13>FTRESET       <15>FTRESET   <16>FTRESET   ; RESET    
       CCLK9   =  FTRESET    <2>FTRESET*5   <12>FTRESET     <13>FTRESET       <15>FTRESET   <16>FTRESET       
       STRB1   =  FTSTRB1    <2>OPEN        <12>FTSTRB1     <13>FTSTRB1       <15>FTSTRB1TR <16>OPEN      ;    
       STRB3   =  FTSTRB3    <2>OPEN        <12>FTSTRB1TR   <13>FTSTRB1TR     <15>FTSTRB1TR <16>OPEN      ;    
       STRB129 =  FTSTRB129  <2>OPEN        <12>FTSTRB129   <13>FTSTRB129     <15>FTSTRB129 <16>OPEN      ;    
       STRB131 =  FTSTRB131  <2>OPEN        <12>FTSTRB129   <13>FTSTRB129     <15>FTSTRB129 <16>OPEN      ;

GOTO CONT


;========================================================================================================================================================================
;        PIN TIMMING END
;========================================================================================================================================================================


VDOWN:
;WRITE /,FAVCC2
        IN1   = FAVCC2,0V
        IN2   = FAVCC2,0V
        IN3   = FAVCC2,0V
        IN4   = FAVCC2,0V
        IN5   = FAVCC2,0V
        IN6   = FAVCC2,0V
        IN7   = FAVCC2,0V
        IN8   = FAVCC2,0V
        IN11  = FAVCC2,0V
        IN12  = FAVCC2,0V
        IN13  = FAVCC2,0V
GOTO CONT
;=========================================================================================================================================================
;;         TEST TIME MEASURE ROUTINE
;=========================================================================================================================================================

TIMCHK:
GOTO CONT

 INSERT WHREGION
 INSERT WHHTMP0 
 INSERT WHIDAS0
;INSERT WHMIXF0
 INSERT WHSHMTEST
 INSERT WHVERI0
 INSERT WHDOUMI

;==================================
;==================================
;    DSOLPART 
;==================================
;==================================

VBASIC:
        ARGUMENT(VCCT,VCCL,VCCX,VIWC,VIWD)
 
        SELECT VS1 PARALLEL
        SELECT VS2 PARALLEL
        SELECT VS3 PARALLEL
        SELECT VS4 PARALLEL

        VCC1 = VCCT*1.72
        VCCH = VCCT
;       VCCL = VCCT
;       IF DVFSC="E"  THEN VCCL=VCCT-150MV
;       IF DVFSC="E"  THEN VCCL=VCCT*0.85 

        IF DVFSQ<>"E" THEN VREFVAL=250MV 
        IF DVFSQ="E"  THEN VREFVAL=180MV  

;       VCCX = VCCT*0.476

        VREFCAVAL=(VREFVAL/VCCX*100-10)*2
        VREFBYTE0=(VREFVAL/VCCX*100-10)*2
        VREFBYTE1=(VREFVAL/VCCX*100-10)*2

;       VREFCAVAL=(25/((LP5VD2/1V)*0.476)-15)*2
;       VREFBYTE0=(25/((LP5VD2/1V)*0.476)-15)*2
;       VREFBYTE1=(25/((LP5VD2/1V)*0.476)-15)*2
        
        VS1  = VCC1, R16V,M0.8A,500MA,-500MA
        VS2  = VCCH, R16V,M0.8A,500MA,-500MA
        VS3  = VCCL, R16V,M0.8A,500MA,-500MA
        VS4  = VCCX, R16V,M0.8A,500MA,-500MA

;       VREFC= VCCX*VRCA               ;VREFCA Range[0]
;       VREFD= VCCX*VRDQ+65MV ;65MV    ;VREFDQ Range[0]
        VREFQ= VCCX*50.0/98.0          ;VOH=VDDQ/2 -> 48/(50+48) ;; LP5  

        VREFOFFSET=0MV
        VREFOFFSET=(VCCT-1.05V)*0.20
        IF DVFSQ="E"  THEN VREFOFFSET=20MV

;       VREFC= VREFVAL+25MV              ;VREFCA Range[0]
;       VREFD= VREFVAL+25MV              ;VREFDQ Range[0]

        VREFC= VREFVAL+VREFOFFSET        ;VREFCA Range[0]
        VREFD= VREFVAL+VREFOFFSET        ;VREFDQ Range[0]


;       VREFC= LP5VDQ*0.35+YREFDQ2              ;VREFCA Range[0]
;       VREFD= LP5VDQ*0.35+YREFDQ2              ;VREFDQ Range[0]


        VTTT = 0V                      ;VSSQ Term.

        INHF = VCCT*0.75
        INLF = VCCT*0.25

        CARAT=60.0/(50.0+60.0)         ; ODT=RZQ/4
        DQRAT=60.0/(50.0+60.0)         ; ODT=RZQ/4

        IF MR11_CAODT=#0 THEN CAODTVAL=10000
        IF MR11_CAODT=#1 THEN CAODTVAL=240
        IF MR11_CAODT=#2 THEN CAODTVAL=120
        IF MR11_CAODT=#3 THEN CAODTVAL=80 
        IF MR11_CAODT=#4 THEN CAODTVAL=60 
        IF MR11_CAODT=#5 THEN CAODTVAL=48 
        IF MR11_CAODT=#6 THEN CAODTVAL=40 

        IF MR11_DQODT=#0 THEN DQODTVAL=10000
        IF MR11_DQODT=#1 THEN DQODTVAL=240
        IF MR11_DQODT=#2 THEN DQODTVAL=120
        IF MR11_DQODT=#3 THEN DQODTVAL=80 
        IF MR11_DQODT=#4 THEN DQODTVAL=60 
        IF MR11_DQODT=#5 THEN DQODTVAL=48 
        IF MR11_DQODT=#6 THEN DQODTVAL=40 

        CARAT=CAODTVAL/(50.0+CAODTVAL)
        IF ORGNUM=8 THEN CARAT=(CAODTVAL/2)/(50.0+(CAODTVAL/2))
        IF MR11_CAODT=#0 THEN CARAT=1

        DQRAT=DQODTVAL/(50.0+DQODTVAL)
        IF MR11_DQODT=#0 THEN DQRAT=1

               
        I2HF = (VREFC+VIWC)/CARAT      ;Relax
        I2LF = (VREFC-VIWC)/CARAT
        I3HF = (VREFD+VIWD)/DQRAT
        I3LF = (VREFD-VIWD)/DQRAT
   
        IN4  = INHF,INLF               ;RST

        I8HF = (VREFD+0.25V)/DQRAT
        I8LF = (VREFD-0.25V)/DQRAT

       ; WRITE MR11_CAODT," ",CAODTVAL," ",CARAT," ",MR11_DQODT," ",DQRAT,I2HF,I2LF
       
        IN1  = I2HF,I2LF               ;CLK
        IN2  = I2HF,I2LF               ;CA
;       IN3  = I2HF,I2LF               ;CS
        IN3  = VCCH,0V                 ;CS
        IF DVFSC="E" THEN IN3  = VCCH*0.7,0V
        IF DVFSC="E" AND ORGNUM=8  THEN IN3  = VCCH,0V
        IN8  = I8HF,I8LF               ;WCK
        IN9  = I3HF,I3LF               ;DQ
        IN10 = I3HF,I3LF               ;DM
        IN11 = I3HF,I3LF               ;DQS

   ; center 250mv --> input center 250*11/6 = 458mv  (odt 60ohm)
   ; swing  300mv --> input swing  300*11/6 = 550mv
   ;                  vih = 458mv+550mv => 1008mv
   ;                  vil = 458mv-550mv =>  -92mv

   ;    IN1  = 1.01V,-0.092V           ;WCK  
   ;    IN2  = 1.01V,-0.092V           ;DQ 
   ;    IN3  = 1.01V,-0.092V           ;DM 
   ;    IN8  = 1.01V,-0.092V           ;WCK
   ;    IN9  = 1.01V,-0.092V           ;DQ 
   ;    IN10 = 1.01V,-0.092V           ;DM 
   ;    IN11 = 1.01V,-0.092V           ;DQS


        OUTHF= VREFQ*0.50;;*0.9
        OUTLF= VREFQ*0.50;;*0.9

        OUT1=OUTHF OUTLF
        OUT3=OUTHF OUTLF

        VT1=VTTT
        VT3=VTTT

GOTO CONT

    
VIDD:  
        ARGUMENT(VCCTI,VCCLI,VCCXI,VIWCI,VIWDI)
 
;;      SELECT VS1 PARALLEL
;;      SELECT VS2 PARALLEL
;;      SELECT VS3 PARALLEL
;;      SELECT VS4 PARALLEL

        VCC1 = VCCTI*1.72
        VCCH = VCCTI
;       VCCL = VCCT
;       VCCX = VCCT*0.476

;;      VS1  = VCC1, R16V,M0.8A,500MA,-500MA
;;      VS2  = VCCH, R16V,M0.8A,500MA,-500MA
;;      VS3  = VCCL, R16V,M0.8A,500MA,-500MA
;;      VS4  = VCCX, R16V,M0.8A,500MA,-500MA

;       VREFC= VCCXI*VRCA               ;VREFCA Range[0]
;       VREFD= VCCXI*VRDQ+65MV ;65MV    ;VREFDQ Range[0]
        VREFQ= VCCXI*50.0/98.0          ;VOH=VDDQ/2 -> 50/(50+48) ;; LP4X

        VREFC= 250MV                   ;VREFCA Range[0]
        VREFD= 250MV                   ;VREFDQ Range[0]

        VTTT = 0V                      ;VSSQ Term.

        INHF = VCCTI*0.75
        INLF = VCCTI*0.25

        CARAT=60.0/(50.0+60.0)         ; ODT=RZQ/4
        DQRAT=60.0/(50.0+60.0)         ; ODT=RZQ/4

        I2HF = (VREFC+VIWCI)           ; ODD OFF   ;Relax
        I2LF = (VREFC-VIWCI)           ; ODD OFF
        I3HF = (VREFD+VIWDI)           ; ODD OFF
        I3LF = (VREFD-VIWDI)           ; ODD OFF
     
        IN4  = INHF,INLF               ;RST

        IN1  = I2HF,I2LF               ;CLK
        IN2  = I2HF,I2LF               ;CA
        IN3  = I2HF,I2LF               ;CS
        IN8  = I3HF,I3LF               ;WCK
        IN9  = I3HF,I3LF               ;DQ
        IN10 = I3HF,I3LF               ;DM
        IN11 = I3HF,I3LF               ;DQS

   ; center 250mv --> input center 250*11/6 = 458mv  (odt 60ohm)
   ; swing  300mv --> input swing  300*11/6 = 550mv
   ;                  vih = 458mv+550mv => 1008mv
   ;                  vil = 458mv-550mv =>  -92mv

   ;    IN1  = 1.01V,-0.092V           ;WCK  
   ;    IN2  = 1.01V,-0.092V           ;DQ 
   ;    IN3  = 1.01V,-0.092V           ;DM 
   ;    IN8  = 1.01V,-0.092V           ;WCK
   ;    IN9  = 1.01V,-0.092V           ;DQ 
   ;    IN10 = 1.01V,-0.092V           ;DM 
   ;    IN11 = 1.01V,-0.092V           ;DQS


        OUTHF= VREFQ*0.50;;*0.9
        OUTLF= VREFQ*0.50;;*0.9

        OUT1=OUTHF OUTLF
        OUT3=OUTHF OUTLF

        VT1=VTTT
        VT3=VTTT

GOTO CONT

;;; CKR 4:1 Case
TFCHG1: 
        ARGUMENT(TCRAT1,TCRAT2)

        TRATE =  TCRAT1
        TRATE2=  TCRAT2

       ;TS1 ---------------        
        TCLKR  =  TRATE*0.5+TRATE*0.0                                     
        TCLKD  =  TRATE*0.5+TRATE*0.5         
        WCKR   =  TRATE*0.5+TRATE*0.0         
        WCKF   =  TRATE*0.5+TRATE*0.5         
        TISHR  =  TRATE*0.5+TRATE*1.0         
        TISHD  =  TRATE*0.5+TRATE*1.5         

        TISHRC =  TRATE*0.5+TRATE*1.0         
        TISHDC =  TRATE*0.5+TRATE*1.5         

        IF DVFSC="E" THEN ENTRY
           TISHRC =  TRATE*0.5+TRATE*1.0+300PS
           TISHDC =  TRATE*0.5+TRATE*1.5+300PS         
           WCKR   =  TRATE*0.5+TRATE*0.0-200PS         
           WCKF   =  TRATE*0.5+TRATE*0.5-200PS         
        EXIT
        

        TDSVA  =  TRATE*0.5+TRATE*0.0-TRATE*0.15;+450PS  
        TDHVA  =  TRATE*0.5+TRATE*0.5-TRATE*0.15;+450PS  
        TSACE  =  WCKR+1NS+TSAC+500PS ;1.56NS       
        TSACO  =  WCKF+1NS+TSAC+500PS ;1.56NS      

        TISHRD =  TRATE*0.5+TRATE*0.5         
        TISHDD =  TRATE*0.5+TRATE*1.5         



       ;TS2 ---------------                                                                   
        TCLKR2 =  TRATE2*0.5+TRATE2*0.0        
        TCLKD2 =  TRATE2*0.5+TRATE2*0.5        
        WCKR2  =  TRATE2*0.5+TRATE2*0.0        
        WCKF2  =  TRATE2*0.5+TRATE2*0.5        
        TISHR2 =  TRATE2*0.5+TRATE2*1.0         
        TISHD2 =  TRATE2*0.5+TRATE2*1.5        
        TDSVA2 =  TRATE2*0.5+TRATE2*0.0-TRATE*0.15;+450PS 
        TDHVA2 =  TRATE2*0.5+TRATE2*0.5-TRATE*0.15;+450PS 
        TSACE2 =  WCKR2+1NS+TSAC+TRATE*0.4 ;1.50NS      
        TSACO2 =  WCKF2+1NS+TSAC+TRATE*0.4 ;1.50NS      

       
        TIMING SET=1

        RATE   =  TRATE  TRATE2  TRATE  TRATE  TRATE  TRATE  TRATE  TRATE2       ;RATE
        BCLK1  =  TCLKR  TCLKR2  TCLKR  TCLKR  TCLKR  TCLKR  TCLKR  TCLKR2       ;CLK
        CCLK1  =  TCLKD  TCLKD2  TCLKD  TCLKD  TCLKD  TCLKD  TCLKD  TCLKD2       ;CLK

        BCLK2  =  TISHR  TISHR2  TISHR  TISHR  TISHR  TISHRD TISHR  TISHR2       ;CA
        CCLK2  =  TISHD  TISHD2  TISHD  TISHD  TISHD  TISHDD TISHD  TISHD2       ;CA

        BCLK3  =  TISHRC TISHR2  TISHR  TISHR  TISHR  TISHRD TISHR  TISHR2       ;CS
        CCLK3  =  TISHDC TISHD2  TISHD  TISHD  TISHD  TISHDD TISHD  TISHD2       ;CS

        BCLK4  =  TISHR  TISHR2  TISHR  TISHR  TISHR  TISHRD TISHR  TISHR2       ;CS
        CCLK4  =  TISHD  TISHD2  TISHD  TISHD  TISHD  TISHDD TISHD  TISHD2       ;CS

        BCLK8  =  WCKR   WCKR2   WCKR   WCKR   WCKR   WCKR   WCKR   WCKR2        ;WCK
        CCLK8  =  WCKF   WCKF2   WCKF   WCKF   WCKF   WCKF   WCKF   WCKF2        ;WCK

;IF  TWCLK<>0PS   THEN ENTRY
;        CCLK8  =  WCKF+TWCLK   WCKF2   WCKF   WCKF   WCKF   WCKF   WCKF   WCKF2        ;WCK
;EXIT

        BCLK9  =  TDSVA  TDSVA2  TDSVA  TDSVA  TDSVA  TDSVA  TDSVA  TDSVA2       ;DQ
        CCLK9  =  TDHVA  TDHVA2  TDHVA  TDHVA  TDHVA  TDHVA  TDHVA  TDHVA2       ;DQ

        BCLK10 =  TDSVA  TDSVA2  TDSVA  TDSVA  TDSVA  TDSVA  TDSVA  TDSVA2       ;DMI
        CCLK10 =  TDHVA  TDHVA2  TDHVA  TDHVA  TDHVA  TDHVA  TDHVA  TDHVA2       ;DMI

        BCLK11 =  TDSVA  TDSVA2  TDSVA  TDSVA  TDSVA  TDSVA  TDSVA  TDSVA2       ;RDQS
        CCLK11 =  TDHVA  TDHVA2  TDHVA  TDHVA  TDHVA  TDHVA  TDHVA  TDHVA2       ;RDQS

        STRB1  =  TSACE  TSACE2  TSACE  TSACE  TSACE  TSACE  TSACE  TSACE2       ;TSAC
        STRB3  =  TSACE  TSACE2  TSACE  TSACE  TSACE  TSACE  TSACE  TSACE2       ;TDQSCK
        STRB129 = TSACO  TSACO2  TSACO  TSACO  TSACO  TSACO  TSACO  TSACO2       ;TSAC
        STRB131 = TSACO  TSACO2  TSACO  TSACO  TSACO  TSACO  TSACO  TSACO2       ;TDQSCK

        TIMING SET=15  ;for Training

        RATE   =  TRATE  TRATE                                                    ;RATE
        BCLK1  =  TCLKR  TCLKR                                                    ;CLK
        CCLK1  =  TCLKD  TCLKD                                                    ;CLK

        BCLK2  =  TISHR  TISHR                                                    ;CA
        CCLK2  =  TISHD  TISHD                                                    ;CA

        BCLK3  =  TISHR  TISHR                                                    ;CS
        CCLK3  =  TISHD  TISHD                                                    ;CS

        BCLK4  =  TISHR  TISHR                                                    ;CS
        CCLK4  =  TISHD  TISHD                                                    ;CS

        BCLK8  =  WCKR   OPEN                                                     ;WCK
        CCLK8  =  WCKF   OPEN                                                     ;WCK

        BCLK9  =  TDSVA  OPEN                                                      ;DQ
        CCLK9  =  TDHVA  OPEN                                                      ;DQ

        BCLK10 =  TDSVA  OPEN                                                      ;DMI
        CCLK10 =  TDHVA  OPEN                                                      ;DMI

        BCLK11 =  TDSVA  OPEN                                                      ;RDQS
        CCLK11 =  TDHVA  OPEN                                                      ;RDQS

        STRB1  =  TSACE  OPEN                                                     ;TSAC
        STRB3  =  TSACE  OPEN                                                     ;TDQSCK
        STRB129 = TSACO  OPEN                                                     ;TSAC
        STRB131 = TSACO  OPEN                                                     ;TDQSCK





GOTO CONT


;;; CKR 2:1 Case
TFCHG2:
        ARGUMENT(TGRAT1,TGRAT2)

        TRATE =  TGRAT1
        TRATE2=  TGRAT2

       ;TS1 ---------------        
        TCLKR  =  TRATE*0.5+TRATE*0.0                                     
        TCLKD  =  TRATE*0.5+TRATE*0.5         
        WCKR   =  TRATE*0.5+TRATE*0.0         
        WCKF   =  TRATE*0.5+TRATE*0.5         
        TISHR  =  TRATE*0.5+TRATE*0.5         
        TISHD  =  TRATE*0.5+TRATE*1.0         
        TDSVA  =  TRATE*0.5+TRATE*0.0-TRATE*0.15;+450PS  
        TDHVA  =  TRATE*0.5+TRATE*0.5-TRATE*0.15;+450PS  
        TSACE  =  WCKR+1NS+TSAC+TRATE*0.4 ;1.56NS       
        TSACO  =  WCKF+1NS+TSAC+TRATE*0.4 ;1.56NS      
 
       ;TS2 ---------------                                                                   
        TCLKR2 =  TRATE2*0.5+TRATE2*0.0        
        TCLKD2 =  TRATE2*0.5+TRATE2*0.5        
        WCKR2  =  TRATE2*0.5+TRATE2*0.0        
        WCKF2  =  TRATE2*0.5+TRATE2*0.5        
        TISHR2 =  TRATE2*0.5+TRATE2*0.5        
        TISHD2 =  TRATE2*0.5+TRATE2*1.0        
        TDSVA2 =  TRATE2*0.5+TRATE2*0.0-TRATE*0.15;+450PS 
        TDHVA2 =  TRATE2*0.5+TRATE2*0.5-TRATE*0.15;+450PS 
        TSACE2 =  WCKR2+1NS+TSAC+TRATE*0.4 ;1.50NS      
        TSACO2 =  WCKF2+1NS+TSAC+TRATE*0.4 ;1.50NS      

       
        TIMING SET=1

        RATE   =  TRATE  TRATE2  TRATE  TRATE  TRATE  TRATE  TRATE  TRATE2       ;RATE
        BCLK1  =  TCLKR  TCLKR2  TCLKR  TCLKR  TCLKR  TCLKR  TCLKR  TCLKR2       ;CLK
        CCLK1  =  TCLKD  TCLKD2  TCLKD  TCLKD  TCLKD  TCLKD  TCLKD  TCLKD2       ;CLK

        BCLK2  =  TISHR  TISHR2  TISHR  TISHR  TISHR  TISHR  TISHR  TISHR2       ;CA
        CCLK2  =  TISHD  TISHD2  TISHD  TISHD  TISHD  TISHD  TISHD  TISHD2       ;CA

        BCLK3  =  TISHR  TISHR2  TISHR  TISHR  TISHR  TISHR  TISHR  TISHR2       ;CS
        CCLK3  =  TISHD  TISHD2  TISHD  TISHD  TISHD  TISHD  TISHD  TISHD2       ;CS

        BCLK4  =  TISHR  TISHR2  TISHR  TISHR  TISHR  TISHR  TISHR  TISHR2       ;CS
        CCLK4  =  TISHD  TISHD2  TISHD  TISHD  TISHD  TISHD  TISHD  TISHD2       ;CS

        BCLK8  =  WCKR   WCKR2   WCKR   WCKR   WCKR   WCKR   WCKR   WCKR2        ;WCK
        CCLK8  =  WCKF   WCKF2   WCKF   WCKF   WCKF   WCKF   WCKF   WCKF2        ;WCK

        BCLK9  =  TDSVA  TDSVA2  TDSVA  TDSVA  TDSVA  TDSVA  TDSVA  TDSVA2       ;DQ
        CCLK9  =  TDHVA  TDHVA2  TDHVA  TDHVA  TDHVA  TDHVA  TDHVA  TDHVA2       ;DQ

        BCLK10 =  TDSVA  TDSVA2  TDSVA  TDSVA  TDSVA  TDSVA  TDSVA  TDSVA2       ;DMI
        CCLK10 =  TDHVA  TDHVA2  TDHVA  TDHVA  TDHVA  TDHVA  TDHVA  TDHVA2       ;DMI

        BCLK11 =  TDSVA  TDSVA2  TDSVA  TDSVA  TDSVA  TDSVA  TDSVA  TDSVA2       ;RDQS
        CCLK11 =  TDHVA  TDHVA2  TDHVA  TDHVA  TDHVA  TDHVA  TDHVA  TDHVA2       ;RDQS

        STRB1  =  TSACE  TSACE2  TSACE  TSACE  TSACE  TSACE  TSACE  TSACE2       ;TSAC
        STRB3  =  TSACE  TSACE2  TSACE  TSACE  TSACE  TSACE  TSACE  TSACE2       ;TDQSCK
        STRB129 = TSACO  TSACO2  TSACO  TSACO  TSACO  TSACO  TSACO  TSACO2       ;TSAC
        STRB131 = TSACO  TSACO2  TSACO  TSACO  TSACO  TSACO  TSACO  TSACO2       ;TDQSCK

        TIMING SET=15  ;for Training

        RATE   =  TRATE  TRATE                                                    ;RATE
        BCLK1  =  TCLKR  TCLKR                                                    ;CLK
        CCLK1  =  TCLKD  TCLKD                                                    ;CLK

        BCLK2  =  TISHR  TISHR                                                    ;CA
        CCLK2  =  TISHD  TISHD                                                    ;CA

        BCLK3  =  TISHR  TISHR                                                    ;CS
        CCLK3  =  TISHD  TISHD                                                    ;CS

        BCLK4  =  TISHR  TISHR                                                    ;CS
        CCLK4  =  TISHD  TISHD                                                    ;CS

        BCLK8  =  WCKR   OPEN                                                     ;WCK
        CCLK8  =  WCKF   OPEN                                                     ;WCK

        BCLK9  =  TDSVA  TDSVA                                                    ;DQ
        CCLK9  =  TDHVA  TDHVA                                                    ;DQ

        BCLK10 =  TDSVA  TDSVA                                                    ;DMI
        CCLK10 =  TDHVA  TDHVA                                                    ;DMI

        BCLK11 =  TDSVA  TDSVA                                                    ;RDQS
        CCLK11 =  TDHVA  TDHVA                                                    ;RDQS

        STRB1  =  TSACE  OPEN                                                     ;TSAC
        STRB3  =  TSACE  OPEN                                                     ;TDQSCK
        STRB129 = TSACO  OPEN                                                     ;TSAC
        STRB131 = TSACO  OPEN                                                     ;TDQSCK

GOTO CONT

;;; CKR 2:1 Case
TFCHG2L:
        ARGUMENT(TGRAT1L,TGRAT2L)

        TRATE =  TGRAT1L
        TRATE2=  TGRAT2L

       ;TS1 ---------------        
        TCLKR  =  TRATE*0.5+TRATE*0.0                                     
        TCLKD  =  TRATE*0.5+TRATE*0.5         
        WCKR   =  TRATE*0.5+TRATE*0.0         
        WCKF   =  TRATE*0.5+TRATE*0.5         
        TISHR  =  TRATE*0.5+TRATE*0.5         
        TISHD  =  TRATE*0.5+TRATE*1.0         
        TDSVA  =  TRATE*0.5+TRATE*0.0;+450PS  
        TDHVA  =  TRATE*0.5+TRATE*0.5;+450PS  
        TSACE  =  TRATE*0.2+WCKR+1NS+TSAC ;1.56NS       
        TSACO  =  TRATE*0.2+WCKF+1NS+TSAC ;1.56NS      
 
       ;TS2 ---------------                                                                   
        TCLKR2 =  TRATE2*0.5+TRATE2*0.0        
        TCLKD2 =  TRATE2*0.5+TRATE2*0.5        
        WCKR2  =  TRATE2*0.5+TRATE2*0.0        
        WCKF2  =  TRATE2*0.5+TRATE2*0.5        
        TISHR2 =  TRATE2*0.5+TRATE2*0.5        
        TISHD2 =  TRATE2*0.5+TRATE2*1.0        
        TDSVA2 =  TRATE2*0.5+TRATE2*0.0;+450PS 
        TDHVA2 =  TRATE2*0.5+TRATE2*0.5;+450PS 
        TSACE2 =  WCKR2+1NS+TSAC ;1.50NS      
        TSACO2 =  WCKF2+1NS+TSAC ;1.50NS      

       
        TIMING SET=1

        RATE   =  TRATE  TRATE2  TRATE  TRATE  TRATE  TRATE  TRATE  TRATE2       ;RATE
        BCLK1  =  TCLKR  TCLKR2  TCLKR  TCLKR  TCLKR  TCLKR  TCLKR  TCLKR2       ;CLK
        CCLK1  =  TCLKD  TCLKD2  TCLKD  TCLKD  TCLKD  TCLKD  TCLKD  TCLKD2       ;CLK

        BCLK2  =  TISHR  TISHR2  TISHR  TISHR  TISHR  TISHR  TISHR  TISHR2       ;CA
        CCLK2  =  TISHD  TISHD2  TISHD  TISHD  TISHD  TISHD  TISHD  TISHD2       ;CA

        BCLK3  =  TISHR  TISHR2  TISHR  TISHR  TISHR  TISHR  TISHR  TISHR2       ;CS
        CCLK3  =  TISHD  TISHD2  TISHD  TISHD  TISHD  TISHD  TISHD  TISHD2       ;CS

        BCLK4  =  TISHR  TISHR2  TISHR  TISHR  TISHR  TISHR  TISHR  TISHR2       ;CS
        CCLK4  =  TISHD  TISHD2  TISHD  TISHD  TISHD  TISHD  TISHD  TISHD2       ;CS

        BCLK8  =  WCKR   WCKR2   WCKR   WCKR   WCKR   WCKR   WCKR   WCKR2        ;WCK
        CCLK8  =  WCKF   WCKF2   WCKF   WCKF   WCKF   WCKF   WCKF   WCKF2        ;WCK

        BCLK9  =  TDSVA  TDSVA2  TDSVA  TDSVA  TDSVA  TDSVA  TDSVA  TDSVA2       ;DQ
        CCLK9  =  TDHVA  TDHVA2  TDHVA  TDHVA  TDHVA  TDHVA  TDHVA  TDHVA2       ;DQ

        BCLK10 =  TDSVA  TDSVA2  TDSVA  TDSVA  TDSVA  TDSVA  TDSVA  TDSVA2       ;DMI
        CCLK10 =  TDHVA  TDHVA2  TDHVA  TDHVA  TDHVA  TDHVA  TDHVA  TDHVA2       ;DMI

        BCLK11 =  TDSVA  TDSVA2  TDSVA  TDSVA  TDSVA  TDSVA  TDSVA  TDSVA2       ;RDQS
        CCLK11 =  TDHVA  TDHVA2  TDHVA  TDHVA  TDHVA  TDHVA  TDHVA  TDHVA2       ;RDQS

        STRB1  =  TSACE  TSACE2  TSACE  TSACE  TSACE  TSACE  TSACE  TSACE2       ;TSAC
        STRB3  =  TSACE+1.5NS  TSACE2  TSACE  TSACE  TSACE  TSACE  TSACE  TSACE2       ;TDQSCK
        STRB129 = TSACO  TSACO2  TSACO  TSACO  TSACO  TSACO  TSACO  TSACO2       ;TSAC
        STRB131 = TSACO+1.5NS  TSACO2  TSACO  TSACO  TSACO  TSACO  TSACO  TSACO2       ;TDQSCK

        TIMING SET=15  ;for Training

        RATE   =  TRATE  TRATE                                                    ;RATE
        BCLK1  =  TCLKR  TCLKR                                                    ;CLK
        CCLK1  =  TCLKD  TCLKD                                                    ;CLK

        BCLK2  =  TISHR  TISHR                                                    ;CA
        CCLK2  =  TISHD  TISHD                                                    ;CA

        BCLK3  =  TISHR  TISHR                                                    ;CS
        CCLK3  =  TISHD  TISHD                                                    ;CS

        BCLK4  =  TISHR  TISHR                                                    ;CS
        CCLK4  =  TISHD  TISHD                                                    ;CS

        BCLK8  =  WCKR   OPEN                                                     ;WCK
        CCLK8  =  WCKF   OPEN                                                     ;WCK

        BCLK9  =  TDSVA  TDSVA                                                    ;DQ
        CCLK9  =  TDHVA  TDHVA                                                    ;DQ

        BCLK10 =  TDSVA  TDSVA                                                    ;DMI
        CCLK10 =  TDHVA  TDHVA                                                    ;DMI

        BCLK11 =  TDSVA  TDSVA                                                    ;RDQS
        CCLK11 =  TDHVA  TDHVA                                                    ;RDQS

        STRB1  =  TSACE  OPEN                                                     ;TSAC
        STRB3  =  TSACE  OPEN                                                     ;TDQSCK
        STRB129 = TSACO  OPEN                                                     ;TSAC
        STRB131 = TSACO  OPEN                                                     ;TDQSCK

GOTO CONT

TPISSR: SET ILMODE 1WAY
        TIMING SET = 1

    RATE   =   40NS   40NS  40NS  40NS  40NS  40NS  40NS  40NS  40NS  40NS  40NS  40NS  40NS  40NS  40NS  40NS

    CCLK1  =   30NS   30NS  30NS  30NS  30NS  30NS  30NS  30NS  30NS  30NS  30NS  30NS  30NS  30NS  30NS  30NS 
    BCLK2  =  0.3NS  0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS  ;CS

    BCLK3  =  0.3NS  0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS  ;DQ

    BCLK4  =  0.3NS  0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS  ;CA
    CCLK4  =   20NS   20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS 
    BCLK7  =  0.5NS  0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS  ;DM
    CCLK7  =   20NS   20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS

    CCLK9  =   20NS   20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS 


    BCLK11 =   10NS   10NS  10NS  10NS  10NS  10NS  10NS  10NS  10NS  10NS  10NS  10NS  10NS  10NS  10NS  10NS  ;CK
    CCLK11 =   30NS   30NS  30NS  30NS  30NS  30NS  30NS  30NS  30NS  30NS  30NS  30NS  30NS  30NS  30NS  30NS

    TNAME="TPISSR"

    GOTO CONT

TPISST: SET ILMODE 1WAY
        TIMING SET = 1
