    RATE   =   40NS   40NS  40NS  40NS  40NS  40NS  40NS 200NS  40NS  40NS  40NS  40NS  40NS  40NS  40NS  40NS 
    BCLK1  =   10NS   10NS  10NS  10NS  10NS  10NS  10NS  10NS  10NS  10NS  10NS  10NS  10NS  10NS  10NS  10NS  ;CK
    CCLK1  =   30NS   30NS  30NS  30NS  30NS  30NS  30NS  30NS  30NS  30NS  30NS  30NS  30NS  30NS  30NS  30NS 
    BCLK2  =  0.3NS  0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS  ;CS
    CCLK2  =   20NS   20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS 
    BCLK3  =  0.3NS  0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS  ;DQ
    CCLK3  =   20NS   20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS 
    BCLK4  =  0.3NS  0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS 0.3NS  ;CA
    CCLK4  =   20NS   20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS 
    BCLK7  =  0.5NS  0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS  ;DM
    CCLK7  =   20NS   20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS 
    BCLK8  =  0.5NS  0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS  ;CKE
    CCLK8  =   20NS   20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS 
    BCLK9  =  0.5NS  0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS 0.5NS  ;RESET
    CCLK9  =   20NS   20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS  20NS 
                                                                                                               
    STRB1  =   20NS   11NS  11NS  11NS  11NS  11NS  11NS  11NS  11NS  11NS  11NS  11NS  11NS  11NS  11NS  11NS 



    TNAME="TPISSR"

    GOTO CONT




TDDR:    
ARGUMENT(WCKRATE,CKRATIO)
     SET ILMODE 1WAY
     TIMING SET = 1
     
     GOSUB DDRTIMVAR(WCKRATE,CKRATIO)

;   TIME   =  tCK      tCK      tCK      tCK      tCK      tCK      tCK      tCK     tCK      ;
    RATE   =  FTRATE   FTRATE   FTRATE   FTRATE   FTRATE   FTRATE   FTRATE   FTRATE  FTRATE  ;
    BCLK1  =  FTCKR    FTCKR    FTCKR    FTCKR    FTCKR    FTCKR    FTCKR    FTCKR   FTCKR    ; CK RISING/FALLING
    CCLK1  =  FTCKF    FTCKF    FTCKF    FTCKF    FTCKF    FTCKF    FTCKF    FTCKF   FTCKF    ; CK FALLING
    BCLK2  =  FTCSR    FTCSR    FTCSR    FTCSR    FTCSR    FTCSR    FTCSR    FTCSR   FTCSR    ; CS 
    CCLK2  =  FTCSF    FTCSF    FTCSF    FTCSF    FTCSF    FTCSF    FTCSF    FTCSF   FTCSF    ;
    BCLK3  =  FTDQ1    FTDQ1    FTDQ1    FTDQ1    FTDQ1    FTDQ1    FTDQ1    FTDQ1   FTDQ1    ; DQ 1ST
    CCLK3  =  FTDQ2    FTDQ2    FTDQ2    FTDQ2    FTDQ2    FTDQ2    FTDQ2    FTDQ2   FTDQ2    ; DQ 2ND
    BCLK4  =  FTCAR    FTCAR    FTCAR    FTCAR    FTCAR    FTCAR    FTCAR    FTCAR   FTCAR    ; CA 
    CCLK4  =  FTCAF    FTCAF    FTCAF    FTCAF    FTCAF    FTCAF    FTCAF    FTCAF   FTCAF    ;
    BCLK5  =  FTWCKR   FTWCKR   FTWCKRE  FTWCKRL  FTWCKR   FTWCKR   FTWCKR   FTWCKR  FTWCKR   ; WCK RISING
    CCLK5  =  FTWCKF   FTWCKF   FTWCKFE  FTWCKFL  FTWCKF   FTWCKF   FTWCKF   FTWCKF  FTWCKF   ; WCK FALLING
    BCLK7  =  FTDM1    FTDM1    FTDM1    FTDM1    FTDM1    FTDM1    FTDM1    FTDM1   FTDM1    ; DM
    CCLK7  =  FTDM2    FTDM2    FTDM2    FTDM2    FTDM2    FTDM2    FTDM2    FTDM2   FTDM2    ;
    BCLK9  =  FTRESET  FTRESET  FTRESET  FTRESET  FTRESET  FTRESET  FTRESET  FTRESET FTRESET  ; RESET
    CCLK9  =  FTRESET  FTRESET  FTRESET  FTRESET  FTRESET  FTRESET  FTRESET  FTRESET FTRESET  ;
                                                                                              ;
    STRB1  =  FTSTRB1  FTSTRB1  FTSTRB1  FTSTRB1  FTSTRB1  FTSTRB1  FTSTRB1  FTSTRB1 FTSTRB1  ;
    STRB3  =  FTSTRB1  FTSTRB1  FTSTRB1  FTSTRB1  FTSTRB1  FTSTRB1  FTSTRB1  FTSTRB1 FTSTRB1  ;
    STRB129=  FTSTRB2  FTSTRB2  FTSTRB2  FTSTRB2  FTSTRB2  FTSTRB2  FTSTRB2  FTSTRB2 FTSTRB2  ;
    STRB131=  FTSTRB2  FTSTRB2  FTSTRB2  FTSTRB2  FTSTRB2  FTSTRB2  FTSTRB2  FTSTRB2 FTSTRB2  ;


    TNAME="TDDR__"

GOTO CONT

TCHIPP: SET ILMODE 1WAY
        TIMING SET = 1

;   TIME  =   ----   ----   ----
    RATE  =   40NS  100NS  100NS
    BCLK1 =   10NS   10NS   10NS
    CCLK1 =   30NS   30NS   30NS
    BCLK2 =  0.3NS  0.3NS  0.3NS
    CCLK2 =   20NS   20NS   20NS
    BCLK3 =   20NS   20NS   20NS
    CCLK3 =   40NS   40NS   40NS
    BCLK4 =  0.3NS  0.3NS  0.3NS
    CCLK4 =   20NS   20NS   20NS
    BCLK5 =    0NS    0NS    0NS
    CCLK5 =   20NS   20NS   20NS
    BCLK7 =  0.5NS  0.5NS  0.5NS
    CCLK7 =   20NS   20NS   20NS
    BCLK8 =  0.5NS  0.5NS  0.5NS
    CCLK8 =   20NS   20NS   20NS
    BCLK9 =  0.5NS  0.5NS  0.5NS
    CCLK9 =   20NS   20NS   20NS

;   DREL1 =    0NS    0NS    0NS
;   DRET1 =    0NS    0NS    0NS
    STRB1 =   15NS    0NS   50NS

    TNAME="TCHIPP"

    GOTO CONT

DDRTIMVAR:
ARGUMENT(FWCKRATE,CKRATO)

;TCK:                     |<------------------------ 1 TCK  --------------------->|   
;LINE:      |<  1 line   >|<  1 line   >|<  1 line   >|<  1 line   >|<  1 line   >|<  1 line   >|<  1 line   >| 
;CK:    __________________                             ___________________________                             _______    
;                         |___________________________|                           |___________________________|       
;WCK:CK      _____________               _____________               _____________               _____________            
;  2:1  ____|             |_____________|             |_____________|             |_____________|             |_______
;WCK:CK ____        ______        ______        ______        ______        ______        ______        ______            
;  4:1      |______|      |______|      |______|      |______|      |______|      |______|      |______|      |______|



; REQUIRED TIMING  ( -- CODING --)
;CK NRZB    H          -->|<--          L          -->|<            H          -->|<--          L          -->|<--   
;CS NRZB    |<--          X          -->|<--          X          -->|<--          X          -->|<--          X        
;CA NRZB    |<--         CAF         -->|<--         CAR         -->|<--         CAF         -->|<--         CAR       
 
; CODING             
;CK NRZB    H          -->|<--          L          -->|<            H          -->|<--          L          -->|<--   
;CS NRZB    X          -->|<--          X          -->|<--          X          -->|<--          X          -->|<--
;CA NRZB   CAF         -->|<--         CAR         -->|<--         CAF         -->|<--         CAR         -->|<--

;CS/CA <= CK + 1 LINE


    FTRATE = FWCKRATE     
         
    FTCKR  = FWCKRATE*1.0  
    FTCKF  = FWCKRATE*2.0  
    FTCSR  = FWCKRATE*0.0  
    FTCSF  = FWCKRATE*1.0  
    FTCAR  = FWCKRATE*0.0  
    FTCAF  = FWCKRATE*1.0  

    FTWCKR = FWCKRATE*1.0  
    FTWCKF = FWCKRATE*1.5

    FTWCKRE= FWCKRATE*0.9  
    FTWCKFE= FWCKRATE*1.4 

    FTWCKRL= FWCKRATE*1.1  
    FTWCKFL= FWCKRATE*1.6 


    FTDQ1  = FWCKRATE*0.75
    FTDQ2  = FWCKRATE*1.25
    FTDM1  = FWCKRATE*0.75
    FTDM2  = FWCKRATE*1.25
  
    FTRESET= FWCKRATE*0.0  

    FTSTRB1= FWCKRATE*0.6  
    FTSTRB2= FWCKRATE*1.1  
    
    IF CKRATO=2 THEN ENTRY
        FTCKR  = FWCKRATE*0.5  
        FTCKF  = FWCKRATE*1.0  
        FTCSR  = FWCKRATE*0.0  
        FTCSF  = FWCKRATE*0.5  
        FTCAR  = FWCKRATE*0.0  
        FTCAF  = FWCKRATE*0.5  
        
        FTWCKR = FWCKRATE*0.5  
        FTWCKF = FWCKRATE*1.0
        
        FTDQ1  = FWCKRATE*0.25
        FTDQ2  = FWCKRATE*0.75
        FTDM1  = FWCKRATE*0.25
        FTDM2  = FWCKRATE*0.75
        
        FTRESET= FWCKRATE*0.0  
        
        FTSTRB1= FWCKRATE*0.25 
        FTSTRB2= FWCKRATE*0.75 
     EXIT
     
GOTO CONT


MR_SETTING:

; --- common -----
        REG MPAT YT   = MR1_WL*#10+#0                                                   ; (MR1)  -   ,           CK Diff, WL6     
        IF TSPEED=1600 THEN REG MPAT YT =MR1_WL*#10+#8                                  ; (MR1)  -   ,           CK Single     

;       IF CUSFLG=3 THEN REG MPAT YT   = #91                                            ; (MR1) BL32 , WCK Diff, CK Diff, WL8  
                                                                                       
        REG MPAT YT2  = MR2_NWR*#10+MR2_RL                                              ; (MR2)  RL12, nWR29 3200Mbps                      
                                                                                       
        REG MPAT YT3  = MR3_PDDS                                                        ; (MR3)  RZQ/6, 4Bank/4BG, SET_A, DBI_OFF 
        
        MR3_BKORG=0
        IF FAPATN(5,1)="6" THEN MR3_BKORG = #10  ; (MR3)  RZQ/6, 16Bank   
        IF FAPATN(5,1)="4" THEN MR3_BKORG = #00  ; (MR3)  RZQ/6, 4Bank/4BG
        IF FAPATN(5,1)="8" THEN MR3_BKORG = #08  ; (MR3)  RZQ/6, 8Bank    
 
        MR3_WLSET=0
        IF WLSET(1)="B"  THEN MR3_WLSET=1

        REG MPAT YT3  = MR3_BKORG+MR3_PDDS+#80*MR3_WDBI+#40*MR3_RDBI+#20*MR3_WLSET  ; (MR3)  RZQ/6, 8Bank    , SET_A, DBI_OFF   
        REG MPAT XT3  = MR3_BKORG+MR3_PDDS+#80*MR3_WDBI+#40+#20*MR3_WLSET           ; (MR3)  RZQ/6, 8Bank    , SET_A, DBI_OFF   

        IF MR22_RECC=#1      THEN REG MPAT YT3  = MR3_BKORG+MR3_PDDS+#80*MR3_WDBI+#20*MR3_WLSET ; (MR3)  RZQ/6, 8Bank    , SET_A, DBI_OFF   
        IF FAPATN(7,3)="DCF" THEN REG MPAT YT3  = MR3_BKORG+MR3_PDDS+#80*MR3_WDBI+#20*MR3_WLSET ; (MR3)  RZQ/6, 8Bank    , SET_A, DBI_OFF   

;       REG MPAT YT4  = #80                   ; (MR13) Thermal Offset No, VRO Normal, Data Mask EN, CBT Mode1, Single 1.05V VDD2 rail
;       IF DVFSC="E" THEN REG MPAT YT4  = #00 ; (MR13) Thermal Offset No, VRO Normal, Data Mask EN, CBT Mode1, Dual VDD2(1.05V & 0.9V) rail

        REG MPAT YT4  = #00                   ; (MR13) Thermal Offset No, VRO Normal, Data Mask EN, CBT Mode1, Dual Rail (200907)
        REG MPAT YT5  = MR41_NTODT*#20+#0     ; (MR41) NT DQ ODT RZQ/4, PRR Disable,                                                 
                                              
        REG MPAT YT6  = #01                   ; (MR16) FSP-OP0, FSP-WR1                                                              
        REG MPAT YT9  = #61                   ; (MR16) FSP-OP0, FSP-WR1, CBT_EN_FSP1, VREF Fast, CK Rising                           
   
        IF WCKCKRATIO=2                 THEN REG MPAT YT8  = #80+#10*MR18_WCKALWAYSON+MR18_WCKODT  ; (MR18) WCK Term RZQ/4, Half-rate sync, CKR 2:1
        IF WCKCKRATIO=4 AND TSPEED<=4500 THEN REG MPAT YT8  = #00+#10*MR18_WCKALWAYSON+MR18_WCKODT  ; (MR18) WCK Term RZQ/4, Full-rate sync, CKR 2:1
        IF WCKCKRATIO=4 AND TSPEED>4500 THEN REG MPAT YT8  = #08+#10*MR18_WCKALWAYSON+MR18_WCKODT  ; (MR18) WCK Term RZQ/4, Full-rate sync, CKR 2:1

;       REG MPAT YT7  = #05                   ; (MR17) SOCODT, RZQ/5, CLK_EN. CA_EN                                                  
        REG MPAT YT7  = MR17_SOCODT+#0        ; (MR17) SOCODT, RZQ/5, CLK_EN. CA_EN                                                  
                                              
        REG MPAT YT10 = #00                   ; (MR10) RDQS Post Toggle, WCKPST 2.5tWCK, RDQS PRE 4*tWCK, Toggle 0, RDQS PST 0.5*WCK 
;       REG MPAT YT11 = #44                   ; (MR11) DQ_ODT RZQ/4, CAODT RZQ/4                                                     
        REG MPAT YT11 = MR11_DQODT+MR11_CAODT*#10+MR11_NTODTEN*#8   ; (MR11) DQ_ODT RZQ/4, CAODT RZQ/4                                                     

;       REG MPAT YT12 = (PCA*100-15)*2        ; (MR12) VREFCA      , 25.0%                                                             
;       REG MPAT YT14 = (PDQ*100-15)*2        ; (MR14) VREFDQ[7:0] , 25.0%                                                             
;       REG MPAT YT15 = (PDQ*100-15)*2        ; (MR15) VREFDQ[15:8], 25.0%                                                             
        REG MPAT YT12 = VREFCAVAL             ; (MR12) VREFCA      , 25.0%                                                             

        REG MPAT YT14 = VREFBYTE0             ; (MR14) VREFDQ[7:0] , 14(0.25)                       
        REG MPAT YT15 = VREFBYTE1             ; (MR15) VREFDQ[15:8], 14(0.25) 
        
        REG MPAT D1H  = VREFBYTE0
        
        IF VREF_VAR="Y" THEN ENTRY

           REG MPAT YT14 = VREFVAR0             ; (MR14) VREFDQ[7:0] , 14(0.25)                       
           REG MPAT YT15 = VREFVAR0             ; (MR15) VREFDQ[15:8], 14(0.25) 
        
        
        EXIT

        MR19=#0
        IF DVFSC="E" AND MR1_WL<#3 THEN MR19=MR19+#1
        IF DVFSQ="E" AND MR1_WL<#6 THEN MR19=MR19+#4

        IF WCK_OSC<>#0 THEN ENTRY
           IF TSPEED>3500 THEN MR19=MR19+#10
        EXIT


;       IF DVFSC="E" AND TSPEED <=1600   THEN    CCFLG = CCFLG.OR.#80       ;  EN                    
;       IF DVFSQ="E" AND TSPEED <=3200   THEN    CCFLG = CCFLG.OR.#40       ;         EN             

        MR20=#02   ; RDQS / WCK ALL ENABLE
        IF TSPEED=1600 THEN MR20=#06    ;; Single Ended


        REG MPAT YH   = MR19 
        REG MPAT YH_2 = MR20 
        REG MPAT YH_3 =(MR21_WDCFE*#10+MR21_RDCFE*#20+MR21_WXFE*#40)
        REG MPAT YH_4 =(MR22_WECC*#10+MR22_RECC*#40)
      

        REG MPAT YT13 = #05                                    ; (MR16) FSP-OP1, FSP-WR1, CBT_DIS                                                     
        IF TSPEED>3500 THEN REG MPAT YT13 = #45                ; (MR16) FSP-OP1, FSP-WR1, CBT_DIS                                                     
        
; ----------------

GOTO CONT

WLRLCAL:
ARGUMENT(I_CKR,I_WL,I_RL,I_DVFSC,I_WLSET,I_DELAY) 
 
   CWL=0 & CRL=0 
   DVFSC_DIFF=0
   RDBI_DIFF=0    
   
    IF I_DELAY="Y" THEN ENTRY                   

       IF I_CKR=2 THEN ENTRY                                                                                          ; WL  DVFSC Disable                          
          IF I_WLSET="A" THEN ENTRY                                                                                   ; CKR    OP     A  B    CKR    OP     A  B      
             WLCAL(1)=4   & WLCAL(2)=4   & WLCAL(3)=6   & WLCAL(4)=8   & WLCAL(5)=8   & WLCAL(6)=10    ; CKR2 OP0~5   ; --------------------- ---------------------
          EXIT                                                                                                        ; 2:1 #0 0000B  4  4    4:1 #0 0000B  2  2   
          IF I_WLSET="B" THEN ENTRY                                                                                   ;     #1 0001B  4  6        #1 0001B  2  3      
             WLCAL(1)=4   & WLCAL(2)=6   & WLCAL(3)=8   & WLCAL(4)=10  & WLCAL(5)=14  & WLCAL(6)=16    ; CKR2 OP0~5   ;     #2 0010B  6  8        #2 0010B  3  4   
          EXIT                                                                                                        ;     #3 0011B  8 10        #3 0011B  4  5      
          WLCAL(7)=0   & WLCAL(8)=0   & WLCAL(9)=0   & WLCAL(10)=0  & WLCAL(11)=0  & WLCAL(12)=0       ; CKR2 OP6~B   ;     #4 0100B  8 14        #4 0100B  4  7   
       EXIT                                                                                                           ;     #5 0101B 10 16        #5 0101B  5  8   
       IF I_CKR=4 THEN ENTRY                                                                                          ; ---------------------     #6 0110B  6  9   
          IF I_WLSET="A" THEN ENTRY                                                                                   ;                           #7 0111B  6 11      
             WLCAL(1)=2   & WLCAL(2)=2   & WLCAL(3)=3   & WLCAL(4)=4   & WLCAL(5)=4   & WLCAL(6)=5     ; CKR4 OP0~5   ;                           #8 1000B  7 12   
             WLCAL(7)=6   & WLCAL(8)=6   & WLCAL(9)=7   & WLCAL(10)=8  & WLCAL(11)=9  & WLCAL(12)=9    ; CKR4 OP6~B   ;                           #9 1001B  8 14   
             WLCAL(13)=11 & WLCAL(14)=12                                                                              ;                           #A 1010B  9 15
          EXIT                                                                                                        ;                           #B 1011B  9 16   
          IF I_WLSET="B" THEN ENTRY                                                                                   ;                           #C 1100B 11 19      
             WLCAL(1)=2   & WLCAL(2)=3   & WLCAL(3)=4   & WLCAL(4)=5   & WLCAL(5)=7   & WLCAL(6)=8     ; CKR4 OP0~5   ;                           #D 1101B 12 22  
             WLCAL(7)=9   & WLCAL(8)=11  & WLCAL(9)=12  & WLCAL(10)=14 & WLCAL(11)=15 & WLCAL(12)=16   ; CKR4 OP6~B   ;                                           
             WLCAL(13)=19 & WLCAL(14)=22
          EXIT 
       EXIT                                                                                                                
       
       RLSET=0
       IF MR21_RDCFE=#1 OR MR3_RDBI=#1 THEN RLSET=RLSET+1
       IF MR22_RECC=#1 THEN RLSET=0
       IF BYTEMODE="Y" THEN RLSET=RLSET+1
      
;      WRITE /,MR3_RDBI,DVFSC,RLSET,I_RL
     
       IF I_CKR=2 THEN ENTRY                                                                                              
          IF MR22_RECC<>#1  AND DVFSC="D" THEN ENTRY   ; Link ECC off case (DVFSC disabled)
             IF RLSET=0 THEN ENTRY & RLCAL(1)=6   & RLCAL(2)=8   & RLCAL(3)=10  & RLCAL(4)=12  & RLCAL(5)=16  & RLCAL(6)=18 & EXIT  ; CKR2 OP0~5 
             IF RLSET=1 THEN ENTRY & RLCAL(1)=6   & RLCAL(2)=8   & RLCAL(3)=10  & RLCAL(4)=14  & RLCAL(5)=16  & RLCAL(6)=20 & EXIT  ; CKR2 OP0~5 
             IF RLSET=2 THEN ENTRY & RLCAL(1)=6   & RLCAL(2)=8   & RLCAL(3)=12  & RLCAL(4)=14  & RLCAL(5)=18  & RLCAL(6)=20 & EXIT  ; CKR2 OP0~5 
          EXIT                                                                                                                   
          IF MR22_RECC<>#1  AND DVFSC="E" THEN ENTRY   ; Link ECC off case (DVFSC enable)
             IF RLSET=0 THEN ENTRY & RLCAL(1)=6   & RLCAL(2)=8   & RLCAL(3)=12  & RLCAL(4)=0   & RLCAL(5)=0   & RLCAL(6)=0  & EXIT   ; CKR2 OP0~5 
             IF RLSET=1 THEN ENTRY & RLCAL(1)=6   & RLCAL(2)=10  & RLCAL(3)=12  & RLCAL(4)=0   & RLCAL(5)=0   & RLCAL(6)=0  & EXIT   ; CKR2 OP0~5 
             IF RLSET=2 THEN ENTRY & RLCAL(1)=6   & RLCAL(2)=10  & RLCAL(3)=14  & RLCAL(4)=0   & RLCAL(5)=0   & RLCAL(6)=0  & EXIT   ; CKR2 OP0~5 
          EXIT                                                                                                                   
          IF MR22_RECC=#1   AND DVFSC="D" THEN ENTRY   ; Link ECC on case (DVFSC disabled))
                                     RLCAL(1)=0   & RLCAL(2)=0   & RLCAL(3)=0   & RLCAL(4)=0   & RLCAL(5)=0   & RLCAL(6)=0           ; CKR2 OP0~5 
          EXIT  
                                     RLCAL(7)=0   & RLCAL(8)=0   & RLCAL(9)=0   & RLCAL(10)=0  & RLCAL(11)=0  & RLCAL(12)=0                            
       EXIT    
     
                                                                      
       IF I_CKR=4 THEN ENTRY                                                                                              
          IF MR22_RECC<>#1  AND DVFSC="D" THEN ENTRY   ; Link ECC off case (DVFSC disabled)
             IF RLSET=0 THEN ENTRY & RLCAL(1)=3   & RLCAL(2)=4   & RLCAL(3)=5   & RLCAL(4)=6   & RLCAL(5)=8   & RLCAL(6)=9           ; CKR2 OP0~5 
                                     RLCAL(7)=10  & RLCAL(8)=12  & RLCAL(9)=13  & RLCAL(10)=15 & RLCAL(11)=16 & RLCAL(12)=17         ; CKR4 OP6~B                          
                                     RLCAL(13)=20 & RLCAL(14)=23                                                             & EXIT  ; CKR4 OPC~D                          
             IF RLSET=1 THEN ENTRY & RLCAL(1)=3   & RLCAL(2)=4   & RLCAL(3)=5   & RLCAL(4)=7   & RLCAL(5)=8   & RLCAL(6)=10          ; CKR2 OP0~5 
                                     RLCAL(7)=11  & RLCAL(8)=13  & RLCAL(9)=14  & RLCAL(10)=16 & RLCAL(11)=17 & RLCAL(12)=18         ; CKR4 OP6~B                          
                                     RLCAL(13)=22 & RLCAL(14)=25                                                             & EXIT  ; CKR4 OPC~D                          
             IF RLSET=2 THEN ENTRY & RLCAL(1)=3   & RLCAL(2)=4   & RLCAL(3)=6   & RLCAL(4)=6   & RLCAL(5)=9   & RLCAL(6)=10          ; CKR2 OP0~5 
                                     RLCAL(7)=12  & RLCAL(8)=14  & RLCAL(9)=15  & RLCAL(10)=17 & RLCAL(11)=19 & RLCAL(12)=20         ; CKR4 OP6~B                          
                                     RLCAL(13)=24 & RLCAL(14)=26                                                             & EXIT  ; CKR4 OPC~D                          
          EXIT                                                                                                                   
          IF MR22_RECC<>#1  AND DVFSC="E" THEN ENTRY   ; Link ECC off case (DVFSC enable)
             IF RLSET=0 THEN ENTRY & RLCAL(1)=3   & RLCAL(2)=4   & RLCAL(3)=6   & RLCAL(4)=0   & RLCAL(5)=0   & RLCAL(6)=0   & EXIT  ; CKR2 OP0~5 
             IF RLSET=1 THEN ENTRY & RLCAL(1)=3   & RLCAL(2)=5   & RLCAL(3)=6   & RLCAL(4)=0   & RLCAL(5)=0   & RLCAL(6)=0   & EXIT  ; CKR2 OP0~5 
             IF RLSET=2 THEN ENTRY & RLCAL(1)=3   & RLCAL(2)=5   & RLCAL(3)=7   & RLCAL(4)=0   & RLCAL(5)=0   & RLCAL(6)=0   & EXIT  ; CKR2 OP0~5 
                                     RLCAL(7)=0   & RLCAL(8)=0   & RLCAL(9)=0   & RLCAL(10)=0  & RLCAL(11)=0  & RLCAL(12)=0                                 
          EXIT                                                                                                                   
          IF MR22_RECC=#1   AND DVFSC="D" THEN ENTRY   ; Link ECC on case (DVFSC disabled))
                                     RLCAL(1)=0   & RLCAL(2)=0   & RLCAL(3)=0   & RLCAL(4)=0   & RLCAL(5)=0   & RLCAL(6)=0           ; CKR2 OP0~5 
                    ; pattern -1
             IF RLSET=0 THEN ENTRY & RLCAL(7)=12  & RLCAL(8)=13  & RLCAL(9)=14  & RLCAL(10)=16 & RLCAL(11)=17 & RLCAL(12)=18 & RLCAL(13)=00 & RLCAL(14)=00 & EXIT  ; CKR4 OP6~B    & RLCAL(9)=15  & RLCAL(10)=17 & RLCAL(11)=18 & RLCAL(12)=19 & RLCAL(13)=23 & RLCAL(14)=26 & 
             IF RLSET=1 THEN ENTRY & RLCAL(7)=13  & RLCAL(8)=14  & RLCAL(9)=15  & RLCAL(10)=17 & RLCAL(11)=19 & RLCAL(12)=20 & RLCAL(13)=00 & RLCAL(14)=00 & EXIT  ; CKR4 OP6~B    & RLCAL(9)=16  & RLCAL(10)=18 & RLCAL(11)=20 & RLCAL(12)=21 & RLCAL(13)=24 & RLCAL(14)=28 &                     
          EXIT                                                                                                                   
       EXIT                                                                                                                
       CWL=WLCAL(I_WL+1)*WCKCKRATIO
       CRL=RLCAL(I_RL+1)*WCKCKRATIO

       IF RLPLUS>0 THEN CRL=(RLCAL(I_RL+1)+RLPLUS*2)*WCKCKRATIO
       IF CRL=80 THEN CRL=79

    EXIT
 

;   CWL=CWL*WCKCKRATIO
;   CRL=CRL*WCKCKRATIO


    
;   DVFSC_DIFF=DVFSC_DIFF*WCKCKRATIO
;   RDBI_DIFF=RDBI_DIFF*WCKCKRATIO
    
;   IF DVFSC="E" THEN CRL=CRL+DVFSC_DIFF

;   WRITE /,"WL LINE DELAY=",CWL," RL LINE DELAY=",CRL," CKR=",I_CKR," DVFSC=",I_DVFSC

GOTO CONT

TEST_TMRS_SETTING:

;    TMRS_1="T0000" & TMRS_2="T0000" & TMRS_3="T0000" & TMRS_4="T0000" & TMRS_5="T0000" & TMRS_6="T0000" & TMRS_7="T0000" & TMRS_8="T0000" & TMRS_9="T0000" &  TMRS_A="T0000" 
;    T_PC=0 & T_PS=0 & T_PG=0 
;    T_C=0  & T_S=0  & T_G=0 
     
        ; PHASE 1   0      0      0     ; PHASE 2    1      2      0
;  X12~X14  :     #01000 #01000 #01000             #02000 #04000 #01000 

      REG MPAT D1B_2=#00000 &   REG MPAT D1C_2=#0000 &   REG MPAT D1D_2=#0000 &   REG MPAT D1E_2=#0000 &   REG MPAT D1F_2=#0000     
      REG MPAT D1G_2=#00000 &   REG MPAT D1H_2=#0000 &   REG MPAT D2B_2=#0000 &   REG MPAT D2C_2=#0000 &   REG MPAT D2D_2=#0000     
      REG MPAT D1B_3=#00000 &   REG MPAT D1C_3=#0000 &   REG MPAT D1D_3=#0000 &   REG MPAT D1E_3=#0000 &   REG MPAT D1F_3=#0000    
      REG MPAT D1G_3=#00000 &   REG MPAT D1H_3=#0000 &   REG MPAT D2B_3=#0000 &   REG MPAT D2C_3=#0000 &   REG MPAT D2D_3=#0000    
      REG MPAT D1B_4=#00000 &   REG MPAT D1C_4=#0000 &   REG MPAT D1D_4=#0000 &   REG MPAT D1E_4=#0000 &   REG MPAT D1F_4=#0000  
      REG MPAT D1G_4=#00000 &   REG MPAT D1H_4=#0000 &   REG MPAT D2B_4=#0000 &   REG MPAT D2C_4=#0000 &   REG MPAT D2D_4=#0000    

;  IF TMRS_1<>"T0000" THEN ENTRY

;     T_C=0       & T_S=0       & T_G=0 
;     T_C=NUMERIC(TMRS_1(2,4),16)
;                                     T_PC=#00000 & T_PS=#00000 & T_PG=#00000 
;     IF TMRS_1(2,1)="1" THEN ENTRY & T_PC=#01000 & T_PS=#01000 & T_PG=#01000 & EXIT  ;PHASE1 X12~X14
;     IF TMRS_1(2,1)="2" THEN ENTRY & T_PC=#02000 & T_PS=#04000 & T_PG=#01000 & EXIT  ;PHASE2 X12~X14
;     IF TMRS_1(3,1)<>"A" THEN T_C=T_PC+2^NUMERIC(TMRS_1(3,1))
;     IF TMRS_1(3,1)="A"  THEN T_C=T_PC+#0600
;     IF TMRS_1(4,1)<>"A" THEN T_S=T_PS+2^NUMERIC(TMRS_1(4,1))
;     IF TMRS_1(4,1)="A"  THEN T_S=T_PS+#0600
;     IF TMRS_1(5,1)<>"A" THEN T_G=T_PG+2^NUMERIC(TMRS_1(5,1))
;     IF TMRS_1(5,1)="A"  THEN T_G=T_PG+#0600
;     REG MPAT D1B_2=T_C
;     REG MPAT D1B_3=T_S
;     REG MPAT D1B_4=T_G 
;  EXIT
   T_P=0
   T_C=0
   IF TMRS_1<>"T0000"  THEN ENTRY & GOSUB TMRS_TO_VAR(TMRS_1)  &  REG MPAT D1B_2=T_P+T_C & EXIT
   IF TMRS_2<>"T0000"  THEN ENTRY & GOSUB TMRS_TO_VAR(TMRS_2)  &  REG MPAT D1C_2=T_P+T_C & EXIT
   IF TMRS_3<>"T0000"  THEN ENTRY & GOSUB TMRS_TO_VAR(TMRS_3)  &  REG MPAT D1D_2=T_P+T_C & EXIT
   IF TMRS_4<>"T0000"  THEN ENTRY & GOSUB TMRS_TO_VAR(TMRS_4)  &  REG MPAT D1E_2=T_P+T_C & EXIT
   IF TMRS_5<>"T0000"  THEN ENTRY & GOSUB TMRS_TO_VAR(TMRS_5)  &  REG MPAT D1F_2=T_P+T_C & EXIT
   IF TMRS_6<>"T0000"  THEN ENTRY & GOSUB TMRS_TO_VAR(TMRS_6)  &  REG MPAT D1G_2=T_P+T_C & EXIT
   IF TMRS_7<>"T0000"  THEN ENTRY & GOSUB TMRS_TO_VAR(TMRS_7)  &  REG MPAT D1H_2=T_P+T_C & EXIT
   IF TMRS_8<>"T0000"  THEN ENTRY & GOSUB TMRS_TO_VAR(TMRS_8)  &  REG MPAT D2B_2=T_P+T_C & EXIT
   IF TMRS_9<>"T0000"  THEN ENTRY & GOSUB TMRS_TO_VAR(TMRS_9)  &  REG MPAT D2C_2=T_P+T_C & EXIT
   IF TMRS_A<>"T0000"  THEN ENTRY & GOSUB TMRS_TO_VAR(TMRS_A)  &  REG MPAT D2D_2=T_P+T_C & EXIT
   IF TMRS_11<>"T0000" THEN ENTRY & GOSUB TMRS_TO_VAR(TMRS_11) &  REG MPAT D1B_3=T_P+T_C & EXIT
   IF TMRS_12<>"T0000" THEN ENTRY & GOSUB TMRS_TO_VAR(TMRS_12) &  REG MPAT D1C_3=T_P+T_C & EXIT
   IF TMRS_13<>"T0000" THEN ENTRY & GOSUB TMRS_TO_VAR(TMRS_13) &  REG MPAT D1D_3=T_P+T_C & EXIT
   IF TMRS_14<>"T0000" THEN ENTRY & GOSUB TMRS_TO_VAR(TMRS_14) &  REG MPAT D1E_3=T_P+T_C & EXIT
   IF TMRS_15<>"T0000" THEN ENTRY & GOSUB TMRS_TO_VAR(TMRS_15) &  REG MPAT D1F_3=T_P+T_C & EXIT
   IF TMRS_16<>"T0000" THEN ENTRY & GOSUB TMRS_TO_VAR(TMRS_16) &  REG MPAT D1G_3=T_P+T_C & EXIT
   IF TMRS_17<>"T0000" THEN ENTRY & GOSUB TMRS_TO_VAR(TMRS_17) &  REG MPAT D1H_3=T_P+T_C & EXIT
   IF TMRS_18<>"T0000" THEN ENTRY & GOSUB TMRS_TO_VAR(TMRS_18) &  REG MPAT D2B_3=T_P+T_C & EXIT
   IF TMRS_19<>"T0000" THEN ENTRY & GOSUB TMRS_TO_VAR(TMRS_19) &  REG MPAT D2C_3=T_P+T_C & EXIT
   IF TMRS_1A<>"T0000" THEN ENTRY & GOSUB TMRS_TO_VAR(TMRS_1A) &  REG MPAT D2D_3=T_P+T_C & EXIT
   IF TMRS_21<>"T0000" THEN ENTRY & GOSUB TMRS_TO_VAR(TMRS_21) &  REG MPAT D1B_4=T_P+T_C & EXIT
   IF TMRS_22<>"T0000" THEN ENTRY & GOSUB TMRS_TO_VAR(TMRS_22) &  REG MPAT D1C_4=T_P+T_C & EXIT
   IF TMRS_23<>"T0000" THEN ENTRY & GOSUB TMRS_TO_VAR(TMRS_23) &  REG MPAT D1D_4=T_P+T_C & EXIT
   IF TMRS_24<>"T0000" THEN ENTRY & GOSUB TMRS_TO_VAR(TMRS_24) &  REG MPAT D1E_4=T_P+T_C & EXIT
   IF TMRS_25<>"T0000" THEN ENTRY & GOSUB TMRS_TO_VAR(TMRS_25) &  REG MPAT D1F_4=T_P+T_C & EXIT
   IF TMRS_26<>"T0000" THEN ENTRY & GOSUB TMRS_TO_VAR(TMRS_26) &  REG MPAT D1G_4=T_P+T_C & EXIT
   IF TMRS_27<>"T0000" THEN ENTRY & GOSUB TMRS_TO_VAR(TMRS_27) &  REG MPAT D1H_4=T_P+T_C & EXIT
   IF TMRS_28<>"T0000" THEN ENTRY & GOSUB TMRS_TO_VAR(TMRS_28) &  REG MPAT D2B_4=T_P+T_C & EXIT
   IF TMRS_29<>"T0000" THEN ENTRY & GOSUB TMRS_TO_VAR(TMRS_29) &  REG MPAT D2C_4=T_P+T_C & EXIT
   IF TMRS_2A<>"T0000" THEN ENTRY & GOSUB TMRS_TO_VAR(TMRS_2A) &  REG MPAT D2D_4=T_P+T_C & EXIT

GOTO CONT


TMRS_TO_VAR:
STRING TMRS_CODE_TMP(5)=""  
ARGUMENT(TMRS_CODE)
   TMRS_CODE_TMP=TMRS_CODE
   T_P=0
   IF TMRS_CODE_TMP(2,1)="2"  THEN T_P=#9000
   IF TMRS_CODE_TMP(2,1)="3"  THEN T_P=#7000 
   T_C=NUMERIC(TMRS_CODE_TMP(3,3),16)
GOTO CONT






GOTO CONT


TPDMEASURE:

DO TPDMEASURERT CHSEL=0 TSTFLG-1 1
  GOSUB TPDM(901, 1,900MV, 52PS,083PS,1.0PS,"TPD RISING  Long *170 ") ; RISING  LONG
  GOSUB TPDM(902, 2,900MV, 52PS,083PS,1.0PS,"TPD RISING  Short*50  ") ; RISING  SHORT
  GOSUB TPDM(903, 4,900MV, 52PS,083PS,1.0PS,"TPD FALLING Long *170 ") ; FALLING LONG
  GOSUB TPDM(904, 5,900MV, 52PS,083PS,1.0PS,"TPD FALLING Short*50  ") ; FALLING SHORT
  GOSUB TPDM(905, 7,900MV, 15PS,100PS,1.0PS,"TPD RISING  Long *170 ") ; RISING  LONG
  GOSUB TPDM(906, 8,900MV, 15PS,100PS,1.0PS,"TPD RISING  Short*50  ") ; RISING  SHORT
  GOSUB TPDM(907,10,900MV, 15PS,100PS,1.0PS,"TPD FALLING Long *170 ") ; FALLING LONG
  GOSUB TPDM(908,11,900MV, 15PS,100PS,1.0PS,"TPD FALLING Short*50  ") ; FALLING SHORT
; GOSUB TPDM(911,15,1050MV,30NS,100NS,0.1NS,"CDC M4                ") ; FALLING SHORT
; GOSUB TPDM(912,16,1050MV,25NS,70NS,0.1NS,"CDC M4toGP VIRTICAL    ") ; FALLING SHORT


  GOSUB TPD2P0(999,1,900MV,"TPD2.0")
  GOSUB TPD2P0(999,2,900MV,"TPD2.0")

TPDMEASURERT:
           
  
GOTO CONT
  
         DIM RSULTA(32)=0PS!32 
         DIM RSULTB(32)=0PS!32 
        DIM TPD2PA(32)= 0
        DIM TPD2PB(32)= 0
        DIM TPD2PC(32)= 0
        DIM TPD2PD(32)= 0

        DIM GANKA(8,80)=0
        DIM GANKB(8,80)=0
        DIM GANKC(8,80)=0
        DIM GANKD(8,80)=0
        DIM TEMPA(32)= 0!32  
        DIM TEMPB(32)= 0!32
        DIM TEMPC(32)= 0!32
        DIM TEMPD(32)= 0!32
TPD2P0:
   ARGUMENT(PD2TN1,T2VAL,PD2VCC,PTITLE2)



        PCA=0.25
        PDQ=0.25

        SIWC=350MV ;; Input Swing CA
        SIWD=350MV ;; Input Swing DQ

        RESET MPAT 
        TEST PD2TN1

;        STRING PNAMN(80)=""

        WL=0   ;14+4=18
        RL=0   ;28+3=31
        ;;=====================================================
        ;; Setting VREF_CA/DQ, Check LP5 Option
        ;;=====================================================
        CVFCA=((PCA*100)-10)/0.5
        CVFDQ=((PDQ*100)-10)/0.5

        REG MPAT YT12=#50       ;;Calculated VREF_CA  Code
        REG MPAT YT14=#50       ;;Calculated VREF_LDQ Code
        REG MPAT YT15=#50       ;;Calculated VREF_UDQ Code
       ;;=====================================================

        REG MPAT YT7=#0015 ;; Soc ODT RZQ/5, ODT-CS Disable
        SET ILMODE  8WAY
        DO VARRS1 I=1,32
           RSULTA(I)=0PS
           RSULTB(I)=0PS
        VARRS1:

      ;    READ EDUT TO INIDUT

      ;    EVDD1=VD2SET*1.72
      ;    EVDD2=VD2SET
      ;    EVDD3=VD2SET
      ;    EVDD4=VD2SET*0.476
           GOSUB FMD00                                     ; Format  @ unipgm
           GOSUB TFCHG1(20NS,10NS)

      FAVCC2=PD2VCC & FAVCC1=PD2VCC*1.71 & FAVCCQ=PD2VCC*0.5
   ;  GOSUB VNTPD

        VDD1   = FAVCC1     ;VDD1
        VDD2H  = FAVCC2     ;VDD2
        VDD2L  = FAVCC2     ;VDD2L
        VDDQ   = FAVCCQ     ;VDDQ


        VREFF  = FAVCCQ*0.5           ;??
        IN1    = FAVCC2*1.0, 0V    ;CK     
        IN2    = FAVCC2*1.0, 0V    ;CS 
        IN3    = FAVCC2*1.0, 0V    ;DQ
        IN4    = FAVCC2*1.0, 0V    ;CA
        IN5    = FAVCC2*1.0, 0V    ;DM
        IN6    = FAVCC2*1.0, 0V    ;   
        IN7    = FAVCC2*1.0, 0V    ;RDQS
        IN8    = FAVCC2*1.0, 0V    ;WCK 
        IN9    = FAVCC2*1.0, 0V    ;RESET

        OUT1  = VREFF+0.001V, VREFF-0.001V
        OUT2  = VREFF+0.001V, VREFF-0.001V
        OUT3  = VREFF+0.001V, VREFF-0.001V

        VT1   = 0V
        VT2   = 0V
        VT3   = 0V



;     GOSUB VBASIC(PD2VCC,PCA,PDQ,SIWC,SIWD)           ; Voltage 


      ;;; WCK1CA = IN2    FIXL
      ;;; WCK1CB = IN2    FIXL
      ;;; WCK1CC = IN2    FIXL
      ;;; WCK1CD = IN2    FIXL

       LDMIP = IN3    FIXL   
       UDMIP = IN3    FIXL   
       ;------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
       RDQSP = IN3    FIXL
       RDQSBP= IN3    FIXH

       WCK0T = IN3    FIXL
       WCK0C = IN3    FIXL
       WCK1T = IN3    FIXL
;      WCK1C = IN3    FIXH       
       WCK1C = IN8    DNRZ   BCLK8   CCLK8  CYP1   <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28> <C27,C28>

       VT1=0MV 
       DQP=OPEN
       DQ0A  = IN3     NRZB   BCLK9   CCLK9  IOC  DRE2  @
               DRENRZ  OUTL1                 VT1  CYP1 <C8> <C8> <C8> <C8> <C8> <C8> <C8> <C8>
       DQ1A  = IN3,   DNRZ,  BCLK9,  CCLK9, IOC, OUTL1, VT1,       DRENRZ, DRCYCDLY(WL),EXPCYCDLY(RL),CPECYCDLY(RL)  @
               [STRB1,CPE1], EXPA1,                 , EXPB129,                                                       @
               CYP1   <D1,SD1> <D1,SD1> <D1,SD1> <D1,SD1> <D1,SD1> <D1,SD1>      @
                      <D1,SD1> <D1,SD1> <D1,SD1> <D1,SD1> <D1,SD1> <D1,SD1> <D1,SD1>
       DQ0B  = IN3     NRZB   BCLK9   CCLK9  IOC  DRE2  @
               DRENRZ  OUTL1                 VT1  CYP1 <C8> <C8> <C8> <C8> <C8> <C8> <C8> <C8>

       DQ1B  = IN3,   DNRZ,  BCLK9,  CCLK9, IOC, OUTL1, VT1,       DRENRZ, DRCYCDLY(WL),EXPCYCDLY(RL),CPECYCDLY(RL)  @
               [STRB1,CPE1], EXPA1,                 , EXPB129,                                                       @
               CYP1   <D1,SD1> <D1,SD1> <D1,SD1> <D1,SD1> <D1,SD1> <D1,SD1>      @
                      <D1,SD1> <D1,SD1> <D1,SD1> <D1,SD1> <D1,SD1> <D1,SD1> <D1,SD1>
       DQ0C  = IN3     NRZB   BCLK9   CCLK9  IOC  DRE2  @
               DRENRZ  OUTL1                 VT1  CYP1 <C8> <C8> <C8> <C8> <C8> <C8> <C8> <C8>
       DQ1C  = IN3,   DNRZ,  BCLK9,  CCLK9, IOC, OUTL1, VT1,       DRENRZ, DRCYCDLY(WL),EXPCYCDLY(RL),CPECYCDLY(RL)  @
               [STRB1,CPE1], EXPA1,                 , EXPB129,                                                       @
               CYP1   <D1,SD1> <D1,SD1> <D1,SD1> <D1,SD1> <D1,SD1> <D1,SD1>      @
                      <D1,SD1> <D1,SD1> <D1,SD1> <D1,SD1> <D1,SD1> <D1,SD1> <D1,SD1>
       DQ0D  = IN3     NRZB   BCLK9   CCLK9  IOC  DRE2  @
               DRENRZ  OUTL1                 VT1  CYP1 <C8> <C8> <C8> <C8> <C8> <C8> <C8> <C8>
       DQ1D  = IN3,   DNRZ,  BCLK9,  CCLK9, IOC, OUTL1, VT1,       DRENRZ, DRCYCDLY(WL),EXPCYCDLY(RL),CPECYCDLY(RL)  @
               [STRB1,CPE1], EXPA1,                 , EXPB129,                                                       @
               CYP1   <D1,SD1> <D1,SD1> <D1,SD1> <D1,SD1> <D1,SD1> <D1,SD1>      @
                      <D1,SD1> <D1,SD1> <D1,SD1> <D1,SD1> <D1,SD1> <D1,SD1> <D1,SD1>


       IF T2VAL=1 THEN SEND MPAT PDCSTPD2P0A 
       IF T2VAL=2 THEN SEND MPAT PDCSTPD2P0S 
       REG MPAT PC=#00 
REG MPAT TIMER=500US

       TPD2CNT=(500US/160NS)-2
;      WRITE /,TPD2CNT

       REG MPAT IDX6=TPD2CNT
   
       SET WET
       SRON
       TEST 4996
       MEAS MPAT(3)


;-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------


  ;    WCK1C = IN3    FIXL       


DO LOOP LTPD= 1,20,1

        SEND MPAT PDCSTPD2P08W        
        REG MPAT PC=#00

     ;;;IF HSDFLG=2 THEN GOSUB FEVEN & REG MPAT CPE2=FIXL
     ;;;IF HSDFLG=3 THEN GOSUB FODD  & REG MPAT CPE2=FIXL

        TEST 4996
        MEAS MPAT(3)

         READ FUNC1 (DQ1) TO TPD2PA
;        READ FUNC1 (DQ1B) TO TPD2PB
;        READ FUNC1 (DQ1C) TO TPD2PC
;        READ FUNC1 (DQ1D) TO TPD2PD

;       WRITE /,TPD2PA(2)
        
        DO LOP0X MUT=1,TP,1
          RTNUM=MUT-32*((MUT-1)/32)-1
          IF SR(CURDUT,RTNUM).AND.#01 <> #0 THEN ENTRY
             IF TPD2PA(MUT).AND.#80000000=0 THEN GANKA(MUT,LTPD)=0 ;; 
        	   ELSE GANKA(MUT,LTPD)=1
             IF TPD2PA(MUT).AND.#40000000=0 THEN GANKB(MUT,LTPD)=0 ;; 
        	   ELSE GANKB(MUT,LTPD)=1
             IF TPD2PA(MUT).AND.#20000000=0 THEN GANKC(MUT,LTPD)=0 ;; 
        	   ELSE GANKC(MUT,LTPD)=1
             IF TPD2PA(MUT).AND.#10000000=0 THEN GANKD(MUT,LTPD)=0 ;; 
        	   ELSE GANKD(MUT,LTPD)=1
        	EXIT
        LOP0X:
LOOP:

        RESET WET
        SROF

WRITE /
; DO LPCHECKA LPLP=1,20,1
;     WRITE[1,1(1,1)], GANKA(2,LPLP)
; LPCHECKA:
; WRITE /
; DO LPCHECKB LPLP=1,20,1
;     WRITE[1,1(1,1)], GANKB(2,LPLP)
; LPCHECKB:
; WRITE /
; DO LPCHECKC LPLP=1,20,1
;     WRITE[1,1(1,1)], GANKC(2,LPLP)
; LPCHECKC:
; WRITE /
; DO LPCHECKD LPLP=1,20,1
;     WRITE[1,1(1,1)], GANKD(2,LPLP)
; LPCHECKD:

;   IF CHSEL=0 THEN WRITE /,"CS0    ",
;   IF CHSEL=1 THEN WRITE /,"CS1    ",



DO CALDUTLP1 TSTORD=1 NTESTCH 1

       IF T2VAL=1 THEN  WRITE /,"TPD2 :",CHSEL*NTESTCH+TSTORD
       IF T2VAL=2 THEN  WRITE /,"TPDS2:",CHSEL*NTESTCH+TSTORD


DO CALDUTLP MUT=1,TP,1
    RTNUM=MUT-32*((MUT-1)/32)-1
    IF SR(CURDUT,RTNUM).AND.#01 <> #0 THEN ENTRY
        TEMPA(MUT)=GANKA(MUT,1)*2^9+GANKA(MUT,2)*2^8+GANKA(MUT,3)*2^7+GANKA(MUT,4)*2^6+GANKA(MUT,5)*2^5+GANKA(MUT,6)*2^4+GANKA(MUT,7)*2^3+GANKA(MUT,8)*2^2+GANKA(MUT,9)*2^1+GANKA(MUT,10)*2^0+GANKA(MUT,11)*2^19+GANKA(MUT,12)*2^18+GANKA(MUT,13)*2^17+GANKA(MUT,14)*2^16+GANKA(MUT,15)*2^15+GANKA(MUT,16)*2^14+GANKA(MUT,17)*2^13+GANKA(MUT,18)*2^12+GANKA(MUT,19)*2^11+GANKA(MUT,20)*2^10    
        IF TSTORD=1 THEN WRITE[1,1(8,2)] 500*1000*1000.0/(TEMPA(MUT)*64*41*2)     
        TEMPB(MUT)=GANKB(MUT,1)*2^9+GANKB(MUT,2)*2^8+GANKB(MUT,3)*2^7+GANKB(MUT,4)*2^6+GANKB(MUT,5)*2^5+GANKB(MUT,6)*2^4+GANKB(MUT,7)*2^3+GANKB(MUT,8)*2^2+GANKB(MUT,9)*2^1+GANKB(MUT,10)*2^0+GANKB(MUT,11)*2^19+GANKB(MUT,12)*2^18+GANKB(MUT,13)*2^17+GANKB(MUT,14)*2^16+GANKB(MUT,15)*2^15+GANKB(MUT,16)*2^14+GANKB(MUT,17)*2^13+GANKB(MUT,18)*2^12+GANKB(MUT,19)*2^11+GANKB(MUT,20)*2^10    
        IF TSTORD=2 THEN WRITE[1,1(8,2)] 500*1000*1000.0/(TEMPB(MUT)*64*41*2)     
        TEMPC(MUT)=GANKC(MUT,1)*2^9+GANKC(MUT,2)*2^8+GANKC(MUT,3)*2^7+GANKC(MUT,4)*2^6+GANKC(MUT,5)*2^5+GANKC(MUT,6)*2^4+GANKC(MUT,7)*2^3+GANKC(MUT,8)*2^2+GANKC(MUT,9)*2^1+GANKC(MUT,10)*2^0+GANKC(MUT,11)*2^19+GANKC(MUT,12)*2^18+GANKC(MUT,13)*2^17+GANKC(MUT,14)*2^16+GANKC(MUT,15)*2^15+GANKC(MUT,16)*2^14+GANKC(MUT,17)*2^13+GANKC(MUT,18)*2^12+GANKC(MUT,19)*2^11+GANKC(MUT,20)*2^10    
        IF TSTORD=3 THEN WRITE[1,1(8,2)] 500*1000*1000.0/(TEMPC(MUT)*64*41*2)     
        TEMPD(MUT)=GANKD(MUT,1)*2^9+GANKD(MUT,2)*2^8+GANKD(MUT,3)*2^7+GANKD(MUT,4)*2^6+GANKD(MUT,5)*2^5+GANKD(MUT,6)*2^4+GANKD(MUT,7)*2^3+GANKD(MUT,8)*2^2+GANKD(MUT,9)*2^1+GANKD(MUT,10)*2^0+GANKD(MUT,11)*2^19+GANKD(MUT,12)*2^18+GANKD(MUT,13)*2^17+GANKD(MUT,14)*2^16+GANKD(MUT,15)*2^15+GANKD(MUT,16)*2^14+GANKD(MUT,17)*2^13+GANKD(MUT,18)*2^12+GANKD(MUT,19)*2^11+GANKD(MUT,20)*2^10    
        IF TSTORD=4 THEN WRITE[1,1(8,2)] 500*1000*1000.0/(TEMPD(MUT)*64*41*2)     
    EXIT
CALDUTLP:

CALDUTLP1:


GOTO CONT




ZQCODETEST:
   ARGUMENT(ZQTSTVDD,ZQTSTITEM)

   MR11_CAODT=#0 & MR11_DQODT=#0 & MR11_NTODTEN=#0 & MR17_SOCODT=#5 & MR18_WCKODT=#0 & MR41_NTODT=#0
   MR1_WL=#0 & MR2_RL=#0 & MR2_NWR=#0
   GOSUB WLRLCAL(WCKCKRATIO,MR1_WL,MR2_RL,DVFSC,WLSET,L_DELAY)
        GOSUB MR_SETTING ;  MR_VALUE TO YTx

    ALLPIN=OPEN
    RL=0 
    WL=0 
    RESET BCLK CCLK STRB DELAYADJUST ; for T5511

    SET ILMODE 16WAY

    RESET MPAT

    SEND MPAT PDCS4SM490K1ANN


    SELECT SCRDATA ENABLE          
    SELECT ARIRAM DISABLE  

    SEND SCRDATA CDCS8FUL

    TSTORD=1 
;   CHSEL=0
    READ CDUT TO CURDUT

     SRON




CODEREAD:
   CH_CODE=CHSEL

    ARGUMENT(CO_HB,CO_SB,CO_NG,CO_LLMT,CO_HLMT)
   
    CO_HLIMIT=0MA 
    CO_LLIMIT=0MA 
    
    IF ORGNUM=16 THEN ENTRY
       READ FUNC1(MRRDQP) TO VTVAL0

       IF FAPATN(7,3)="OSC" THEN ENTRY
          READ FUNC4(MRRDQP) TO VTVAL0
          READ FUNC8(MRRDQP) TO VTVAL1
       EXIT
    EXIT
    IF ORGNUM=8 THEN ENTRY
       READ FUNC1(MRRDQP)  TO VTVAL0
       READ FUNC1(MRRDQPU) TO VTVAL1
       IF FAPATN(7,3)="OSC" THEN ENTRY
          READ FUNC4(MRRDQP)  TO VTVAL0
          READ FUNC8(MRRDQP)  TO VTVAL1
          READ FUNC4(MRRDQPU) TO VTVAL2
          READ FUNC8(MRRDQPU) TO VTVAL3
       EXIT
    EXIT
    
    CH_CODE=CHSEL
    IF MIXEDCHIP="0" OR MIXEDCHIP="1" THEN CH_CODE=0
     

;;=================================================================================================================================
;        WH CODE READ LOGIC ROUTINE      
;;=================================================================================================================================

         TTCNTP=0
         TTCNTL=0
         TTCNTH=0
;------------------------------------------------------------------------
         DO LCODERD I=1,TP,1
;------------------------------------------------------------------------

IF ORGNUM=16 THEN ENTRY
            VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+1,I)=SR0(VTVAL0(I),24).AND.#000000FF     
            VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+2,I)=SR0(VTVAL0(I),16).AND.#000000FF     
            VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+3,I)=SR0(VTVAL0(I),8).AND.#000000FF     
            VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+4,I)=VTVAL0(I).AND.#000000FF     

    IF FAPATN(7,3)="ZQC" THEN ENTRY
            VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+1,I)=SR0(VTVAL0(I),24).AND.#0000003F     
            VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+2,I)=SR0(VTVAL0(I),16).AND.#0000003F     
            VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+3,I)=SR0(VTVAL0(I),8).AND.#0000003F     
            VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+4,I)=VTVAL0(I).AND.#0000003F     
    EXIT


    IF FAPATN(7,3)="OSC" THEN ENTRY
            VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+1,I)=(SR0(VTVAL1(I),16).AND.#0000FF00).OR.SR0(VTVAL0(I),24).AND.#000000FF     
            VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+2,I)=(SR0(VTVAL1(I),8).AND.#0000FF00).OR.SR0(VTVAL0(I),16).AND.#000000FF     
            VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+3,I)=(VTVAL1(I).AND.#0000FF00).OR.SR0(VTVAL0(I),8).AND.#000000FF      
            VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+4,I)=(SL0(VTVAL1(I),8).AND.#0000FF00).OR.VTVAL0(I).AND.#000000FF   
            IF VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+1,I)>=#FFFF THEN VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+1,I)=#0     
            IF VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+2,I)>=#FFFF THEN VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+2,I)=#0    
            IF VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+3,I)>=#FFFF THEN VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+3,I)=#0
            IF VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+4,I)>=#FFFF THEN VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+4,I)=#0  
    EXIT

    IF FAPATN(7,3)="MRF" THEN ENTRY
            VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+1,I)=(SR0(VTVAL1(I),16).AND.#0000FF00).OR.SR0(VTVAL0(I),24).AND.#000000FF     
            VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+2,I)=(SR0(VTVAL1(I),8).AND.#0000FF00).OR.SR0(VTVAL0(I),16).AND.#000000FF     
            VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+3,I)=(VTVAL1(I).AND.#0000FF00).OR.SR0(VTVAL0(I),8).AND.#000000FF      
            VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+4,I)=(SL0(VTVAL1(I),8).AND.#0000FF00).OR.VTVAL0(I).AND.#000000FF   
            IF VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+1,I)>=#FFFF THEN VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+1,I)=#0     
            IF VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+2,I)>=#FFFF THEN VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+2,I)=#0    
            IF VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+3,I)>=#FFFF THEN VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+3,I)=#0
            IF VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+4,I)>=#FFFF THEN VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+4,I)=#0  
    EXIT
EXIT

IF ORGNUM=8  THEN ENTRY
            VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+1,I)=SR0(VTVAL0(I),24).AND.#000000FF     
            VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+2,I)=SR0(VTVAL1(I),24).AND.#000000FF     
            VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+3,I)=SR0(VTVAL0(I),16).AND.#000000FF     
            VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+4,I)=SR0(VTVAL1(I),16).AND.#000000FF     
            VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+5,I)=SR0(VTVAL0(I),8).AND.#000000FF     
            VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+6,I)=SR0(VTVAL1(I),8).AND.#000000FF     
            VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+7,I)=VTVAL0(I).AND.#000000FF     
            VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+8,I)=VTVAL1(I).AND.#000000FF     

    IF FAPATN(7,3)="ZQC" THEN ENTRY
            VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+1,I)=SR0(VTVAL0(I),24).AND.#0000003F     
            VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+2,I)=SR0(VTVAL1(I),24).AND.#0000003F     
            VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+3,I)=SR0(VTVAL0(I),16).AND.#0000003F     
            VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+4,I)=SR0(VTVAL1(I),16).AND.#0000003F     
            VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+5,I)=SR0(VTVAL0(I),8).AND.#0000003F     
            VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+6,I)=SR0(VTVAL1(I),8).AND.#0000003F     
            VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+7,I)=VTVAL0(I).AND.#0000003F     
            VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+8,I)=VTVAL1(I).AND.#0000003F     
    EXIT


    IF FAPATN(7,3)="OSC" THEN ENTRY
            VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+1,I)=(SR0(VTVAL1(I),16).AND.#0000FF00).OR.SR0(VTVAL0(I),24).AND.#000000FF     
            VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+2,I)=(SR0(VTVAL3(I),16).AND.#0000FF00).OR.SR0(VTVAL2(I),24).AND.#000000FF     
            VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+3,I)=(SR0(VTVAL1(I),8).AND.#0000FF00).OR.SR0(VTVAL0(I),16).AND.#000000FF     
            VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+4,I)=(SR0(VTVAL3(I),8).AND.#0000FF00).OR.SR0(VTVAL2(I),16).AND.#000000FF     
            VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+5,I)=(VTVAL1(I).AND.#0000FF00).OR.SR0(VTVAL0(I),8).AND.#000000FF      
            VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+6,I)=(VTVAL3(I).AND.#0000FF00).OR.SR0(VTVAL2(I),8).AND.#000000FF      
            VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+7,I)=(SL0(VTVAL1(I),8).AND.#0000FF00).OR.VTVAL0(I).AND.#000000FF   
            VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+8,I)=(SL0(VTVAL3(I),8).AND.#0000FF00).OR.VTVAL2(I).AND.#000000FF   

            IF VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+1,I)>=#FFFF THEN VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+1,I)=#0     
            IF VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+2,I)>=#FFFF THEN VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+2,I)=#0    
            IF VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+3,I)>=#FFFF THEN VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+3,I)=#0
            IF VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+4,I)>=#FFFF THEN VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+4,I)=#0  
            IF VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+5,I)>=#FFFF THEN VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+5,I)=#0     
            IF VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+6,I)>=#FFFF THEN VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+6,I)=#0    
            IF VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+7,I)>=#FFFF THEN VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+7,I)=#0
            IF VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+8,I)>=#FFFF THEN VTVAL7(CH_CODE*NTESTCH+8,I)=#0  
    EXIT

;   IF FAPATN(7,3)="MRF" THEN ENTRY
;           VTVAL7(1,I)=(SR0(VTVAL1(I),16).AND.#0000FF00).OR.SR0(VTVAL0(I),24).AND.#000000FF     
;           VTVAL7(2,I)=(SR0(VTVAL1(I),8).AND.#0000FF00).OR.SR0(VTVAL0(I),16).AND.#000000FF     
;           VTVAL7(3,I)=(VTVAL1(I).AND.#0000FF00).OR.SR0(VTVAL0(I),8).AND.#000000FF      
;           VTVAL7(4,I)=(SL0(VTVAL1(I),8).AND.#0000FF00).OR.VTVAL0(I).AND.#000000FF   
;   EXIT
EXIT

         LCODERD:

;        IF CHSEL<TSTFLG-1 AND CHSEL=0 THEN ENTRY & CHSEL=1 & GOTO CODERDODEORD & EXIT  ;;      
;        TSTORD=1
;        CHSEL=0

        
    READ CDUT TO CURDUT
    
    WCKTIMER=WCK_OSC*16
    IF FAPATN(7,7)="OSC0N1A" OR FAPATN(7,7)="OSC0N1C" THEN ENTRY
       IF WCK_OSC>=#40 AND WCK_OSC<#80 THEN WCKTIMER=2048
       IF WCK_OSC>=#80 AND WCK_OSC<#C0 THEN WCKTIMER=4096
       IF WCK_OSC>=#C0                 THEN WCKTIMER=8192
    EXIT
    IF FAPATN(7,7)="OSC0N2A" OR FAPATN(7,7)="OSC0N2C" THEN ENTRY
       IF WCK_OSC>=#40 AND WCK_OSC<#80 THEN WCKTIMER=2048
       IF WCK_OSC>=#80 AND WCK_OSC<#C0 THEN WCKTIMER=4096
       IF WCK_OSC>=#C0                 THEN WCKTIMER=8192
    EXIT
    IF FAPATN(7,7)="OSC0N3A" OR FAPATN(7,7)="OSC0N3C" THEN ENTRY
       IF WCK_OSC>=#40 AND WCK_OSC<#80 THEN WCKTIMER=2048
       IF WCK_OSC>=#80 AND WCK_OSC<#C0 THEN WCKTIMER=4096
       IF WCK_OSC>=#C0                 THEN WCKTIMER=8192
    EXIT
  
 
;   IF FK=#10 THEN WRITE ,"                              ","#",ASCII(WCK_OSC,5,4)," #",ASCII(MR1_WL,5,1)," ",;FAPATN(7,7)," "
;------------------------------------------------------------------------
    DO WCODERD1 TSTORD=1,NTESTCH,1      ; ch loop
;------------------------------------------------------------------------
       DO WCODERD I=1,TP,1              ; dut loop
;------------------------------------------------------------------------
;        FDNUM=(MOD((I-1)/(TP/2))/32)*2+(I-1)/(TP/2)+1
         RTNUM=I-32*((I-1)/32)-1
         IF TP<=32 THEN FDNUM=1
         IF SR(CURDUT,RTNUM).AND.#01 <> #0 THEN ENTRY
         ; WCK OSC
            IF FAPATN(7,3)="OSC" THEN ENTRY ; WCK OSC I/O TIME
;              WRITE ASCII(WCKTIMER*LP5TCK/1NS*WCKCKRATIO/(2*VTVAL7(TSTORD+CH_CODE*NTESTCH,I)),1,6,3," ")
               CO_CHK(I)=1MA*WCKTIMER*(LP5TCK/1PS)*WCKCKRATIO/(2*VTVAL7(TSTORD+CH_CODE*NTESTCH,I))
               IF WCK_OSC=#C0 THEN ENTRY 
                  IF FAPATN(13,1)="A" THEN ENTRY 
                     IF MR2_RL=#C AND LP5VD2>1.12V THEN WOSCI0(TSTORD+CH_CODE*NTESTCH,I)=WCKTIMER*LP5TCK/1NS*WCKCKRATIO/(2*VTVAL7(TSTORD+CH_CODE*NTESTCH,I))
                     IF MR2_RL=#C AND LP5VD2<1.01V THEN WOSCI1(TSTORD+CH_CODE*NTESTCH,I)=WCKTIMER*LP5TCK/1NS*WCKCKRATIO/(2*VTVAL7(TSTORD+CH_CODE*NTESTCH,I))
                     IF MR2_RL=#5 AND LP5VD2>1.12V THEN WOSCI2(TSTORD+CH_CODE*NTESTCH,I)=WCKTIMER*LP5TCK/1NS*WCKCKRATIO/(2*VTVAL7(TSTORD+CH_CODE*NTESTCH,I))
                     IF MR2_RL=#5 AND LP5VD2<1.01V THEN WOSCI3(TSTORD+CH_CODE*NTESTCH,I)=WCKTIMER*LP5TCK/1NS*WCKCKRATIO/(2*VTVAL7(TSTORD+CH_CODE*NTESTCH,I))
                  EXIT
                  IF FAPATN(13,1)="C" THEN ENTRY
                     IF MR2_RL=#C AND LP5VD2>1.12V THEN WOSCO0(TSTORD+CH_CODE*NTESTCH,I)=WCKTIMER*LP5TCK/1NS*WCKCKRATIO/(2*VTVAL7(TSTORD+CH_CODE*NTESTCH,I))
                     IF MR2_RL=#C AND LP5VD2<1.01V THEN WOSCO1(TSTORD+CH_CODE*NTESTCH,I)=WCKTIMER*LP5TCK/1NS*WCKCKRATIO/(2*VTVAL7(TSTORD+CH_CODE*NTESTCH,I))
                     IF MR2_RL=#5 AND LP5VD2>1.12V THEN WOSCO2(TSTORD+CH_CODE*NTESTCH,I)=WCKTIMER*LP5TCK/1NS*WCKCKRATIO/(2*VTVAL7(TSTORD+CH_CODE*NTESTCH,I))
                     IF MR2_RL=#5 AND LP5VD2<1.01V THEN WOSCO3(TSTORD+CH_CODE*NTESTCH,I)=WCKTIMER*LP5TCK/1NS*WCKCKRATIO/(2*VTVAL7(TSTORD+CH_CODE*NTESTCH,I))
                  EXIT
               EXIT
            EXIT
         ; ZQ CODE
            IF FAPATN(7,3)="ZQC" THEN ENTRY ; ZQ CODE READ
           ;   IF FK=#10 THEN WRITE  "  #",ASCII(VTVAL7(TSTORD+CH_CODE*NTESTCH,I),5,2)
               CO_CHK(I)=1MA*VTVAL7(TSTORD+CH_CODE*NTESTCH,I)
               IF FAPATN(13,1)="D" THEN ZQPD0(TSTORD+CH_CODE*NTESTCH,I)=VTVAL7(TSTORD+CH_CODE*NTESTCH,I)
               IF FAPATN(13,1)="U" THEN ZQPU0(TSTORD+CH_CODE*NTESTCH,I)=VTVAL7(TSTORD+CH_CODE*NTESTCH,I)
            EXIT
         ; MR?  
            IF FAPATN(7,3)="MRF" THEN ENTRY ; MR49 MR50
               IF FK=#10 THEN WRITE  "  #",ASCII(VTVAL7(TSTORD+CH_CODE*NTESTCH,I),5,2)
               CO_CHK(I)=1MA*VTVAL7(TSTORD+CH_CODE*NTESTCH,I)
            EXIT
         ; TQW T-C
            IF FAPATN(7,3)="TQW" AND TSTITEM(1,6)="TQW_RQ" THEN ENTRY ; TQW RDQST-C
               CO_CHK(I)=TQW_VALUE0(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,19)-TQW_VALUE0(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,20)
               IF ORGNUM=16 THEN ENTRY
               CO_CH1(I)=TQW_VALUE0(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,21)-TQW_VALUE0(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,22)
               EXIT
            EXIT
            IF FAPATN(7,3)="TQW" AND TSTITEM(1,6)="TQ1_RQ" THEN ENTRY ; TQW RDQST-C
               CO_CHK(I)=TQW_VALUE1(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,19)-TQW_VALUE1(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,20)
               IF ORGNUM=16 THEN ENTRY
               CO_CH1(I)=TQW_VALUE1(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,21)-TQW_VALUE1(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,22)
               EXIT
            EXIT

            IF FAPATN(7,3)="TQW" AND TSTITEM(1,6)="TQW_D1" THEN ENTRY ; TQW RDQST-C
               CO_CHK(I)=TQW_VALUE0(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,1)-TQW_VALUE0(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,2)
               IF ORGNUM=16 THEN ENTRY
               CO_CH1(I)=TQW_VALUE0(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,3)-TQW_VALUE0(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,4)
               EXIT
            EXIT
            IF FAPATN(7,3)="TQW" AND TSTITEM(1,6)="TQ1_D1" THEN ENTRY ; TQW RDQST-C
               CO_CHK(I)=TQW_VALUE1(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,1)-TQW_VALUE1(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,2)
               IF ORGNUM=16 THEN ENTRY
               CO_CH1(I)=TQW_VALUE1(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,3)-TQW_VALUE1(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,4)
               EXIT
            EXIT
            IF FAPATN(7,7)="COB4N2W" OR FAPATN(7,7)="COB5N5W" OR FAPATN(7,7)="PCP4N2W" THEN ENTRY
               CO_CHK(I)=GETWRMIN(WCKDUTYMRS*32+(I-1)*8+CH_CODE*NTESTCH+TSTORD)*1UA     
            EXIT
            IF TSTITEM(1,6)="VRO_C0" THEN ENTRY
               CO_CHK(I)=0MA
               IF ORGNUM=16 AND TSTORD=1 AND NFDQ1(I,TSTORD) <> #0 THEN  CO_CHK(I)=1MA
               IF ORGNUM=16 AND TSTORD=2 AND NFDQ1(I,TSTORD) <> #0 THEN  CO_CHK(I)=1MA
               IF ORGNUM=16 AND TSTORD=3 AND NFDQ1(I,TSTORD) <> #0 THEN  CO_CHK(I)=1MA
               IF ORGNUM=16 AND TSTORD=4 AND NFDQ1(I,TSTORD) <> #0 THEN  CO_CHK(I)=1MA
            EXIT
            IF TSTITEM(1,6)="VRO_C1" THEN ENTRY
               CO_CHK(I)=0MA
               IF ORGNUM=16 AND TSTORD=1 AND NFDQ2(I,TSTORD) <> #0 THEN  CO_CHK(I)=1MA
               IF ORGNUM=16 AND TSTORD=2 AND NFDQ2(I,TSTORD) <> #0 THEN  CO_CHK(I)=1MA
               IF ORGNUM=16 AND TSTORD=3 AND NFDQ2(I,TSTORD) <> #0 THEN  CO_CHK(I)=1MA
               IF ORGNUM=16 AND TSTORD=4 AND NFDQ2(I,TSTORD) <> #0 THEN  CO_CHK(I)=1MA
            EXIT

            IF FAPATN(7,7)="TQW0N10" AND TSTITEM(1,6)="OCD_TQ" THEN ENTRY ; TQW RDQST-C
               CO_CHK(I)=TQW_VALUE5(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,1)-TQW_VALUE5(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,5)
               IF ORGNUM=16 THEN ENTRY
               CO_CH1(I)=TQW_VALUE5(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,9)-TQW_VALUE5(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,13)
               EXIT
            EXIT
            IF FAPATN(7,7)="TQW0N1A" AND TSTITEM(1,6)="OCD_TQ" THEN ENTRY ; TQW RDQST-C
               CO_CHK(I)=TQW_VALUEA(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,1)-TQW_VALUEA(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,5)
               IF ORGNUM=16 THEN ENTRY
               CO_CH1(I)=TQW_VALUEA(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,9)-TQW_VALUEA(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,13)
               EXIT
            EXIT

               IF TSTITEM(1,6)="DCA_00" THEN ENTRY

                  CO_CH1(I)=(DCA_VALUE0(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL+TSTORD,6)-DCA_VALUE0(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL+TSTORD,4))*1

               IF TSTITEM(1,6)="DCA_01" THEN ENTRY

                  CO_CH1(I)=(DCA_VALUE0(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL+TSTORD,6)-DCA_VALUE0(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL+TSTORD,5))*1 
               EXIT

               IF TSTITEM(1,6)="DCA_04" THEN ENTRY                                                  
                  CO_CHK(I)=(DCA_VALUE0(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL+TSTORD,3)-DCA_VALUE0(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL+TSTORD,2))*1

            EXIT

            IF TSTITEM(1,6)="4P_GAP" THEN ENTRY

                                                                           T4P_MIN=TQW_PHASE1(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,DQI)

                  IF T4P_MIN>TQW_PHASE4(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,DQI) THEN T4P_MIN=TQW_PHASE4(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,DQI)
                  IF T4P_MIN>TQW_PHASE8(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,DQI) THEN T4P_MIN=TQW_PHASE8(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,DQI)
                                                                           
                                                                           T4P_MAX=TQW_PHASE1(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,DQI)
                  IF T4P_MAX<TQW_PHASE2(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,DQI) THEN T4P_MAX=TQW_PHASE2(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,DQI)
                  IF T4P_MAX<TQW_PHASE4(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,DQI) THEN T4P_MAX=TQW_PHASE4(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,DQI)
                  IF T4P_MAX<TQW_PHASE8(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,DQI) THEN T4P_MAX=TQW_PHASE8(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,DQI)

                                                                           T4P_MIN=TQW_PHASE1(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,DQI)

                  IF T4P_MIN>TQW_PHASE8(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,DQI) THEN T4P_MIN=TQW_PHASE8(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,DQI)

                                                                           T4P_MAX=TQW_PHASE1(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,DQI)
                  IF T4P_MAX<TQW_PHASE2(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,DQI) THEN T4P_MAX=TQW_PHASE2(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,DQI)

                  IF T4P_MAX<TQW_PHASE8(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,DQI) THEN T4P_MAX=TQW_PHASE8(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,DQI)

                  WRITE / "DO=",ASCII(TSTORD,2,2,0," "),"DU=",ASCII(I,2,2,0," "),DQI
                  WRITE ASCII(TQW_PHASE1(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,DQI)/1UA,2,8,1," ")
                  WRITE ASCII(TQW_PHASE2(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,DQI)/1UA,2,8,1," ")
                  WRITE ASCII(TQW_PHASE4(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,DQI)/1UA,2,8,1," ")
                  WRITE ASCII(TQW_PHASE8(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,DQI)/1UA,2,8,1," ")," : "
                  WRITE ASCII(T4P_MIN/1UA,2,8,1," ")

                  WRITE ASCII((T4P_MAX-T4P_MIN)/1UA,2,8,1," ")
                  WRITE ASCII(IOBLGAPMAX/1UA,2,8,1," ")

               T4P_MAX=-100MA

                  IF T4P_MIN>BYGAP_VAL THEN T4P_MIN=BYGAP_VAL
                  IF T4P_MAX<BYGAP_VAL THEN T4P_MAX=BYGAP_VAL

;            WRITE /,I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,DQI,BYGAP_VAL,T4P_MIN,T4P_MAX,TQW_VALUT5(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,DQI),TQW_VALUTA(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,DQI)

                     TQW_BYTE_GAP(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,4)=T4P_MAX

;              IF FK=#10 THEN WRITE /,I,TSTORD,RDVMIN0,CO_CHK(I)

               IF (VWM_MED(12)-WRVMIN1)<=(VWM_MED(4)-WRVMIN0) THEN CO_CHK(I)=(VWM_MED(4)-WRVMIN0)*1MA
               
;              WRITE /,I,TSTORD,WRVMIN0,VWM_MED(4),(VWM_MED(4)-WRVMIN0),WRVMIN1,VWM_MED(12),(VWM_MED(12)-WRVMIN1),CO_CHK(I)
               PMAP_VAR3((I-1)*8+NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD)=VWM_MED(4)-WRVMIN0

                  ODT_MED(6) =ODT_VALUE0(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,6)

               IF ORGNUM=16 THEN ENTRY

                  TQW_GAP(15)=TQW_VALUE5(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL+TSTORD,15)-TQW_VALUEA(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL+TSTORD,15)

                  IF (DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-0,35)-DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-0,21))<DCMA_MIN THEN DCMA_MIN=(DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-0,35)-DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-0,21))
                  IF (DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-0,34)-DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-0,21))<DCMA_MIN THEN DCMA_MIN=(DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-0,34)-DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-0,21))
                  IF (DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-0,35)-DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-0,22))<DCMA_MIN THEN DCMA_MIN=(DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-0,35)-DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-0,22))
                  IF (DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-0,34)-DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-0,22))<DCMA_MIN THEN DCMA_MIN=(DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-0,34)-DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-0,22))
               EXIT
               IF TSTITEM(1,6)="DCM_G0" THEN ENTRY
                  IF (DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-1,12)-DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-1,4))<DCMA_MIN THEN DCMA_MIN=(DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-1,12)-DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-1,4))
                  IF (DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-0,12)-DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-0,4))<DCMA_MIN THEN DCMA_MIN=(DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-0,12)-DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-0,4))
                  IF (DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-1,32)-DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-1,24))<DCMA_MIN THEN DCMA_MIN=(DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-1,32)-DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-1,24))
                  IF (DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-0,32)-DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-0,24))<DCMA_MIN THEN DCMA_MIN=(DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-0,32)-DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-0,24))
               EXIT
               IF TSTITEM(1,6)="DCM_G1" THEN ENTRY
                  IF (DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-1,12)-DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-1,8))<DCMA_MIN THEN DCMA_MIN=(DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-1,12)-DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-1,8))
                  IF (DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-0,12)-DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-0,8))<DCMA_MIN THEN DCMA_MIN=(DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-0,12)-DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-0,8))
                  IF (DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-1,32)-DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-1,28))<DCMA_MIN THEN DCMA_MIN=(DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-1,32)-DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-1,28))
                  IF (DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-0,32)-DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-0,28))<DCMA_MIN THEN DCMA_MIN=(DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-0,32)-DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-0,28))
               EXIT
               IF TSTITEM(1,6)="DCM_G2" THEN ENTRY
                  IF (DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-1,8)-DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-1,4))<DCMA_MIN THEN DCMA_MIN=(DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-1,8)-DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-1,4))
                  IF (DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-0,8)-DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-0,4))<DCMA_MIN THEN DCMA_MIN=(DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-0,8)-DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-0,4))
                  IF (DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-1,28)-DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-1,24))<DCMA_MIN THEN DCMA_MIN=(DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-1,28)-DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-1,24))
                  IF (DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-0,28)-DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-0,24))<DCMA_MIN THEN DCMA_MIN=(DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-0,28)-DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+TSTORD*2-0,24))
               EXIT
               CO_CHK(I)=DCMA_MIN*1MA
               IF FK=#10 THEN WRITE /,TSTITEM(1,6),I,TSTORD,CO_CHK(I),"(",CO_LLMT,")"
            EXIT          

         EXIT

       WCODERD:
;------------------------------------------------------------------------
; LIMIT
;------------------------------------------------------------------------
    IF FAPATN(7,3)="OSC" THEN ENTRY
       CO_HLIMIT=1MA*(CO_HLMT/1PS)
       CO_LLIMIT=1MA*(CO_LLMT/1PS)
    EXIT
    IF FAPATN(7,3)="ZQC" OR FAPATN(7,3)="MRF" THEN ENTRY
       CO_HLIMIT=1MA*(CO_HLMT)
       CO_LLIMIT=1MA*(CO_LLMT)
    EXIT
    IF FAPATN(7,3)="TQW" THEN ENTRY
       CO_HLIMIT=CO_HLMT
       CO_LLIMIT=CO_LLMT
    EXIT

    IF TSTITEM(1,6)="NDT_ME" THEN ENTRY 
       CO_HLIMIT=CO_HLMT
       CO_LLIMIT=CO_LLMT
    EXIT

    IF FAPATN(7,7)="COB4N2W" OR FAPATN(7,7)="COB5N5W" OR FAPATN(7,7)="PCP4N2W" OR FAPATN(7,7)="COB5D5W" THEN ENTRY
       CO_HLIMIT=CO_HLMT/1PS*1UA
       CO_LLIMIT=CO_LLMT/1PS*1UA
    EXIT
    IF TSTITEM(1,6)="ALLIOQ" OR TSTITEM(1,6)="TQW_BL" THEN ENTRY
       CO_HLIMIT=0.5MA
       CO_LLIMIT=-0.1MA
    EXIT
    IF TSTITEM(1,4)="RDVW" OR TSTITEM(1,4)="WRVW" OR TSTITEM(1,6)="WRWGAP" THEN ENTRY 
       CO_HLIMIT=1MA*(CO_HLMT/1PS)
       CO_LLIMIT=1MA*(CO_LLMT/1PS)
    EXIT

    IF FAPATN(7,7)="M266N4P" OR FAPATN(7,7)="M267N5P" THEN ENTRY 
       CO_HLIMIT=CO_HLMT
       CO_LLIMIT=CO_LLMT
    EXIT


    IF TSTITEM(1,3)="DCA" OR TSTITEM(1,3)="DCM" THEN ENTRY
       CO_HLIMIT=CO_HLMT
       CO_LLIMIT=CO_LLMT
    EXIT
;------------------------------------------------------------------------
; JUDGE
;------------------------------------------------------------------------
    TN=CO_NG
    TEST TN
    LIMIT JUDGE = CO_HLIMIT,CO_LLIMIT
    JUDGE CO_CHK

  IF FK=#10 AND SHMTESTING=0 THEN ENTRY
   GOSUB DUTRESLT
   IF TSPEED>=400 THEN WRITE /,STEP," ",CSN," ","TN=",ASCII(TN,2,5,0," "),ASCII(LP5VD2/1V,2,6,3," "),"V",ASCII(LP5VD2L/1V,2,6,3," "),"V",ASCII(LP5VDQ/1V,2,6,3," "),"V",ASCII(LP5TCK/1PS,2,7,1," "),"PS"
   IF TSPEED<400 THEN WRITE /,STEP," ",CSN," ","TN=",ASCII(TN,2,5,0," "),ASCII(LP5VD2/1V,2,6,3," "),"V",ASCII(LP5VD2L/1V,2,6,3," "),"V",ASCII(LP5VDQ/1V,2,6,3," "),"V",ASCII(LP5TCK/1NS,2,7,1," "),"NS"
   IF TSTITEM(1,6)<>"NDT_ME" AND TSTITEM(1,2)<>"TQ" AND TSTITEM(1,4)<>"RDVW" AND TSTITEM(1,6)<>"ALLIOQ" THEN WRITE  ," ",FREQ," ",FAFMT1," ",FAMOD2," ",ASCII(HSDOCNT,2,1,0," ")," ",FAPATN," ",ASCII(AA/1S,1,6,1," "),ASCII(CC/1S,1,6,2," "),"   "
   IF TSTITEM(1,6)="NDT_ME"  OR  TSTITEM(1,2)="TQ"  OR  TSTITEM(1,4)="RDVW"  OR  TSTITEM(1,6)="ALLIOQ"  THEN WRITE  ," ",FREQ," ","FMD01"," ","PNNNN"," ","2"," ",FAPATN," ",ASCII(AA/1S,1,6,1," "),ASCII(CC/1S,1,6,2," "),"   "

  ; WRITE ,DSPREPA(1,TP)," ",CO_LLIMIT,CO_HLIMIT
    WRITE ,DSPREPA(1,TP),"                          ","DO=",ASCII(NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,0,1,10)," "
    IF FAPATN(7,3)="ZQC"     THEN WRITE ,"  #",ASCII(VTVAL7(TSTORD+CH_CODE*NTESTCH,I),5,2)  ; ZQ CODE READ
    IF FAPATN(7,3)="OSC"     THEN WRITE  "  #",ASCII(VTVAL7(TSTORD+CH_CODE*NTESTCH,2),5,4),"(",WCKTIMER*LP5TCK*WCKCKRATIO/(2*VTVAL7(TSTORD+CH_CODE*NTESTCH,2)),")", "  #",ASCII(VTVAL7(TSTORD+CH_CODE*NTESTCH,4),5,4),"(",WCKTIMER*LP5TCK*WCKCKRATIO/(2*VTVAL7(TSTORD+CH_CODE*NTESTCH,4)),")", 
    IF TSTITEM(1,6)="TQW_BL" THEN WRITE  "MR30:0x",ASCII(MR30_DCA,5,2)," MR33:0x",ASCII(MR33_RCAL0P,5,2)," "

  DO WCODE0SHOW I=1,TP,1
;   FDNUM=(MOD((I-1)/(TP/2))/32)*2+(I-1)/(TP/2)+1
    RTNUM=I-32*((I-1)/32)-1
    IF TP<=32 THEN FDNUM=1
    IF SR(CURDUT,RTNUM).AND.#01 <> #0 THEN ENTRY
     IF TSTITEM(1,6)="ALLIOQ"  THEN WRITE "#",ASCII(I,0,1,10),":","DQ_",ASCII(TQW_GAP_DQP(I),0,2,10),ASCII(TQW_GAP_MAX(I)/1UA,2,7,1)," "
     IF TSTITEM(1,6)="TQW_BL"  THEN WRITE "#",ASCII(I,0,1,10),":","DQ_",ASCII(TQW_GAP_DQP(I),0,2,10),ASCII(TQW_GAP_MAX(I)/1UA,2,7,1)," "
     IF TSTITEM(1,7)="BY_GAP1" THEN WRITE "#",ASCII(I,0,1,10),":",ASCII((TQW_BYTE_GAP(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,1)-TQW_BYTE_GAP(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,2))/1UA,2,7,1)," "
     IF TSTITEM(1,7)="BY_GAP2" THEN WRITE "#",ASCII(I,0,1,10),":",ASCII((TQW_BYTE_GAP(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,5)-TQW_BYTE_GAP(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,6))/1UA,2,7,1)," "
     IF TSTITEM(1,6)="TQ1_RQ"  THEN WRITE ASCII(CO_CHK(I)/1UA,2,7,1)," "
     IF TSTITEM(1,6)="TQW_RQ"  THEN WRITE ASCII(CO_CHK(I)/1UA,2,7,1)," "
    EXIT
 WCODE0SHOW:
  EXIT

    IF CO_HB<>0 THEN ENTRY
       IF FAIL THEN ENTRY
               GOSUB FCHK_CD(TSTORD,CO_SB)
               SET CATEGORY CO_SB
               SET SORT CO_HB
               SET EXCLUSION :TEXT
       EXIT
    EXIT
;------------------------------------------------------------------------
; Byte1 JUDGE, if need
;------------------------------------------------------------------------
    IF FAPATN(7,3)="TQW" AND ORGNUM=16 AND TSTITEM(1,6)<>"ALLIOQ" AND TSTITEM(1,6)<>"TQW_BL" THEN ENTRY ; TQW RDQST-C  FOR BYTE
       JUDGE CO_CH1

       IF FK=#10 AND SHMTESTING=0 THEN ENTRY
           GOSUB DUTRESLT
           IF TSPEED>=400 THEN WRITE /,STEP," ",CSN," ","TN=",ASCII(TN,2,5,0," "),ASCII(LP5VD2/1V,2,6,3," "),"V",ASCII(LP5VD2L/1V,2,6,3," "),"V",ASCII(LP5VDQ/1V,2,6,3," "),"V",ASCII(LP5TCK/1PS,2,7,1," "),"PS"
           IF TSPEED<400 THEN WRITE /,STEP," ",CSN," ","TN=",ASCII(TN,2,5,0," "),ASCII(LP5VD2/1V,2,6,3," "),"V",ASCII(LP5VD2L/1V,2,6,3," "),"V",ASCII(LP5VDQ/1V,2,6,3," "),"V",ASCII(LP5TCK/1NS,2,7,1," "),"NS"
           IF TSTITEM(1,6)<>"NDT_ME" AND TSTITEM(1,2)<>"TQ" AND TSTITEM(1,6)<>"ALLIOQ" THEN WRITE  ," ",FREQ," ",FAFMT1," ",FAMOD2," ",ASCII(HSDOCNT,2,1,0," ")," ",FAPATN," ",ASCII(AA/1S,1,6,1," "),ASCII(CC/1S,1,6,2," "),"   "
           IF TSTITEM(1,6)="NDT_ME"  OR  TSTITEM(1,2)="TQ"  OR  TSTITEM(1,6)="ALLIOQ"  THEN WRITE  ," ",FREQ," ","FMD01"," ","PNNNN"," ","2"," ",FAPATN," ",ASCII(AA/1S,1,6,1," "),ASCII(CC/1S,1,6,2," "),"   "
           WRITE ,DSPREPA(1,TP),"                          ","DO=",ASCII(NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,0,1,10)," "
       EXIT

       DO WCODE_SHOW I=1,TP,1
      ;   FDNUM=(MOD((I-1)/(TP/2))/32)*2+(I-1)/(TP/2)+1
          RTNUM=I-32*((I-1)/32)-1
          IF TP<=32 THEN FDNUM=1
          IF SR(CURDUT,RTNUM).AND.#01 <> #0 THEN ENTRY
             IF TSTITEM(1,7)="BY_GAP1" THEN WRITE "#",ASCII(I,0,1,10),":",ASCII((TQW_BYTE_GAP(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,3)-TQW_BYTE_GAP(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,4))/1UA,2,7,1)," "
             IF TSTITEM(1,7)="BY_GAP2" THEN WRITE "#",ASCII(I,0,1,10),":",ASCII((TQW_BYTE_GAP(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,7)-TQW_BYTE_GAP(I,NTESTCH*CH_CODE+TSTORD,8))/1UA,2,7,1)," "
             IF TSTITEM(1,6)="TQ1_RQ"  THEN WRITE ASCII(CO_CH1(I)/1UA,2,7,1)," "
             IF TSTITEM(1,6)="TQW_RQ"  THEN WRITE ASCII(CO_CH1(I)/1UA,2,7,1)," "
          EXIT
WCODE_SHOW:

       IF CO_HB<>0 THEN ENTRY
          IF FAIL THEN ENTRY
                  GOSUB FCHK_CD(TSTORD,CO_SB)
                  SET CATEGORY CO_SB
                  SET SORT CO_HB
                  SET EXCLUSION :TEXT
          EXIT
       EXIT
    EXIT
;------------------------------------------------------------------------

WCODERD1:
         
GOTO CONT
;===================================================================================================================================================================
; FUSE & RCCM & RUPTURE Subroutine
;===================================================================================================================================================================
FUSE_RCCM_INFO:
    
WRITE /,"== WH LINE/PROD/MASK MIX CHECK =="
    FUSE_TYPE="RCCM"
    SET ILMODE 1WAY
;   SELECT SCRDATA DISABLE
;   SELECT ARIRAM DISABLE

    PINALL=OPEN
    SETTLING TIME=5MS,0.5MS 

    FAVCC2=1.05V & FAVCC1=1.8V & FAVCCQ=1.05V 
    VDD1=FAVCC1 & VDD2H=FAVCC2 & VDD2L=FAVCC2 & VDDQ=FAVCCQ

    RESET  MPAT

    REG MPAT TPH=#FFFF
    TSTORD=1
FUSERCCMRPT_INFO:

    GOSUB VNS01
    GOSUB FMR04       ;EPISSR
    GOSUB TPISSR

    RESET  MPAT
    RESET REG ALL

    REG MPAT XMAX  = #3FFFF
    REG MPAT YMAX  = #FFF

    SRON

    SELECT SCRDATA ENABLE          
    SELECT ARIRAM DISABLE  

    SEND SCRDATA CDCS8FUL

    PMTN=981
    TEST PMTN
    REG  MPAT PC=#00
    REG MPAT XMAX  = #3FFFF
    REG MPAT YMAX  = #FFF
    
    SET RDUT 1

; PROD + LINE 
    WRITE /,"--------------- RCCM  PROD + LINE "

IF LINFLG<>2 THEN ENTRY    ;; LINE P1L
    FAMAPRCCM =#64F011 & IFS=100 & FUSE_RUP="O" & FUSE_DESC="SIG #000                         " & GOSUB RCCMRD(1,6)           
    FAMAPRCCM =#64D011 & IFS=100 & FUSE_RUP="O" & FUSE_DESC="SIG #001                         " & GOSUB RCCMRD(1,6)           
    FAMAPRCCM =#64B011 & IFS=100 & FUSE_RUP="X" & FUSE_DESC="SIG #002                         " & GOSUB RCCMRD(1,6)           
    FAMAPRCCM =#649011 & IFS=100 & FUSE_RUP="O" & FUSE_DESC="SIG #003                         " & GOSUB RCCMRD(1,6)           
    FAMAPRCCM =#647011 & IFS=100 & FUSE_RUP="X" & FUSE_DESC="SIG #004                         " & GOSUB RCCMRD(1,6)           
    FAMAPRCCM =#645011 & IFS=100 & FUSE_RUP="O" & FUSE_DESC="SIG #005                         " & GOSUB RCCMRD(1,6)           
    FAMAPRCCM =#643011 & IFS=100 & FUSE_RUP="X" & FUSE_DESC="SIG #006                         " & GOSUB RCCMRD(1,6)           
    FAMAPRCCM =#641011 & IFS=100 & FUSE_RUP="X" & FUSE_DESC="SIG #007                         " & GOSUB RCCMRD(1,6)           
    FAMAPRCCM =#64F031 & IFS=100 & FUSE_RUP="X" & FUSE_DESC="SIG #008                         " & GOSUB RCCMRD(1,6)           
    FAMAPRCCM =#64D031 & IFS=100 & FUSE_RUP="O" & FUSE_DESC="SIG #009                         " & GOSUB RCCMRD(1,6)           
    FAMAPRCCM =#64B031 & IFS=100 & FUSE_RUP="X" & FUSE_DESC="SIG #010                         " & GOSUB RCCMRD(1,6)           
EXIT

; MASK 
    WRITE /,"--------------- RCCM  MASK        "
    ;                                        ABCDEFGH
    FAMAPRCCM =#64B0F1 & IFS=100 & FUSE_RUP="XXXXXXXX" & FUSE_DESC="MASK 5th                         " & GOSUB RCCMRD(MSKFLG,6) 
    FAMAPRCCM =#6490F1 & IFS=100 & FUSE_RUP="XXXXXXXO" & FUSE_DESC="MASK 4th                         " & GOSUB RCCMRD(MSKFLG,6) 
    FAMAPRCCM =#6470F1 & IFS=100 & FUSE_RUP="XXXOOOOX" & FUSE_DESC="MASK 3rd                         " & GOSUB RCCMRD(MSKFLG,6) 
    FAMAPRCCM =#6450F1 & IFS=100 & FUSE_RUP="XOOXXOOX" & FUSE_DESC="MASK 2nd                         " & GOSUB RCCMRD(MSKFLG,6) 
    FAMAPRCCM =#6430F1 & IFS=100 & FUSE_RUP="OXOXOXOX" & FUSE_DESC="MASK 1st                         " & GOSUB RCCMRD(MSKFLG,6) 

;;  FAMAPRCCM =#C170F1 & IFS=100 & FUSE_RUP="X" & FUSE_DESC="MASK 5th                         " & GOSUB RCCMRD(1,6) 
;;  FAMAPRCCM =#C1B0F1 & IFS=100 & FUSE_RUP="X" & FUSE_DESC="MASK 4th                         " & GOSUB RCCMRD(1,6) 
;;  FAMAPRCCM =#C1F0F1 & IFS=100 & FUSE_RUP="O" & FUSE_DESC="MASK 3rd                         " & GOSUB RCCMRD(1,6) 
;;  FAMAPRCCM =#C131F1 & IFS=100 & FUSE_RUP="X" & FUSE_DESC="MASK 2nd                         " & GOSUB RCCMRD(1,6) 
;;  FAMAPRCCM =#C171F1 & IFS=100 & FUSE_RUP="O" & FUSE_DESC="MASK 1nd                         " & GOSUB RCCMRD(1,6) 

    SROF

 ;  TSTORD=TSTORD+1
 ; IF TSTORD-1<TSTFLG THEN GOTO PKGRPT

    TSTORD=1
    READ TEST TO TN
    GOSUB DUTRESLT 
   ;IF FK=#10 THEN WRITE /,STEP," ",CSN," ","TN=",TN,LP5VD2,LP5TCK,FREQ,"    SIG. READ   "," ",ASCII(AA/1S,1,6,1," "),ASCII(CC/1S,1,6,2," "),"   ", DSPREPA(1,TP)," "
   ;IF FK=#10 THEN WRITE /,STEP," ",CSN," ","TN=",TN,LP5VD2,LP5TCK,FREQ,"FUSE RCCM     " & GOSUB DUTRESLT

    FUSE_TYPE="____"

    GOTO CONT   
;-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
FUSE_RUPTURE:  
    
    FUSE_TYPE="RUP_"
    SET ILMODE 1WAY

    PINALL=OPEN
    SETTLING TIME=5MS,0.5MS 

    FAVCC2=1.05V & FAVCC1=1.8V & FAVCCQ=1.05V 
    VDD1=FAVCC1 & VDD2H=FAVCC2 & VDD2L=FAVCC2 & VDDQ=FAVCCQ
 
    RESET  MPAT

    REG MPAT TPH=#FFFF
    TSTORD=1

FUSERUPRPT:

    GOSUB VNS01
    GOSUB FMR04       ;EPISSR
    GOSUB TPISSR

    RESET  MPAT
    RESET REG ALL

    REG MPAT XMAX  = #3FFFF
    REG MPAT YMAX  = #FFF

    SRON

    SELECT SCRDATA ENABLE          
    SELECT ARIRAM DISABLE  

    SEND SCRDATA CDCS8FUL

    PMTN=980
    TEST PMTN
    REG  MPAT PC=#00
    REG MPAT XMAX  = #3FFFF
    REG MPAT YMAX  = #FFF
    
    SET RDUT 1

;=====     RUPTURE ROUTINE                             ======

    WRITE /,"--------------- PKG RUPTURE       "

;  PKG FUSE for 15.0E @ 200922 --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 
    FAMAPRCCM =#8031B1  & IFS=4710 &  FUSE_RUP="OO" & FUSE_DESC="TMRSF_VGNLA2DRV_ACT_ONLY   " & GOSUB RCCMRD(FUSEINFORM,1)
    FAMAPRCCM =#80F1B1  & IFS=5574 &  FUSE_RUP="OO" & FUSE_DESC="TMRSF_VGNLA2FREQ_UP        " & GOSUB RCCMRD(FUSEINFORM,1)
    FAMAPRCCM =#244171  & IFS=1342 &  FUSE_RUP="OO" & FUSE_DESC="TMRSF_LAPG1_OC_2ND_G0      " & GOSUB RCCMRD(FUSEINFORM,1)

FUSE_RUPTURE_AD:  
    
    FUSE_TYPE="RUP_"
    SET ILMODE 1WAY

    PINALL=OPEN
    SETTLING TIME=5MS,0.5MS 

    FAVCC2=1.05V & FAVCC1=1.8V & FAVCCQ=1.05V 
    VDD1=FAVCC1 & VDD2H=FAVCC2 & VDD2L=FAVCC2 & VDDQ=FAVCCQ
 
    RESET  MPAT

    REG MPAT TPH=#FFFF
    TSTORD=1

FUSERUP_CH:

    GOSUB VNS01
    GOSUB FMR04       ;EPISSR
    GOSUB TPISSR

    DQ1A= IN3 DNRZ BCLK3 CCLK3 IOC DRENRZ OUTL1 STRB1 EXPA1 EXPDLY0 CPEDLY0 VT1 CYP1 <X8,X9>,<X10,X11>,<X4,X5>,<X6,X7>,<X0,X1>,<X2,X3>,<D0,SD0>,<D0,SD0>,<D0,SD0>,<D0,SD0>,<Y8,Y9>,<Y10,Y11>,<Y4,Y5>,<Y6,Y7>,<Y0,Y1>,<Y2,Y3>
    DQ1B= OPEN
    DQ1C= OPEN
    DQ1D= IN3 DNRZ BCLK3 CCLK3 IOC DRENRZ OUTL1 STRB1 EXPA1 EXPDLY0 CPEDLY0 VT1 CYP1 <X8,X9>,<X10,X11>,<X4,X5>,<X6,X7>,<X0,X1>,<X2,X3>,<D0,SD0>,<D0,SD0>,<D0,SD0>,<D0,SD0>,<Y8,Y9>,<Y10,Y11>,<Y4,Y5>,<Y6,Y7>,<Y0,Y1>,<Y2,Y3>

    RESET  MPAT
    RESET REG ALL

    REG MPAT XMAX  = #3FFFF
    REG MPAT YMAX  = #FFF

    SRON

    SELECT SCRDATA ENABLE          
    SELECT ARIRAM DISABLE  

    SEND SCRDATA CDCS8FUL

    PMTN=980
    TEST PMTN
    REG  MPAT PC=#00
    REG MPAT XMAX  = #3FFFF
    REG MPAT YMAX  = #FFF
