    FAMAPRCCM =#C190B1   & IFS=2991 &  FUSE_RUP="OOO" & FUSE_DESC="TMRSF_LSAEN_DIS_P1D_C        " & GOSUB RCCMRD(FUSEINFORM,6); new fuse 200924
    FAMAPRCCM =#0290B0   & IFS=3879 &  FUSE_RUP="OOO" & FUSE_DESC="TMRSF_LSAEN_DIS_P1D_R        " & GOSUB RCCMRD(FUSEINFORM,6); new fuse 200924
    FAMAPRCCM =#C8C1D1   & IFS=799  &  FUSE_RUP="OOO" & FUSE_DESC="TMRSF_LSAEN_P1D_R            " & GOSUB RCCMRD(FUSEINFORM,6); new fuse 200924
    FAMAPRCCM =#C8D1D1   & IFS=831  &  FUSE_RUP="OOO" & FUSE_DESC="TMRSF_LSAEN_P1D_C            " & GOSUB RCCMRD(FUSEINFORM,6); new fuse 200924
    FAMAPRCCM =#C8E1D1   & IFS=863  &  FUSE_RUP="OOO" & FUSE_DESC="TMRSF_LSAEN_P1D_M            " & GOSUB RCCMRD(FUSEINFORM,6); new fuse 200924
    FAMAPRCCM =#09C1D1   & IFS=1648 &  FUSE_RUP="OOO" & FUSE_DESC="TMRSF_LSAEN_P1D_L            " & GOSUB RCCMRD(FUSEINFORM,6); new fuse 200924
    FAMAPRCCM =#01E1D0   & IFS=1680 &  FUSE_RUP="OOO" & FUSE_DESC="TMRSF_LSAEN_P1D_CL           " & GOSUB RCCMRD(FUSEINFORM,6); new fuse 200924
    FAMAPRCCM =#81D1D1   & IFS=2645 &  FUSE_RUP="OOO" & FUSE_DESC="TMRSF_LSAEN_P1D_L            " & GOSUB RCCMRD(FUSEINFORM,6); new fuse 200924
    FAMAPRCCM =#C1D1D1   & IFS=3528 &  FUSE_RUP="OOO" & FUSE_DESC="TMRSF_LSAEN_P1D_C            " & GOSUB RCCMRD(FUSEINFORM,6); new fuse 200924
    FAMAPRCCM =#02D1D0   & IFS=4520 &  FUSE_RUP="OOO" & FUSE_DESC="TMRSF_LSAEN_P1D_R            " & GOSUB RCCMRD(FUSEINFORM,6); new fuse 200924
;---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    FAMAPRCCM =#C800F1   & IFS=16   &  FUSE_RUP="OOO" & FUSE_DESC="TMRSF_PWACSL2_M1_R           " & GOSUB RCCMRD(FUSEINFORM,6); new fuse 201012
    FAMAPRCCM =#C810F1   & IFS=48   &  FUSE_RUP="OOO" & FUSE_DESC="TMRSF_PWACSL2_M1_C           " & GOSUB RCCMRD(FUSEINFORM,6); new fuse 201012
    FAMAPRCCM =#C820F1   & IFS=80   &  FUSE_RUP="OOO" & FUSE_DESC="TMRSF_PWACSL2_M1_M           " & GOSUB RCCMRD(FUSEINFORM,6); new fuse 201012
    FAMAPRCCM =#0900F1   & IFS=912  &  FUSE_RUP="OOO" & FUSE_DESC="TMRSF_PWACSL2_M1_L           " & GOSUB RCCMRD(FUSEINFORM,6); new fuse 201012
    FAMAPRCCM =#0120F0   & IFS=948  &  FUSE_RUP="OOO" & FUSE_DESC="TMRSF_PWACSL2_M1_CL          " & GOSUB RCCMRD(FUSEINFORM,6); new fuse 201012
    FAMAPRCCM =#8110F1   & IFS=1785 &  FUSE_RUP="OOO" & FUSE_DESC="TMRSF_PWACSL2_M1_L           " & GOSUB RCCMRD(FUSEINFORM,6); new fuse 201012
    FAMAPRCCM =#C110F1   & IFS=2769 &  FUSE_RUP="OOO" & FUSE_DESC="TMRSF_PWACSL2_M1_C           " & GOSUB RCCMRD(FUSEINFORM,6); new fuse 201012
    FAMAPRCCM =#0210F0   & IFS=3625 &  FUSE_RUP="OOO" & FUSE_DESC="TMRSF_PWACSL2_M1_R           " & GOSUB RCCMRD(FUSEINFORM,6); new fuse 201012
    FAMAPRCCM =#0AC131   & IFS=4507 &  FUSE_RUP="OOO" & FUSE_DESC="TMRSF_FRPD_DQ_X16_M2_1B      " & GOSUB RCCMRD(FUSEINFORM,6); new fuse 201012
    FAMAPRCCM =#0A30D1   & IFS=3712 &  FUSE_RUP="OOO" & FUSE_DESC="TMRSF_RDREP_ON_P1_R          " & GOSUB RCCMRD(FUSEINFORM,6); new fuse 201012

;----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    FAMAPRCCM =#C9A110  & IFS=3458 &  FUSE_RUP="9X9" & FUSE_DESC="TMRSF_WAFER_BIZ              " & GOSUB RCCMRD(FUSEINFORM,6)  ; ch A,D only
;----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    SROF

    TSTORD=1
    READ TEST TO TN
    GOSUB DUTRESLT 
   ;IF FK=#10 THEN WRITE /,STEP," ",CSN," ","TN=",TN,LP5VD2,LP5TCK,FREQ,"    SIG. READ   "," ",ASCII(AA/1S,1,6,1," "),ASCII(CC/1S,1,6,2," "),"   ", DSPREPA(1,TP)," "
   ;IF FK=#10 THEN WRITE /,STEP," ",CSN," ","TN=",TN,LP5VD2,LP5TCK,FREQ,"FUSE RCCM     " & GOSUB DUTRESLT
    FUSE_TYPE="____"
GOTO CONT   

;-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
CHIPLOG:
 DO D_LOGA I=1,TP
    IF PMSRTC(I)<>0 THEN ENTRY
       WRITE / "DUT=",ASCII(I,0,3,10,"0")," ","HB=",ASCII(PMSRTC(I),1,1,10," ")," ","NB="
       DO D_LOGB J=1 MCNUM
          WRITE " ",ASCII(NG256(J,I),1,5,10," ")
       D_LOGB:
    EXIT
 D_LOGA:
 WRITE /
GOTO CONT
;-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
RCCMRD:
 ARGUMENT(FUSE_INFO,BIN_INFO)
    F_INFO=FUSE_INFO
    RCCMBIN=BIN_INFO
    REG  MPAT PC=#00

    STRING FUSE_PATN(10)="          "
    IF FUSE_TYPE="RUP_" THEN FUSE_PATN(1,10)="PDCSPRU10B"
    IF FUSE_TYPE="RCCM" THEN FUSE_PATN(1,10)="PDCSPRC10B"

    IF FUSE_TYPE<>"RUP_" AND FUSE_TYPE<>"RCCM" AND FUSE_TYPE<>"RCMA" THEN SET ILMODE 8WAY   ; for rte
    IF F_INFO=0                                    THEN GOTO CONT
    IF FUSE_TYPE="RUP_" AND FUSE_RUP(F_INFO,1)="X" THEN GOTO CONT

    SEND MPAT <FUSE_PATN>

    REG MPAT TPH = SR0((FAMAPRCCM.AND.#100000),9).OR.SR0((FAMAPRCCM.AND.#400000),12).OR.SR0((FAMAPRCCM.AND.#010000),7).OR.SR0((FAMAPRCCM.AND.#040000),10).OR.SR0((FAMAPRCCM.AND.#001000),5).OR.SR0((FAMAPRCCM.AND.#004000),8).OR.SR0((FAMAPRCCM.AND.#000100),3).OR.SR0((FAMAPRCCM.AND.#000400),6).OR.SR0((FAMAPRCCM.AND.#000010),1).OR.SR0((FAMAPRCCM.AND.#000040),4).OR.SL0((FAMAPRCCM.AND.#000001),1).OR.SR0((FAMAPRCCM.AND.#0000004),2) ; EVEN
    REG MPAT TPH2= SR0((FAMAPRCCM.AND.#200000),10).OR.SR0((FAMAPRCCM.AND.#800000),13).OR.SR0((FAMAPRCCM.AND.#020000),8).OR.SR0((FAMAPRCCM.AND.#080000),11).OR.SR0((FAMAPRCCM.AND.#002000),6).OR.SR0((FAMAPRCCM.AND.#008000),9).OR.SR0((FAMAPRCCM.AND.#000200),4).OR.SR0((FAMAPRCCM.AND.#000800),7).OR.SR0((FAMAPRCCM.AND.#000020),2).OR.SR0((FAMAPRCCM.AND.#000080),5).OR.(FAMAPRCCM.AND.#000002).OR.SR0((FAMAPRCCM.AND.#0000008),3)       ; ODD

    REG MPAT D1  = SR0((FAMAPRCCM.AND.#FFF000),12)
    REG MPAT D2  = FAMAPRCCM.AND.#0000FFF

    IF FUSE_RUP(F_INFO,1)="O" THEN ENTRY & REG MPAT D5=#FFFF & REG MPAT D6=#FFFF & EXIT
    IF FUSE_RUP(F_INFO,1)="X" THEN ENTRY & REG MPAT D5=#0000 & REG MPAT D6=#0000 & EXIT
    IF FUSE_RUP(F_INFO,1)="9" THEN ENTRY & REG MPAT D5=#9999 & REG MPAT D6=#9999 & EXIT

    WAIT TIME 1MS
    
    MEAS MPAT(3)

    READ FUNC1(PMAPIO) TO FID1 
;   READ FUNC1(PMAPIOX8) TO FID1 
    
    GOSUB DUTRESLT
    
    IF FK=#10 THEN ENTRY
       WRITE /,STEP," ",CSN," ","TN=",ASCII(PMTN,2,5,0," "),ASCII(FAVCC1/1V,2,6,3," "),"V",ASCII(FAVCC2/1V,2,6,3," "),"V" 
       WRITE  ," ",FUSE_TYPE,"  #",ASCII(FAMAPRCCM,0,6,16,"0")," ",ASCII(IFS,2,5,0," ")," ",FUSE_DESC(1,28)," ",FUSE_RUP(F_INFO,1)," ",ASCII(AA/1S,1,6,1," "),ASCII(CC/1S,1,6,2," "),"   ",DSPREPA(1,TP)
       WRITE ,"_(",DSPREPA(1*TP+1,TP),")(",DSPREPA(2*TP+1,TP),")(",DSPREPA(3*TP+1,TP),")(",DSPREPA(4*TP+1,TP),")"
    EXIT

    IF FUSE_TYPE="RCCM" THEN ENTRY
       GOSUB FCHK
       GOSUB NRNCHK(IFS,980,6)
       GOSUB FBIN(RCCMBIN,131)    ;;NORMAL REJECTION
    EXIT

    IF FUSE_TYPE="RCMA" THEN ENTRY
       GOSUB FCHK
       GOSUB NRNCHK(982,980,6)
       GOSUB FBIN(6,132)    ;;NORMAL REJECTION
    EXIT

   GOTO CONT

FUSE_RCCM_ALL:
    
    FUSE_TYPE="RCMA"   ; RCCM ALL
    SET ILMODE 1WAY
;   SELECT SCRDATA DISABLE
;   SELECT ARIRAM DISABLE

    PINALL=OPEN
    SETTLING TIME=5MS,0.5MS 

    FAVCC2=1.05V & FAVCC1=1.8V & FAVCCQ=1.05V 
    VDD1=FAVCC1 & VDD2H=FAVCC2 & VDD2L=FAVCC2 & VDDQ=FAVCCQ
 
    RESET  MPAT

    REG MPAT TPH=#FFFF
    TSTORD=1

    GOSUB VNS01
    GOSUB FMR04       ;EPISSR
    GOSUB TPISSR

    RESET  MPAT
    RESET REG ALL

    REG MPAT XMAX  = #3FFFF
    REG MPAT YMAX  = #FFF

    SRON

    SELECT SCRDATA ENABLE          
    SELECT ARIRAM DISABLE  

    SEND SCRDATA CDCS8FUL

    PMTN=982
    TEST PMTN
    REG  MPAT PC=#00
    REG MPAT XMAX  = #3FFFF
    REG MPAT YMAX  = #FFF
    
    SET RDUT 1

    SEND MPAT PDCSPRCATA & FUSE_DESC="FUSE CHK ALL #1                  " & GOSUB RCCMRD(1)  
    SEND MPAT PDCSPRCATB & FUSE_DESC="FUSE CHK ALL #2                  " & GOSUB RCCMRD(1)  
 
    SROF

 ;  TSTORD=TSTORD+1
 ; IF TSTORD-1<TSTFLG THEN GOTO PKGRPT

    TSTORD=1
    READ TEST TO TN
    GOSUB DUTRESLT 
   ;IF FK=#10 THEN WRITE /,STEP," ",CSN," ","TN=",TN,LP5VD2,LP5TCK,FREQ,"    SIG. READ   "," ",ASCII(AA/1S,1,6,1," "),ASCII(CC/1S,1,6,2," "),"   ", DSPREPA(1,TP)," "
   ;IF FK=#10 THEN WRITE /,STEP," ",CSN," ","TN=",TN,LP5VD2,LP5TCK,FREQ,"FUSE RCCM     " & GOSUB DUTRESLT

 GOTO CONT   

;-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
CDC_CHK:

    SET ILMODE 1WAY

    PINALL=OPEN
    SETTLING TIME=5MS,0.5MS

    FAVCC2=1.05V & FAVCC1=1.8V & FAVCCQ=0.50V
    VDD1=FAVCC1 & VDD2H=FAVCC2 & VDD2L=FAVCC2 & VDDQ=FAVCCQ

    RESET REG ALL

;   REG MPAT TPH=#FFFF

;   GOSUB VNCDT
    GOSUB VNTPD   ; JJH
    GOSUB TCHIPP

    SELECT SCRDATA ENABLE
    SELECT ARIRAM DISABLE

    SEND SCRDATA CDCS8FUL
    REG  MPAT PC=#00
    REG MPAT XMAX  = #3FFFF
    REG MPAT YMAX  = #FFF

;   SRON

DO CDC_LOOP CHSEL=0 TSTFLG-1

    GOSUB FMS07

    TSTORD=1

    SET RDUT 1

    PMTN=801 & SEND MPAT PDCSPCDT01 & FUSE_DESC="CDC_M4_AREA1            " & REG MPAT PC=#000 & GOSUB CDC_RD
    PMTN=803 & SEND MPAT PDCSPCDT01 & FUSE_DESC="CDC_M4_AREA2            " & REG MPAT PC=#400 & GOSUB CDC_RD
    PMTN=802 & SEND MPAT PDCSPCDT02 & FUSE_DESC="CDC_M4_AREA3            " & REG MPAT PC=#000 & GOSUB CDC_RD
    PMTN=805 & SEND MPAT PDCSPCDT02 & FUSE_DESC="CDC_M4_AREA4            " & REG MPAT PC=#400 & GOSUB CDC_RD
    PMTN=804 & SEND MPAT PDCSPCDT03 & FUSE_DESC="CDC_M4_AREA5            " & REG MPAT PC=#000 & GOSUB CDC_RD
    PMTN=806 & SEND MPAT PDCSPCDT04 & FUSE_DESC="CDC_GP_M3_AREA1         " & REG MPAT PC=#000 & GOSUB CDC_RD
    PMTN=808 & SEND MPAT PDCSPCDT04 & FUSE_DESC="CDC_GP_M3_AREA2         " & REG MPAT PC=#400 & GOSUB CDC_RD
    PMTN=807 & SEND MPAT PDCSPCDT05 & FUSE_DESC="CDC_GP_M3_AREA3         " & REG MPAT PC=#000 & GOSUB CDC_RD
    PMTN=810 & SEND MPAT PDCSPCDT05 & FUSE_DESC="CDC_GP_M3_AREA4         " & REG MPAT PC=#400 & GOSUB CDC_RD
    PMTN=809 & SEND MPAT PDCSPCDT06 & FUSE_DESC="CDC_GP_M3_AR            " & REG MPAT PC=#000 & GOSUB CDC_RD

CDC_LOOP:
    SROF
    CHSEL=0

    GOTO CONT

CDC_RD:

    TEST PMTN
    READ TEST TO TN

    WAIT TIME 1MS

    MEAS MPAT(3)

;   READ FUNC1(DQ1) TO FID1 & READ FUNC1(DQ1) TO FID2 & EXIT     ;; FID1= (MSB) DQ0,DQ1 (LSB)
;   READ FUNC1(PMAPIO) TO FID1

    GOSUB DUTRESLT
   ;IF FK=#10 THEN  WRITE /,STEP," ",CSN," ","TN=",ASCII(PMTN,2,5,0," ")," ",FUSE_DESC,"                          ",ASCII(AA/1S,1,6,1," "),ASCII(CC/1S,1,6,2," "),,"       ",DSPREPA(1,TP)," "
    IF FK=#10 THEN  ENTRY
       WRITE /,STEP," ",CSN," ","TN=",ASCII(TN,2,5,0," "),ASCII(FAVCC1/1V,2,6,3," "),"V",ASCII(FAVCC2/1V,2,6,3," "),"V",ASCII(FAVCCQ/1V,2,6,3," "),"V"," ",ASCII(40NS/1NS,2,6,2," "),"NS"
       WRITE  ," ","----"," ","FMS07"," ",FUSE_DESC(1,23)," ",ASCII(AA/1S,1,6,1," "),ASCII(CC/1S,1,6,2," "),"   ",DSPREPA(1,TP)
    EXIT

    GOSUB FCHK
    GOSUB NRNCHK(862,199,8)
    GOSUB FBIN(6,131)    ;;NORMAL REJECTION

    RESET  MPAT

GOTO CONT

GETTRRD:
   DO GETRDR1D II=1 TP 1
       RTNUM=II-32*((II-1)/32)-1
       IF SR(CURDUT,RTNUM).AND.#01<>#0 THEN ENTRY
         IF FK=#10 THEN ENTRY
         DO GETRDR2D IJ=1 NTESTCH 1
           IF ORGNUM=16 THEN ENTRY     
              WRITE /,"WCK DUT:",ASCII(II,2,1,0," ")," CH:",ASCII(IJ+NTESTCH*CHSEL,2,1,0," ")," ",ASCII(FIDP2(IJ+NTESTCH*CHSEL,II),0,8,16,"0"),ASCII(FIDP1(IJ+NTESTCH*CHSEL,II),0,8,16,"0")," RD : "
              ;DO GETRDR3 IK=1 22 1
              DO GETRDR3D IK=1 22 1
                 WRITE ASCII(GETRDTR9((II-1)*88+(IJ-1)*22+IK),2,7,2," ")
              GETRDR3D:
            EXIT
         GETRDR2D:
         EXIT
       EXIT
GETRDR1D:

GOTO CONT

GETTRWR:
   DO GETWRR1D II=1 TP 1
       RTNUM=II-32*((II-1)/32)-1
       IF SR(CURDUT,RTNUM).AND.#01<>#0 THEN ENTRY
         IF FK=#10 THEN ENTRY
         DO GETWRR2D IJ=1 NTESTCH 1
           IF ORGNUM=16 THEN ENTRY     
              WRITE /,"WCK DUT:",ASCII(II,2,1,0," ")," CH:",ASCII(IJ+NTESTCH*CHSEL,2,1,0," ")," ",ASCII(FIDP2(IJ+NTESTCH*CHSEL,II),0,8,16,"0"),ASCII(FIDP1(IJ+NTESTCH*CHSEL,II),0,8,16,"0")," WR : "
              ;DO GETWRR3 IK=1 22 1
              DO GETWRR3D IK=1 22 1
                 WRITE ASCII(GETWRTR9((II-1)*88+(IJ-1)*22+IK),2,7,2," ")
              GETWRR3D:
            EXIT
         GETWRR2D:
         EXIT
       EXIT
GETWRR1D:

GOTO CONT


M26OUTA:


 DCMCNT=1
DO M26CAA XORTCC= 36PS -36PS -3PS
   TIMING SET=1
   ;            1      2      3     4                  5              6             7           
              TIMING SET=1
           ;            1            2      3     4                  5                6             7           
;          BCLK8  =  WCKR          WCKR2   WCKR   WCKR+TRATE*0.1    WCKR-TRATE*0.1    WCKR   WCKR   WCKR2        ;WCK
           CCLK8  =  WCKF+XORTCC   WCKF2   WCKF   WCKF+TRATE*0.1    WCKF-TRATE*0.1    WCKF   WCKF   WCKF2        ;WCK


    MEAS MPAT(3)
    READ FUNC1(DQDCMA) TO PFDATA0 
;   WRITE /,XORTCC,PFDATA0(2)," ",PFDATA0(4)
    WAIT TIME 2MS
     
    DO DCMSCAN0A I=1,TP,1
      RTNUM=I-32*((I-1)/32)-1
      IF SR(CURDUT,RTNUM).AND.#01 <> #0 THEN ENTRY
;;;;;;   IF PFDATA0(I).AND.#80000000 <> #0 AND PFDATA0(I).AND.#40000000 <> #0 AND DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+1,DCACNT)=0    THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+1,DCACNT)=DCMCNT
;;;;;;   IF PFDATA0(I).AND.#20000000 <> #0 AND PFDATA0(I).AND.#10000000 <> #0 AND DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+2,DCACNT)=0    THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+2,DCACNT)=DCMCNT
;;;;;;   IF PFDATA0(I).AND.#08000000 <> #0 AND PFDATA0(I).AND.#04000000 <> #0 AND DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+3,DCACNT)=0    THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+3,DCACNT)=DCMCNT
;;;;;;   IF PFDATA0(I).AND.#02000000 <> #0 AND PFDATA0(I).AND.#01000000 <> #0 AND DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+4,DCACNT)=0    THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+4,DCACNT)=DCMCNT
;;;;;;   IF PFDATA0(I).AND.#00800000 <> #0 AND PFDATA0(I).AND.#00400000 <> #0 AND DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+5,DCACNT)=0    THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+5,DCACNT)=DCMCNT
;;;;;;   IF PFDATA0(I).AND.#00200000 <> #0 AND PFDATA0(I).AND.#00100000 <> #0 AND DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+6,DCACNT)=0    THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+6,DCACNT)=DCMCNT
;;;;;;   IF PFDATA0(I).AND.#00080000 <> #0 AND PFDATA0(I).AND.#00040000 <> #0 AND DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+7,DCACNT)=0    THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+7,DCACNT)=DCMCNT
;;;;;;   IF PFDATA0(I).AND.#00020000 <> #0 AND PFDATA0(I).AND.#00010000 <> #0 AND DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+8,DCACNT)=0    THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+8,DCACNT)=DCMCNT

         IF PFDATA0(I).AND.#80000000 <> #0                                    AND   DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+1,DCACNT)=0                                                                     THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+1,DCACNT)=100
         IF PFDATA0(I).AND.#20000000 <> #0                                    AND   DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+2,DCACNT)=0                                                                     THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+2,DCACNT)=100
         IF PFDATA0(I).AND.#08000000 <> #0                                    AND   DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+3,DCACNT)=0                                                                     THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+3,DCACNT)=100
         IF PFDATA0(I).AND.#02000000 <> #0                                    AND   DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+4,DCACNT)=0                                                                     THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+4,DCACNT)=100
         IF PFDATA0(I).AND.#00800000 <> #0                                    AND   DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+5,DCACNT)=0                                                                     THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+5,DCACNT)=100
         IF PFDATA0(I).AND.#00200000 <> #0                                    AND   DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+6,DCACNT)=0                                                                     THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+6,DCACNT)=100
         IF PFDATA0(I).AND.#00080000 <> #0                                    AND   DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+7,DCACNT)=0                                                                     THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+7,DCACNT)=100
         IF PFDATA0(I).AND.#00020000 <> #0                                    AND   DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+8,DCACNT)=0                                                                     THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+8,DCACNT)=100
         IF                                    PFDATA0(I).AND.#40000000 <> #0 AND   DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+1,DCACNT+20)=0                                                                  THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+1,DCACNT+20)=100
         IF                                    PFDATA0(I).AND.#10000000 <> #0 AND   DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+2,DCACNT+20)=0                                                                  THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+2,DCACNT+20)=100
         IF                                    PFDATA0(I).AND.#04000000 <> #0 AND   DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+3,DCACNT+20)=0                                                                  THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+3,DCACNT+20)=100
         IF                                    PFDATA0(I).AND.#01000000 <> #0 AND   DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+4,DCACNT+20)=0                                                                  THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+4,DCACNT+20)=100
         IF                                    PFDATA0(I).AND.#00400000 <> #0 AND   DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+5,DCACNT+20)=0                                                                  THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+5,DCACNT+20)=100
         IF                                    PFDATA0(I).AND.#00100000 <> #0 AND   DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+6,DCACNT+20)=0                                                                  THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+6,DCACNT+20)=100
         IF                                    PFDATA0(I).AND.#00040000 <> #0 AND   DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+7,DCACNT+20)=0                                                                  THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+7,DCACNT+20)=100
         IF                                    PFDATA0(I).AND.#00010000 <> #0 AND   DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+8,DCACNT+20)=0                                                                  THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+8,DCACNT+20)=100

         IF PFDATA0(I).AND.#80000000 <> #0                                    AND   DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+1,DCACNT)<>0    AND DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+1,DCACNT)   >(DCMCNT-3)     THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+1,DCACNT)=100
         IF PFDATA0(I).AND.#20000000 <> #0                                    AND   DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+2,DCACNT)<>0    AND DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+2,DCACNT)   >(DCMCNT-3)     THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+2,DCACNT)=100
         IF PFDATA0(I).AND.#08000000 <> #0                                    AND   DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+3,DCACNT)<>0    AND DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+3,DCACNT)   >(DCMCNT-3)     THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+3,DCACNT)=100
         IF PFDATA0(I).AND.#02000000 <> #0                                    AND   DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+4,DCACNT)<>0    AND DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+4,DCACNT)   >(DCMCNT-3)     THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+4,DCACNT)=100
         IF PFDATA0(I).AND.#00800000 <> #0                                    AND   DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+5,DCACNT)<>0    AND DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+5,DCACNT)   >(DCMCNT-3)     THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+5,DCACNT)=100
         IF PFDATA0(I).AND.#00200000 <> #0                                    AND   DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+6,DCACNT)<>0    AND DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+6,DCACNT)   >(DCMCNT-3)     THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+6,DCACNT)=100
         IF PFDATA0(I).AND.#00080000 <> #0                                    AND   DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+7,DCACNT)<>0    AND DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+7,DCACNT)   >(DCMCNT-3)     THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+7,DCACNT)=100
         IF PFDATA0(I).AND.#00020000 <> #0                                    AND   DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+8,DCACNT)<>0    AND DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+8,DCACNT)   >(DCMCNT-3)     THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+8,DCACNT)=100
         IF                                    PFDATA0(I).AND.#40000000 <> #0 AND   DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+1,DCACNT+20)<>0 AND DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+1,DCACNT+20)>(DCMCNT-3)     THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+1,DCACNT+20)=100
         IF                                    PFDATA0(I).AND.#10000000 <> #0 AND   DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+2,DCACNT+20)<>0 AND DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+2,DCACNT+20)>(DCMCNT-3)     THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+2,DCACNT+20)=100
         IF                                    PFDATA0(I).AND.#04000000 <> #0 AND   DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+3,DCACNT+20)<>0 AND DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+3,DCACNT+20)>(DCMCNT-3)     THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+3,DCACNT+20)=100
         IF                                    PFDATA0(I).AND.#01000000 <> #0 AND   DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+4,DCACNT+20)<>0 AND DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+4,DCACNT+20)>(DCMCNT-3)     THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+4,DCACNT+20)=100
         IF                                    PFDATA0(I).AND.#00400000 <> #0 AND   DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+5,DCACNT+20)<>0 AND DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+5,DCACNT+20)>(DCMCNT-3)     THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+5,DCACNT+20)=100
         IF                                    PFDATA0(I).AND.#00100000 <> #0 AND   DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+6,DCACNT+20)<>0 AND DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+6,DCACNT+20)>(DCMCNT-3)     THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+6,DCACNT+20)=100
         IF                                    PFDATA0(I).AND.#00040000 <> #0 AND   DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+7,DCACNT+20)<>0 AND DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+7,DCACNT+20)>(DCMCNT-3)     THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+7,DCACNT+20)=100
         IF                                    PFDATA0(I).AND.#00010000 <> #0 AND   DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+8,DCACNT+20)<>0 AND DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+8,DCACNT+20)>(DCMCNT-3)     THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+8,DCACNT+20)=100
                                                                              
                                                                              
                                                                                                                                  
         IF PFDATA0(I).AND.#80000000 = #0                                     AND DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+1,DCACNT)=100     THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+1,DCACNT)=DCMCNT
         IF PFDATA0(I).AND.#20000000 = #0                                     AND DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+2,DCACNT)=100     THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+2,DCACNT)=DCMCNT
         IF PFDATA0(I).AND.#08000000 = #0                                     AND DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+3,DCACNT)=100     THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+3,DCACNT)=DCMCNT
         IF PFDATA0(I).AND.#02000000 = #0                                     AND DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+4,DCACNT)=100     THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+4,DCACNT)=DCMCNT
         IF PFDATA0(I).AND.#00800000 = #0                                     AND DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+5,DCACNT)=100     THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+5,DCACNT)=DCMCNT
         IF PFDATA0(I).AND.#00200000 = #0                                     AND DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+6,DCACNT)=100     THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+6,DCACNT)=DCMCNT

         IF PFDATA0(I).AND.#00020000 = #0                                     AND DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+8,DCACNT)=100     THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+8,DCACNT)=DCMCNT
                                                                              
         IF                                    PFDATA0(I).AND.#40000000 = #0  AND DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+1,DCACNT+20)=100  THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+1,DCACNT+20)=DCMCNT
         IF                                    PFDATA0(I).AND.#10000000 = #0  AND DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+2,DCACNT+20)=100  THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+2,DCACNT+20)=DCMCNT

         IF                                    PFDATA0(I).AND.#00400000 = #0  AND DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+5,DCACNT+20)=100  THEN DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+5,DCACNT+20)=DCMCNT

DCMA_CHECK:



    DO DCMSCAN00 I=1,TP,1
    DO DCMSCAN02 K=1,NTESTCH*(ORGNUM/8),1
    DO DCMSCAN04 DCACNT=1,15,1
    
       DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+K,DCACNT)=0
       DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+K,DCACNT+20)=0

DCMSCAN04:
DCMSCAN02:  
DCMSCAN00:  


 REG MPAT D1_2=#77 & DCACNT=1  & GOSUB M26OUTA
 REG MPAT D1_2=#66 & DCACNT=2  & GOSUB M26OUTA
;REG MPAT D1_2=#55 & DCACNT=3  & GOSUB M26OUTA
 REG MPAT D1_2=#44 & DCACNT=4  & GOSUB M26OUTA
;REG MPAT D1_2=#33 & DCACNT=5  & GOSUB M26OUTA
;REG MPAT D1_2=#22 & DCACNT=6  & GOSUB M26OUTA
;REG MPAT D1_2=#11 & DCACNT=7  & GOSUB M26OUTA
 REG MPAT D1_2=#00 & DCACNT=8  & GOSUB M26OUTA
;REG MPAT D1_2=#99 & DCACNT=9  & GOSUB M26OUTA
;REG MPAT D1_2=#AA & DCACNT=10 & GOSUB M26OUTA
;REG MPAT D1_2=#BB & DCACNT=11 & GOSUB M26OUTA
 REG MPAT D1_2=#CC & DCACNT=12 & GOSUB M26OUTA
;REG MPAT D1_2=#DD & DCACNT=13 & GOSUB M26OUTA
 REG MPAT D1_2=#EE & DCACNT=14 & GOSUB M26OUTA
 REG MPAT D1_2=#FF & DCACNT=15 & GOSUB M26OUTA

    DO DCMSCAN10 I=1,TP,1
    DO DCMSCAN11 K=1,NTESTCH*(ORGNUM/8),1
      RTNUM=I-32*((I-1)/32)-1
      IF SR(CURDUT,RTNUM).AND.#01 <> #0 THEN ENTRY
 
       WRITE /," TRANSITION POINT =",I,K
     DO DCMSCAN12 J=1,35,1
           WRITE " ",ASCII(DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+K,J)*1,2,3,1," ")
 DCMSCAN12:  
;;;   WRITE " ",ASCII((DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+K,15)-DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+K,1))*1,2,5,1," ")
;;;   WRITE " ",ASCII((DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+K,14)-DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+K,2))*1,2,5,1," ")
;;;   WRITE " ",ASCII((DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+K,15)-DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+K,2))*1,2,5,1," ")
;;;   WRITE " ",ASCII((DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+K,14)-DCMA_CHECK_PT(I,NTESTCH*CHSEL*2+K,1))*1,2,5,1," ")

EXIT
DCMSCAN11:  
DCMSCAN10:  

GOTO CONT

IBIS_PRINT:
 IF TSTITEM(1,3)="OCD" OR TSTITEM(1,6)="OC_RCD" OR TSTITEM(1,6)="NT_ODT"  OR TSTITEM(1,3)="VRO" THEN ENTRY
    DO OCDV1 TD1=2,4,2
    DO OCDV2 IJ=1,NTESTCH,1
       WRITE /,TSTITEM," : ","DUT ",ASCII(TD1,2,1,0," "),
       WRITE " CH ",ASCII(IJ+NTESTCH*CHSEL,2,1,0," ")," ",
       WRITE ASCII(FIDP2(IJ+NTESTCH*CHSEL,TD1),0,8,16,"0"),ASCII(FIDP1(IJ+NTESTCH*CHSEL,TD1),0,8,16,"0")," ",RRVAL," : "
       
        IF TSTITEM(1,7)="OCD_TQW" THEN WRITE "#",ASCII(MR_RCAL_BL,0,2,16,"0")," ",TWCLK,"#",ASCII(MR30_DCA,0,2,16,"0")," "
       
    DO OCDV3 NDQ=1,26,1
       IF TSTITEM(1,6)="OCD_PD"  AND NDQ<19 THEN WRITE ASCII(OCD_VALUE0(TD1,NTESTCH*CHSEL+IJ,NDQ)/1UA,2,8,1," ")," "
       IF TSTITEM(1,6)="OCDZPD"  AND NDQ<19 THEN WRITE ASCII(OCD_VALUE1(TD1,NTESTCH*CHSEL+IJ,NDQ)/1UA,2,8,1," ")," "
       IF TSTITEM(1,6)="OCD_PU"  AND NDQ<19 THEN WRITE ASCII(OCD_VALUE2(TD1,NTESTCH*CHSEL+IJ,NDQ)/1UA,2,8,1," ")," "
       IF TSTITEM(1,6)="NT_ODT"             THEN WRITE ASCII(NDT_VALUE0(TD1,NTESTCH*CHSEL+IJ,NDQ)/1UA,2,8,1," ")," "
       IF TSTITEM(1,7)="OCD_TQW" AND NDQ<23 THEN WRITE ASCII(TQW_VALUE0(TD1,NTESTCH*CHSEL+IJ,NDQ)/1UA,2,8,1," ")," "
       IF TSTITEM(1,7)="OCD_OPO" AND NDQ<23 THEN WRITE ASCII(TQW_VALUE0(TD1,NTESTCH*CHSEL+IJ,NDQ)/1UA,2,8,1," ")," "
       IF TSTITEM(1,4)="VRO1"    AND NDQ<5  THEN WRITE ASCII(VRO_VALUE0(TD1,NTESTCH*CHSEL+IJ,NDQ)/1MV,2,8,1," ")," "
       IF TSTITEM(1,4)="VRO2"    AND NDQ<5  THEN WRITE ASCII(VRO_VALUE1(TD1,NTESTCH*CHSEL+IJ,NDQ)/1MV,2,8,1," ")," "
       IF TSTITEM(1,6)="OC_RCD"  AND NDQ<9  THEN WRITE ASCII(OCR_VALUE0(TD1,NTESTCH*CHSEL+IJ,NDQ)/1UA,2,8,1," ")," "
OCDV3:
OCDV2:
OCDV1:
 
 EXIT

GOTO CONT
